Chapter 401: Shady Establishment

The carriage ambled along the official road, whose surface was pitted and worn from years of neglect. Yet, the old horse traversed the uneven path as if it was on level ground, leaving the two passengers inside completely undisturbed by any jolts.

“Ah, we’ve reached Wilderness Province?” Lu Yang unfolded a map with a glowing dot that marked their position. This was a magical artifact essential for travel.

“It’s getting late. Let’s find somewhere nearby to rest.” Noticing that the sky was getting dark and they had arrived in Wilderness Province, Meng Jingzhou felt there was no need to rush.

“Eh, look! There’s an inn! We could stay there!” Meng Jingzhou pointed to an inn ahead.

Its signboard hung precariously, and the name was barely visible. The condition of the inn could be described as...concerning.

Lu Yang eyed the inn skeptically. It was gloomy and eerie, looking like a squall could topple it.

“Let’s make do. Better than sleeping in the carriage,” Lu Yang consoled himself.

Approaching the entrance, they saw that the doors were wide open. The interior was swallowed in darkness, and there was not a single soul in sight, as if the place had been abandoned for ages.

The two also finally deciphered the fading sign: Qingming Inn[1]

“This name doesn’t sound too auspicious. Is this place still operating, or has it shut down?” Meng Jingzhou muttered before striding inside and shouting, “Is anyone here? We’d like to stay for the night!”

No response.

Meng Jingzhou yelled again, “Is anyone here? We’d like to stay for the night!”

Thud!

It sounded like a heavy corpse had hit the floor behind the counter.

“Who’s shouting? Don’t you know the rules?!” A man in a white paper hat darted out from the counter, glaring at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“We’d like to stay here. Give me two of your best rooms!” Meng Jingzhou always stayed at the best places.

“You two? Stay here?” The man stared at them in surprise. He then peered behind them, but saw no one else was with them.

“Off with you! Don’t cause trouble here. This is not a place for you. Go find somewhere else to stay.” The man impatiently shooed them away.

Meng Jingzhou was baffled. He had stayed in many inns, but this was his first time encountering one that refused him. “Is your inn full?”

“Half the rooms are empty.”

“Then why turn us away?”

Seeing that the two really didn’t know the rules, the man was about to explain when noises suddenly came from upstairs.

Thud. Thud. Thud. The synchronized footsteps echoed unnervingly from above.

A cultivator in Daoist robes descended from the second floor, followed by a group of people wrapped in black cloth who kept silent, appearing especially frightening in the darkness.

The sheer number of figures shrouded in black cloth made Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou doubt the inn’s capacity, especially with half the rooms supposedly vacant.

Could a dozen people be crammed into one room? But how do they sleep? Do they stand against the walls?

"Lad, I'm checking out. This is the worst Qingming Inn I've ever stayed at." The Daoist-robed cultivator tossed a string of copper coins to the man in the white paper hat. The coins bore an unfamiliar design, and faint ripples of magical energy lingered on their surfaces, seemingly carrying some special properties.

The hatted man chuckled wordlessly. As long as there’s money to earn.

Lu Yang was bemused. It’s already dark. Why are they leaving now?

When Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou saw the appearances of the shrouded figures, both froze in shock.

These black-clothed figures had vacant and lifeless eyes. Some had their mouths and nostrils stuffed with mud and grass, others were disfigured, as if their faces had been crushed by something, while some decrepit ones were emaciated to the point of having a mere layer of skin draped over their bones.

“Died from drowning, crushed to death, died of old age... These are all corpses!”

“Corpse-Driving Technique?!”

No wonder they are checking out at night, resting during the day, and driving corpses at night—this is what the books describe.

The two didn’t expect to encounter the legendary Corpse-Driving Technique so soon after entering Wilderness Province.

The white paper-hatted man pocketed the coins and shot them a sidelong glance. “This is a corpse inn that provides lodging for Corpse Drivers. The rooms are meant for the dead. If you don’t mind, you’re welcome to stay here.”

The two’s eyelids twitched at the thought of staying in rooms meant for corpses, finding it more or less unsettling.

“Was the man who performed the Corpse-Driving Technique from the Corpse-Driving Sect?” Lu Yang asked. If he is from the Corpse-Driving Sect, this would be a great opportunity to have a chat with him.

The hatted man shook his head. “You two must be outsiders. I knew it! Our Qingming Inn is a chain establishment in Wilderness Province. How could any living person know our name, much less come looking for lodging?”

“We’re from Yun Province.”

Realization dawned upon the white paper-hatted man. “Ah, from the great provinces of the Central Plains! No wonder! I’ve heard that the Dao-Seeking Sect, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, and the whole of Yun Province are powerful and prosperous. The transportation is convenient, the economy is developed, and strong cultivators are everywhere.”

He corrected the two’s misconceptions. “Corpse-Driving Techniques are not exclusive to the Corpse-Driving Sect. Many rogue cultivators among the common folks know them too, though they’re far less formal about it than the Corpse-Driving Sect.

“In our Wilderness Province, both corpse-driving rogue cultivators and disciples of the Corpse-Driving Sects are collectively called Corpse Drivers. They don’t use spirit stones for transactions, but rather Great Copper Spell Coins.” The man shook the string of copper coins in his hand. “These right here.”

The two thanked the white paper-hatted man and decided to search for another inn.

After leaving Qingming Inn, Lu Yang noticed a fallen sign at the entrance. Out of kindness, he stood it back up.

The sign read: Due to adjustments in business strategy, this establishment has relocated 20 li east of Baiquan Town. We seek your understanding and apologize for any inconvenience.[2]

The date at the bottom was from five years ago.

“What?!”

The two looked up in shock at the Qingming Inn before them, a chill rising from the bottom of their hearts.

If the real Qingming Inn has moved, who were we just talking to?

They rushed back inside, only to find the inn empty, no trace of the man in the white paper hat in sight.

“Was he a human or a ghost?”

The two were horrified that they hadn’t detected anything unusual about the white paper-hatted man earlier. The fact that he hadn’t reacted to Meng Jingzhou’s Pure Yang Physique suggested that his cultivation had reached terrifying heights. Was he a Ghost King?

“Go!” a decisive voice commanded as a group of cultivators dressed as constables emerged from all directions and stormed into the inn.

“Damn it, he got away!” The bearded leader was in a foul mood upon finding no sign of the man in the white paper hat.

“Big Brother, may I ask what’s going on here?” Lu Yang inquired politely.

Seeing that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had just exited the inn, the bearded constable concluded they were not suspicious figures and explained, “This Qingming Inn has been abandoned for five years, yet people keep claiming they have stayed here. They thought it was haunted and reported it to us. Through our secret investigation and cross-checking of testimonies, we finally uncovered the truth.

“A man wearing a white paper hat has been impersonating the innkeeper and tricking Corpse Drivers into paying for lodging here.

“Since corpses aren’t picky about accommodations, the poor conditions were initially understandable. Eventually, some Corpse Drivers couldn’t endure the deplorable conditions anymore and complained to the main Qingming Inn branch. They were flabbergasted, saying that the branch in this location had closed long ago. And that’s how the scam was exposed.

“After uncovering the truth, we thought we could simply wait here to catch him, but we didn’t think we’d let him escape!”

Lu Yang, “...”

You people in Wilderness Province go to such lengths just to make money?

1. The Qingming Festival is the day where people honor their ancestors and deceased family. ☜

2. “Baiquan” translates directly to “white spring.” ☜

Chapter 402: White Paper-Hatted Man

“You two are outsiders, right?” The bearded constable noticed Lu Yang’s unfamiliarity with the Wilderness Province and was kind enough to remind him. “If you run into that bastard in the white paper hat again, you must be careful! He’s been committing crimes everywhere, sly and slippery as an eel!”

“How so?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were puzzled.

The bearded constable fumed. “We’ve been searching for that scoundrel for ages, but to no avail. We have no idea where he came from, but he’s been active here for several years.

“Pick any place in the Wilderness Province—chances are, he’s committed a crime there. This time, it’s impersonating an innkeeper to run a shady establishment. Last time, it was instigating his accomplice into theft, and when his accomplice got wanted, he turned them in for the bounty. What made things worse was that the bastard collected the reward right under our noses, and none of us recognized that it was him!

“Before that, he pretended to be a corpse and sold himself to a Corpse Driver. When they tried refining him, they realized that the ‘corpse’ moved! It nearly gave them a heart attack. Even after that bastard left, they were still so shaken that they thought the corpse had come back to life. They chanted incantations for several days before finally realizing they had been duped!

“There was another time when the Barbarian Tribe reported someone smuggling people across the border. It was him again!

“This bastard of a grandson would stoop to anything for money! If we could catch him, it’d shave five working days off our annual schedule!”

The bearded constable grew increasingly furious as he spoke about the white-hatted man. Had the man appeared at that moment, the constable might have swallowed him whole.

Capturing this white paper-hatted man is not just my wish but the wish of the entire Wilderness Province.

“There’s something strange about this scoundrel. On several occasions, he appeared in two different locations simultaneously, as if there were two of him. I’m not sure whether they’re twins or if something else is at play.

“And just now, we surrounded the inn, and you two were at the entrance, but who actually detected him leaving?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded. Given their cultivation, the actions of ordinary cultivators couldn’t have slipped past their scope of detection, not even master thieves and recidivists.

For someone to have escaped under such circumstances suggested that the white paper-hatted man either possessed extraordinary methods or cultivation far beyond people’s expectations.

“Immortal Fairy, did you notice the white paper-hatted man escaping?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes, thinking Lu Yang was seriously underestimating her. “He fled westward. But don’t waste your energy. Even if you two help, don’t count on the constables catching up to him. His escape techniques are unconventional.

“Besides, even if you catch him, it’d likely just be a clone and won’t affect him at all.”

Lu Yang was stunned. For the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to make such an assessment means that this white paper-hatted man is even more troublesome to deal with than I’d imagined.

The bearded constable directed the other constables to secure the scene and scour for clues. “Don’t forget to paste the seal strips!” he barked.

“Big Boss, are seal strips effective? He always tears them off anyway,” a subordinate gingerly asked. With the white paper-hatted man’s blatant disregard for the law, he would simply tear the seal strips off and ‘reopen’ the inn as usual.

The bearded constable glared at him. “Just do it! If he tears them off, that’s on him! He’ll face an extra charge!”

“We’ll take our leave then.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou bid goodbye to the bearded constable. Before departing, Lu Yang added helpfully, “I sensed him fleeing westward when he escaped.”

The bearded constable gave Lu Yang a surprised look but said nothing.

“Wilderness Province truly breeds talents. Who knows? We might actually find a solution to my curse here,” Meng Jingzhou remarked. I should really go out and travel around more. I mean, we’ve barely entered this place and already encountered such extraordinary people and events.

“After wasting half a day, we still haven’t secured lodging,” Lu Yang reminded Meng Jingzhou of their priorities.

Meng Jingzhou patted their horse’s back. “Old Horse, can you find us a village to rest in?”

The old horse swished its tail and nibbled some roadside grass before considerately pulling the carriage to the nearest village.

Before long, they arrived at a village. At the entrance was a boulder engraved with the characters “Jianshi Village.”[1]

“Why’s it so quiet?”

The two alighted, hoping to seek lodging for the night. However, they soon realized that every household had its doors tightly shut, with only the faint glow of oil lamps. Silence blanketed the entire place. Naturally, there was not a single soul walking the paths in the village.

In Lu Yang’s impression, with no entertainment available, this time of day was when villagers would have their doors open, visiting and chatting with neighbors. “It’s almost as if they’re scared of something. Strange.” Lu Yang’s brow furrowed.

Meng Jingzhou approached the largest homestead and knocked. “Fellow villager, we’d like to seek lodging for the night.”

Clank. Creak. An old man opened the door, revealing only half of his face as he peered at his two visitors warily. “Who are you?”

Meng Jingzhou flashed his amiable smile he had honed at the barbeque shop. “We are travelers passing by. It’s already late, and we were hoping to stay over for the night. Would that be possible? We will pay, of course.”

The old man impatiently chased them away. “Shoo shoo shoo! Jianshi Village doesn’t welcome outsiders. Leave now! If you don’t, be careful of getting eaten by the corpses!”

“Eaten by corpses? You have corpses here? We brothers are cultivators; we can help you get rid of the corpses.”

His words only seemed to incense the old man further. “No need! Begone!” With that, he slammed the door shut.

“Hey, old man, you’re being unreasonable!” Meng Jingzhou felt that the old man was a bit unhinged. I kindly offered to solve his problem, yet he chased me away.

“Perhaps there are females in the family, so you’re unable to go in?” Lu Yang teased mischievously.

“Buzz off.” Meng Jingzhou chased Lu Yang away as if he was swatting at a fly.

Unwilling to give up, Meng Jingzhou tried several other households, but they would either chase the two away or not open their doors at all.

Meng Jingzhou pouted. “Not friendly at all.”

“What do we do then? Try another village?”

Meng Jingzhou didn’t want to go somewhere else again. “That’s too troublesome. I noticed what looked like a shrine or an ancestral hall near the village entrance just now. It looked quite clean. We could make do there for the night.”

“Fine by me.” Lu Yang was also weary of moving back and forth again. We were turned away by the Qingming Inn earlier, and now we’re rejected again at Jianshi Village. Who knows if it’ll be the same at the next village? Instead of running around like this, we might as well find a place to make do for the night and investigate things in the morning.

~~~

Upon arriving at the ancestral hall, they used Three Flavor True Fire to light the oil lamps, illuminating the ancestral hall.

“Quite clean.”

The two bowed to the ancestral tablets. “Sorry, seniors. We’ll just be staying here for one night.”

~~~

Meanwhile, at the village’s cemetery, stones shook, and the ground loosened, as though something was stirring below.

A dessicated claw burrowed out of the soil.

In the next instant, claws burst out of the soil like bamboo shoots after a rain, too numerous to count...

1. “Jianshi” translates literally to “tough/firm rock.” ☜

Chapter 403: This Immortal Uses the Peak Corpse-Driving Technique! freeωebnovēl.c૦m

Ancestral hall.

“It seems like the villagers here frequent this ancestral hall. Look, there are so many food offerings before the ancestral tablets.”

Meng Jingzhou was somewhat surprised. The ancestral hall was clean and bright, with plain offerings of mantou and pickled vegetables placed in front of the spirit tablets. “You don’t say. The food is still warm.”

Lu Yang noticed mantou was still giving off heat, as if they had been freshly steamed. “Looking at this makes me hungry. Let's eat something.”

Meng Jingzhou took out various prepared dishes from his identity jade tablet. These were purchased from the commercial street and could greatly aid one’s cultivation. Such were the wonders and advantages of spirit chefs.

Seeing these dishes reminded Lu Yang of the immortal chef residing in his mental space. Eating her meals provides even greater cultivation benefits. Lu Yang’s mood grew heavy.

Raising his hand, he tossed out a ball of Three Flavor True Fire. Without needing any fuel like branches, just a wisp of spirit energy was enough to keep the flame burning steadily.

The two heated the food over the flame, enhancing the already tantalizing aromas.

“Speaking of Big Senior Sister’s absence, can’t you use your Lu-Style Animal Form Fist to summon her?” An idea suddenly struck Meng Jingzhou. This is the most convenient solution. It’s not like Big Senior Sister would be affected by the karmic backlash.

Lu Yang shot Meng Jingzhou a sidelong glance. Easy for you to suggest when you’re not the one summoning Big Senior Sister. “Every time I summoned Big Senior Sister, it was a life-or-death crisis. It’s not like you have any emergency. To summon Big Senior Sister for something as trivial as your karmic backlash, do you think she’ll take care of your karmic backlash first or take care of you first?”

Meng Jingzhou imagined the scene in his mind.

Lu Yang summons Big Senior Sister. After she hears about everything that has transpired, she stares at me coldly, as if she’s looking at a dead person.

His blood ran cold. “In...in that case, forget it. Let’s settle the karmic backlash ourselves.”

Lu Yang explained further, “Besides, Big Senior Sister is immensely busy and has many important matters to handle. If I disturb her and she makes a mistake or gets things delayed, what then?”

This was precisely the reason Lu Yang wouldn’t easily summon Yun Zhi. While I can ask for Big Senior Sister’s help when I run into difficulties, it doesn’t allow me to hone myself, and I shouldn’t interrupt her crucial duties.

Unless Lu Yang faced a life-and-death crisis, he wouldn’t summon her.

“It’s a pity that First Elder isn’t here. With his experience, he probably could have offered alternative ideas.” Although Meng Jingzhou wasn’t certain what First Elder was up to outside, he could make a good guess. He’s most likely constructing tombs again.

Given First Elder’s penchant for building tombs and filling them with jiangshi, Meng Jingzhou was certain he had business dealings with the Corpse-Driving Sect. With his high cultivation and rich experience, First Elder might know how to handle their situation or at least direct them to the right people in Wilderness Province.

“I heard that the corpse-driving tradition here dates back to the collapse of the Great Yu Dynasty one hundred thousand years ago. The world was in turmoil, and rebellions swept across every corner of the land. This place was rampant with slaughter, with blood staining rivers and corpses strewn across the land. Numerous corpses underwent unnatural transformations, giving rise to many Corpse Drivers. Some came together to seek strength in numbers and eventually formed a sect—the Corpse-Driving Sect you see today.” Meng Jingzhou pointed to a section in the Anthropology of the Wilderness Province.

“So the custom runs deep,” Lu Yang mused. 100,000 years is already considered distant; even the Dao-Seeking Sect, one of the most ancient sects, only traces back 120,000 years.

“Corpse-Driving predates even that,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy chimed in.

“Corpse-Driving Techniques already existed in ancient times?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy smacked her lips as she reminisced about those eventful years. “More or less. That said, they varied wildly back then, and there was no standardized name like today, where they’re collectively known as ‘Corpse-Driving Techniques.’

“Remember that fool who knew Law Follows Words? Just his voice could command corpses. When he faced formidable opponents, he would burrow into cemeteries and shout, then corpses would come scrambling out. That was genuinely terrifying; one of the most powerful opponents I’ve met.”

For the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to call someone a fool, he must have truly been one. Lu Yang recalled this person. He was a troublesome opponent who knew Law Follows Words. His reputation in ancient times was resounding. He was among the prime candidates for ascending to an immortal, and later generations passed down his legends. However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy ambushed him, and after he yelled, “The pain is killing me!” he really ended up dying.

“Then there was that person who formed the Harem Golden Core. By chance, he nurtured a beautiful jiangshi. After a period of bonding, she developed emotions and advanced to the level of a hanba drought demon, as if she had truly resurrected. Eventually, she joined that guy’s harem.”

Lu Yang also recalled the person with the Harem Golden Core. He was surrounded by countless beauties, with many in his harem. With the help of various beauties, he cultivated the Blissful Union art and trained with women every night, allowing his cultivation to skyrocket. However, due to his failure in managing the relations within his harem, he was ultimately torn to pieces by these women.

Honestly speaking, if we exclude the final outcome, the experiences of this Harem Golden Core prodigy are pretty enviable.

“Immortal Fairy, do you know Corpse-Driving Techniques?”

“Of course! This immortal uses the peak Corpse-Driving Technique!”

“You do?” Lu Yang’s eyes lit up in surprise. As expected of the Immortal Fairy! She knows every spell, and even the finest ones! Hers will definitely be superior to the Corpse-Driving Sect’s techniques!

“Do you want to learn the Play-Dead Technique?”

“I want... hold on, Play-Dead Technique?” Lu Yang quickly reacted.

“Yes! I’ll first play dead, and then revive—isn’t that the peak Corpse-Driving Technique?”

Lu Yang fell silent. Resurrecting the dead does qualify as a peak Corpse-Driving Technique, but I can’t help but find something off.

Recalling something else, he asked, “Apart from your Play-Dead Technique, are there other Corpse-Driving Techniques that can resurrect the dead?”

“Not sure.”

“Not sure?”

“In theory, there are, but I’ve yet to see any Corpse-Driving Technique rivalling my Play-Dead Technique.

“The five of us had discussed this issue when we gathered for meals. Logically speaking, peak Corpse-Driving Techniques can resurrect the dead, but with the original soul gone and a new consciousness born within the old body, how can it be called resurrection?”

Lu Yang wondered, Did the four other immortals raise this topic because they were worried about suddenly dropping dead from eating your food?

“Wait, something is approaching!” Lu Yang didn’t continue the conversation, abruptly exiting his mental space. He sensed multiple entities drawing near, and judging by the sounds, the number was overwhelming!

Almost simultaneously, Meng Jingzhou reacted, assuming a stance to defend against their enemies.

Bang! The doors to the ancestral hall burst open, revealing hordes of shriveled corpses outside. At a glance, there were close to a hundred!

The two released their spiritual consciousness and realized these withered corpses had completely surrounded the ancestral hall!

“Why are there walking corpses everywhere in Wilderness Province?”

Chapter 404: The People of Wilderness Province Have Remarkably Progressive Ideals

In the span of a single night’s rest, they had encountered two groups of walking corpses. The walking corpses held farming tools—shovels, rakes, and the like—seemingly snatched from villagers’ homes. In their hands, these tools had transformed into dangerous weapons.

“Say what you will, but only in Wilderness Province can you encounter something like this. Quite the eye-opener,” Lu Yang joked with a smirk tugging the corner of his mouth. He drew out his Qingfeng Sword, whose blade gleamed under the candlelight.

Despite the sheer number of armed walking corpses surrounding the ancestral hall, we are almighty Golden Core seniors who can even establish our own minor clans outside and become the founding ancestors of sects. How could we be troubled by mere rural walking corpses?

“No wonder the villagers didn’t let us stay overnight. They were worried about danger. And they even mentioned something about being eaten by corpses—is this what they meant?” Although the villagers’ attitude had been less than welcoming, Meng Jingzhou was one to hold a grudge. Helping the village get rid of the walking corpses wasn’t an issue.

“Look, there are female corpses!” Lu Yang suddenly exclaimed, pointing at a long-haired female zombie.

Meng Jingzhou was bewildered. “Why would a corpse’s gender matter? Isn’t it normal for there to be female corpses?”

“What I mean is—doesn’t your karmic backlash prevent you from meeting women? But you can run into these female corpses, which shows that your karmic backlash is only limited to living people. Corpses and demons don’t count. If we can’t solve your problem in Wilderness Province, you could go stay in the Demon Region until you reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage.”

“Go to hell! I refuse to believe Big Senior Sister won’t return eventually!” Meng Jingzhou snapped. He acted first, launching himself at the walking corpses.

“Crushing Fist!” Meng Jingzhou drove his horn-like knuckles into the walking corpses.

Boom! The walking corpse exploded, and the force sent the encroaching horde flying back, clearing a path.

“Hmm, these corpses are so tough.” Meng Jingzhou was stunned. He had assumed that these were random corpses from the wild, fragile enough to be beaten into pulp with a single Crushing Fist.

“Immortal Fairy, these walking corpses aren’t contagious, right?” Lu Yang had originally intended to stop Meng Jingzhou from acting until they understood the dangers, but it seemed too late for any of that now.

“What do you by ‘contagious?’” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was confused by Lu Yang’s question.

“You know, if a living person gets bitten, they turn into a walking corpse?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang as if he was an idiot. “Of course not, or rather, I have never even heard of such a thing. Why would you think that?”

“Just a random thought.”

Assured there was no risk of infection, Lu Yang joined the fray without hesitation. Upon engaging them, he also noticed that these walking corpses were unusually tough, a clear sign of being refined by an expert.

“Did you really think you could eat us? Dream on!” The two burst out laughing as they hurled the walking corpses out of the ancestral hall.

To the walking corpses, it might have seemed like they had surrounded the duo. But from the duo’s perspective, they had the walking corpses cornered.

“None of you shall escape! Today, we brothers will eradicate this menace for the people!”

Just as the two were about to unleash their unique arts and wipe out the walking corpses, they heard an elderly voice nearby.

“Young brothers, please show mercy! They mean no harm!”

It was the same old man who had refused them lodging at the start.

“What I said about them eating people was just a scare tactic! They simply wanted to eat the offerings in the ancestral hall, and you two happened to be there!”

The two froze. Upon closer reflection, it did seem like the walking corpses never had any intentions of attacking them.

They tentatively ceased their assault and observed that the corpses didn’t attack them but instead went around them to enter the ancestral hall.

Only after all the walking corpses had shuffled into the ancestral hall did they approach the old man for an explanation.

The old man sighed. “I’m the village chief of Jianshi Village. You might find the explanation behind this matter of the walking corpses hard to believe, so it’s better that I show you something first.”

They watched the walking corpses swarm into the ancestral hall, crowding around the still-warm mantou. Soon, the mantou turned cold, all traces of warmth gone. Only then did the walking corpses give up.

When they left the ancestral hall, the walking corpses held their shovels, rakes, and plows as they marched in unison out of Jianshi Village.

The trio tailed them all the way, though the walking corpses didn’t go far, stopping at the fields to till the soil with their farming tools. Some even collected water from the river with carrying poles and tirelessly irrigated the fields. Others, lacking tools, squatted to pull weeds or squash pests. With well-defined delegation of roles, the walking corpses looked like diligent old farmers.

After finishing their tasks, the walking corpses grabbed their tools and walked from the fields to the village entrance, then to the cemetery at the outskirts, where they dug holes with their tools in hand and buried themselves.

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

The two rubbed their temples, wondering if they were hallucinating.

“Do all of you people in Wilderness Province use walking corpses for farming?” This is far more advanced than anything in other provinces. Even our Dao-Seeking Sect can’t compare. Back in our sect, we only used the Blue-Eyed Water Buffaloes and Third Elder for plowing the land.

The village chief helplessly explained, “It’s not what you think. We’re just ordinary folks. How could we afford to maintain so many walking corpses? The truth is, we also don’t know where they came from.

“One night, we were resting under the tree at the village entrance when we saw them approaching. At first, everyone was terrified and thought those walking corpses were going to attack us. But after coming into contact with them, we discovered that they meant no harm. Perhaps they had exhausted their energy and simply stayed on in our village.

“Although we don’t have Corpse Drivers here, I’d apprenticed under one in my youth. Using whatever fraction of what I’d learned, I tried steaming mantou to feed them.

“This method proved effective. The walking corpses became active again. Then, someone suggested putting them to work in the fields. I thought it was a good idea, so I drove them to plow the land.

“And just like that, we now rest during the day, steam a pot of mantou at dusk, and place them in the ancestral hall. At night, the walking corpses climb out of their graves, absorb the mantou’s yang energy, and till the fields. Since everyone is still afraid of the walking corpses, all the households close their doors and stay indoors after dark.

“After the walking corpses are done farming, they will automatically bury themselves until the next night, and the cycle repeats.

“I'm not sure if I should be saying this, but ever since the walking corpses took over farming, life’s been much easier. We even have free time for other matters.”

“Then why did you refuse us lodging?”

The village chief admitted honestly, “We feared you’d find out about the ownerless walking corpses here and report it to the authorities. If the authorities locate their master, wouldn’t we have to farm by ourselves again?

“We initially wanted to scare you off. Who would have thought that you not only stayed but also decided to sleep in the ancestral hall? Seeing that the truth would be exposed regardless, I figured showing up to explain the matter was better than letting you get beaten by the walking corpses.”

Chapter 405: Unusual Walking Corpses

After listening to the village chief’s account, the two suddenly wrapped their heads around the whole situation. “No wonder these walking corpses are so tough. They don’t seem like they were refined by an ordinary person. So it’s because they were lost.”

“Is it common for walking corpses to go missing?”

The village chief shook his head. “How could it be? I’ve lived for eighty years, and this is my first time seeing masterless walking corpses. Before this, I’d only heard stories.”

“May I ask what usually causes walking corpses to lose their masters?”

“I’ve heard there are mainly two reasons walking corpses are masterless. Either the master has died, freeing the walking corpses from their control and leaving them to wander, or the master voluntarily lifted the control over the walking corpses. Otherwise, there is a third possibility that the walking corpses turned on their master and devoured them.

“Judging by the behavior of the walking corpses in our village, they don’t seem bloodthirsty, so the third scenario seems unlikely.”

“Is there any way to find their master?” Lu Yang asked.

The village chief’s face twisted into a complicated expression, his brows furrowed tightly before he finally sighed. “There is. Every Corpse Driver leaves a unique mark on their walking corpses to claim ownership. The ones in our village all bear the same mark on their right wrists—like this.” He crouched and traced three interlocking circles on the ground, with the character for “ghost” inscribed in the center.

“If the master is still alive, the same mark would be on his right wrist.

“Although my cultivation is limited at the Apex Level Two Qi Training Stage, I studied under a remarkable Corpse Driver in my youth. My teacher was at the Apex Level Six Qi Training Stage!

“During my apprenticeship, I memorized the marks of every Corpse Driver in the surrounding commanderies and counties, and none had a similar style. As for those from other regions, I’ve never seen them before.” This was one of the reasons the village chief hadn’t reported the matter. Since the walking corpses didn’t belong to any Corpse Drivers nearby, even if he handed them over to the local authorities, they wouldn’t be able to track down the master.

“Old Sir, have you heard of the Corpse-Driving Sect?”

The village chief couldn’t help but chuckle. “How could I not have heard of them? Thirty years ago, I even glimpsed a young talented disciple from a distance, someone far beyond the likes of me, who struggled just to grasp the basics of Corpse-Driving Techniques.”

“Do you know where the Corpse-Driving Sect is located?”

“That’s quite far.” The village chief pointed west. “The Corpse-Driving Sect lies right in the center of Wilderness Province. If you keep heading west from here, it’s eighty million li away.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded. “Looks like we’ll need a few more days of travel.”

With the old horse around, eighty million li was not considered far. When Meng Jingzhou had run away from home, the journey from the imperial capital to the Dao-Seeking Sect was even longer, yet it had taken mere days.

The speed depended entirely on the old horse’s mood.

Back then, Meng Jingzhou had assumed that the chassis of the carriage was embedded with spatial arrays, allowing it to traverse space and shrink distances instantly. Only later did he realize that while the carriage was indeed a treasure, the old horse was the real reason for their speed.

“Old Sir, since we are already aware of the walking corpses’ presence, could you let us brothers stay for the night?”

“Alright then. Anyway, my old partner has passed away, and my children have moved to the county. Having you stay overnight is simply adding two more quilts.”

~~~

After a night’s rest in Jianshi Village, the two bid the village chief farewell and resumed their journey.

“You two had pretty good luck last night,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked as she lazily stretched her limbs and relaxed her muscles and bones. Although souls had no true muscles and bones, some habits from life persisted beyond death.

“Pretty good luck?”

“Exactly! Those walking corpses you bumped into last night had been meticulously refined by a powerful cultivator. Without anyone to command them and with insufficient yang energy, they didn’t even have the strength to move and were barely surviving on those big mantou. Otherwise, you would have stood no chance against them.

“If I’m not mistaken, that horde of walking corpses could collectively rival a Fusion cultivator.”

“Fusion cultivator?!” Lu Yang was astonished. He only knew that the walking corpses from last night were sturdy, but he never expected it’d be to the extent of facing off with a Fusion cultivator. Even if Lu Yang lacked the expertise in corpse refinement techniques, he could figure out that only a Fusion cultivator was capable of crafting such walking corpses.

These walking corpses are a Fusion cultivator’s combat method. How could they have been abandoned so carelessly? Did a Fusion-stage Corpse Driver die?

The thought sent a chill down his spine.

In this age, brutal conflicts were rare, and Fusion cultivators seldom fought to the death. Beyond their sheer power, they possessed a multitude of life-saving techniques, making it extremely difficult for one to kill another, unless the gap in strength was overwhelming—as with the Taciturn Daoist, the First Elder, or Qiu Jin’an compared to an ordinary Fusion cultivator.

Noticing Lu Yang’s expression shift, Meng Jingzhou asked, “What’s wrong?”

“You remember that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy resides within me, right?” Back when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was resurrected, Meng Jingzhou was right beside him.

Meng Jingzhou blinked, then smacked his palm as if he had jolted from a reverie. “Ah~ I remember now. You have an ancient immortal inside you. What did she say?”

“...Hold on, let’s not talk about what she has said for now; why do you look like you just remembered?”

“You can’t blame me for this.” Meng Jingzhou scratched his head sheepishly and counted off on his fingers. “In my mind, I envision someone with an ancient immortal inside them to have endless miraculous luck, wield battered ancient relics as weapons, hold myriad earth-shattering secrets, be well-versed in sundry cultivation methods, be unbeatable among peers, often spout astounding wisdom beyond their level, be constantly surrounded by beautiful women throwing themselves at them, and treat exploring secret domains like going home.

“However, your daily life doesn’t match. The only fitting trait is being unbeatable among peers, though that isn’t anything spectacular in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Oh right, and you know various random ancient secrets useful only for bluffing the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Yeah, I’d like to know why too.

“So, what did the immortal say?”

“She said that last night’s horde of walking corpses could rival a Fusion cultivator in terms of combat power.”

Meng Jingzhou’s pupils contracted, evidently thinking of the same issue as Lu Yang. How could corpses of such caliber be left wandering outside? Something must have happened in secret!

“Let’s head to a major city and ask around to check whether there were any battles or if a Fusion cultivator had perished. Something this big must have left a trace.”

Lu Yang nodded, concurring with his suggestion.

“By the way, since you have an ancient immortal inside you, can you help me ask if she has a solution for my karmic backlash?” Meng Jingzhou’s fervent gaze bore into Lu Yang.

That’s right, even if Big Senior Sister isn’t here to help, I still have an ancient immortal here. Ancient immortals possessed heaven-defying powers—resolving a mere karmic backlash should be nothing more than a flick of the wrist for them, right?

“I’ve asked her.”

“What did she say?”

“She told you to go die.”

“?”

Chapter 406: Meng Jingzhou’s Immortal Calamity

Within the mental space.

Despite his mortal frame, Lu Yang assisted Meng Jingzhou in resisting an immortal’s calamity—a touching act of immeasurable virtue.

“Just watch me teach this Meng boy a lesson! What does he mean by saying it makes no difference whether this immortal is here or not?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy bristled like a kitten with claws bared, prepared to give Meng Jingzhou a piece of her mind.

“Immortal Fairy, Immortal Fairy, Old Meng is just a mortal running his mouth. He’s not worth your anger.” Lu Yang desperately clutched her arm to prevent her from storming out. ƒreeωebnovel.ƈom

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy huffed. “Tell me—haven’t I been kind enough to help him think of a solution, all on your account? I treated him decently, didn’t I? And this is how he repays me? By slandering me?”

“Immortal Fairy, you are magnanimous. Old Meng is young and insensible. Please let it slide this time.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy begrudgingly plopped back down, swinging her tiny feet petulantly. “Tell me then, which of the Meng boy’s criteria don’t I fit?”

“Old Meng said that someone with an ancient immortal inside them should have endless miraculous luck?” Lu Yang tentatively responded.

“Didn’t I make you the acting sect leader of the almighty Dao-Seeking Sect, with even Lass Yun obeying your orders?! You even hosted the Five-Elements Sect!”

“Then what about wielding battered ancient relics as weapons?”

“Isn’t your Mingyue Sword exactly that? It’s an immortal’s flying sword meticulously forged by the Heaven Mandate Immortal himself, treasured by the Qilin Immortal, and handled with extreme care until those two lasses from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes snapped it.”

“Then what about holding earth-shattering secrets?”

“All those secret ancient tales I’ve shared—aren’t they secrets? Where else could you hear them?”

Lu Yang pondered. True, if I share her stories with others, the dignified image the pretentious Heaven Mandate Immortal worked so hard to maintain would crumble. Those do count as earth-shattering secrets.

“And what about being well-versed in sundry cultivation methods?”

“Haven’t I been demonstrating how one can cultivate through sleep? Not to mention the most ancient Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth art that can boost your cultivation speed.”

“What about being unbeatable among peers?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grew smug at this. In a flash, she stood up on the bed and peered down at Lu Yang with pride.

“Have you forgotten the Unbeatable Golden Core I taught you? It lets you become unbeatable among peers of the same level and win every battle. Only I can achieve that—not even the Mandate Immortal, Qilin Immortal, or anyone else!

“Also, when you were the acting sect leader, didn’t you defeat Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration experts while being merely at the Foundation Establishment Stage? Could you have done that without me?”

“Then what about spouting astounding wisdom far beyond one’s level?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s excitement waned, and she sat back on the bed, her resentment toward Meng Jingzhou now dissipated.

“Despite your young age, you already know more secret tales of immortals and the ancient era, making you more erudite than Fusion cultivators. Doesn’t this count?”

“What about beautiful women throwing themselves at you?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed a rare troubled look and hissed. “Having beautiful women throw themselves at you might be a bit tricky. However, you still have plenty of pretty girls around you, such as Lass Yun, your junior sister Tao Yaoye, that little lass from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace...what was her name again—oh right, Lan Ting.”

“...But I knew them all before you were revived.”

“Shall I graciously hug you instead?”

Lu Yang eyed her exquisite face that ranked first among the Ten Ancient Beauties and calmly declined. My fortune and fate are too fragile to withstand the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—the source of curses.

“And what about treating exploring secret domains like going home?”

“That’s a bit hard. Most secret domains I know are probably gone... wait, haven’t you been to the Everlasting Secret Domain? My kitchen’s there!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Old Meng is absolutely right. How am I anything like someone with an ancient immortal inside them? I’ve survived until now only because of my tough fate.

Even my shifu’s childhood tale about having an ancient ferocious beast sealed inside him sounds more believable.

Having pacified the ruffled Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang finally exited his mental space.

“Remember—you owe me a life.”

“?” It’s not Lu Yang’s first time acting unhinged. Meng Jingzhou didn’t pay much mind to Lu Yang’s eccentricities.

“Old Horse, go to the nearest city. We’ll gather some news.” Meng Jingzhou patted the old horse.

The old horse ambled unhurriedly, as if it knew where the city was.

As the carriage traversed a lonely mountain path, a torrential rain pelted down without warning, as though the heavens sought to wash the world clean.

Boom! A thunderous noise echoed above, sounding like something massively heavy was tumbling down.

The two lifted the carriage curtain to peer through the curtain of rain. The mountain convulsed violently, spewing mud and rocks like a rampaging wild beast wreaking havoc as it tore madly down the slope. Countless trees were uprooted by the mudslide, toppling and tumbling down the mountain.

“It’s a landslide!”

Crash! The sludge charged toward the carriage like underworld soldiers.

Fortunately, the old horse’s cultivation was profound, and the carriage was a magical treasure; mere natural disasters in the mortal world did not pose a threat to the carriage.

After the landslide was over, the two assessed the situation.

“Both front and back are blocked.”

Meng Jingzhou frowned. The carriage was unharmed, but both the road ahead and behind were blocked by mud and rocks, making passage impossible.

If the old horse chose to, they could escape. However, judging by the old horse’s leisurely demeanor which was indistinguishable from an ordinary horse, it was clear it had no intention of intervening.

Meng Jingzhou sighed helplessly. It’s somewhat understandable. The old horse is here to ensure my safety, not serve as my servant and do everything for me. If it did, it would defeat the purpose of training.

“Clear the obstacles.”

The two disembarked and wrapped themselves with spirit energy to avoid getting drenched by the rain. They each unleashed their methods against the debris.

“Crushing Fist!” Meng Jingzhou employed Crushing Fist again. While it lacked destructive power, its impact was tremendous, suitable for dealing with weaker cultivators.

Boom! The debris ahead swayed slightly. Meng Jingzhou mustered his strength and unleashed a barrage of Crushing Fists, his punches carving a road through the sludge.

Not to be outdone, Lu Yang activated his spell, focusing his gaze as he slightly parted his mouth. “Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth!” With a sharp inhalation, Lu Yang sucked up all the debris at the back!

Meng Jingzhou was awestruck. This move is so formidable! So much debris vanished in just a breath!

“Care to learn?” Lu Yang grinned mischievously. Meng Jingzhou instinctively sensed a conspiracy within.

The two were about to continue their conversation when they heard another rumbling sound from above again.

Meng Jingzhou bellowed, “Another landslide? Is this never-ending?!”

Lu Yang silently stared at Meng Jingzhou, seeming to have understood the reason. I’m an innocent bystander implicated in this calamity, just like the fishes dying from the river drying up because the water was used to extinguish the fire at the city’s gates.

“We want to go to the city, but there are undoubtedly women inside the city. With your karmic backlash, you won’t be able to enter the city. I’m purely collateral damage.”

“What should we do then?” Realization dawned upon Meng Jingzhou.

“You stay here. I’ll proceed alone.”

Chapter 407: Intelligence on Wilderness Province

After parting ways with Meng Jingzhou, Lu Yang’s luck did improve significantly.

On the way to the nearest city, Lu Yang valiantly defeated mountain bandits and rescued two noble young ladies. Despite their effusive gratitude, Lu Yang firmly refused their requests to marry into their families, bidding them farewell and departing with an air of loftiness.

Later, he ran into robbers attacking a convoy of armed escorts. Lu Yang lent them a hand, and the young miss of the armed escort agency was extremely moved. She said that it was her first time overseeing the convoy in escorting goods, and if not for Lu Yang’s timely intervention, the escort mission would have failed, severely damaging their agency’s reputation. Impressed by Lu Yang’s extraordinary skills, she invited him to join their armed escort agency and even offered him the position of Head Armed Escort.

Unsurprisingly, Lu Yang declined again.

Finally, Lu Yang encountered a young lady hosting a martial arts contest for marriage. She invited heroes from diverse backgrounds, proclaiming she would wed whoever defeated her.

At the sight of this, Lu Yang quickened his pace and hastily left. “I've long heard of the heroism and mettle women in Wilderness Province possess and how they often go out and about. I’ve finally seen it for myself today.”

The people of Wilderness Province were known for their boldness and heroism, and the same applied to the women there. Unlike most women in the Central Plains, who were confined to their boudoirs, the women here engaged in similar pursuits as men.

With Meng Jingzhou by his side previously, Lu Yang never had the chance to witness it.

“It’s a pity that Old Meng’s sparse fortune prevents him from seeing this.” Lu Yang thought of Meng Jingzhou with schadenfreude. “That said, public security in Wilderness Province is really poor. There aren’t so many mountain bandits and robbers elsewhere.”

After passing through these “beauty trials”, Lu Yang arrived at the nearest city.

The walls were built from giant bricks and exuded a rugged grandeur reminiscent of the Demon Suppression Pass, yet with a distinct style of its own.

“Yuanshan City.”[1] Lu Yang raised his head and softly read the name of the city before entering its gates.

Since the Luodi Merchant Guild operated businesses dealing with intelligence brokerage, purchasing their reports would be the most efficient way of understanding local affairs.

However, there was some information that the Luodi Merchant Guild didn’t dare to sell, such as intelligence regarding the Five Great Immortal Sects, especially the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Thus, Yun Zhi’s victories over her peers and all the sect leaders during the Immortal Sect Grand Tournament were not within the scope of information the merchant guild would peddle.

Lu Yang noted how extremely few people were aware of Yun Zhi’s existence. Without special means, they wouldn’t even know her name. Even if they did learn of her existence, they simply regarded her as just another unremarkable disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect with nothing worthy of their attention.

He speculated that this stemmed from Yun Zhi’s rare public demonstrations and the merchant guild refraining from selling such information.

As for the other four immortal sects, the merchant guild still sold bits of information here and there—for example, that the number of people in the Hanging Monastery had reached a historic high, now exceeding twelve members, and that the abbot had cultivated the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation to comprehend the true meaning of Buddhism, so he no longer spoke and only communicated by beating people.

As for intelligence concerning the imperial court, the merchant guild would exercise discretion in selling it. For example, they didn’t sell the information that the Taciturn Daoist Priest and the Minister of Justice were locked in the same prison cell and that the entire Ministry of Justice had to relocate their office because of it.

Arriving at the merchant guild, Lu Yang bought their most detailed Wilderness Province intelligence report, and the first entry already struck him like thunder.

“The daughter of Wilderness Province’s governor organized a birthday banquet. The governor sent out invitations to various factions, asking them to send their representatives to offer their blessings and celebratory gifts. At the birthday banquet, talented young men from these factions showcased their all to win a smile from the governor’s daughter. However, the governor is now suspected of receiving bribes, and these factions are suspected of bribing influential figures. All involved have been arrested.”

The merchant guild even thoughtfully appended the relevant legal clauses and precedent cases as a stern warning.

“The newly appointed governor of Wilderness Province took office and delivered a speech titled Rectifying the Crooked Customs of Wilderness Province, requesting that all local officials study its contents.

“The Barbarian Tribe’s coming-of-age ceremony proceeded as scheduled. The young barbarian, Man Gu, survived for over seven days in the wilderness and slaughtered nearly a hundred Golden Core demon beasts, attaining victory.

“This brat Man Gu only mentioned he was going home to visit his family. Turns out he was taking part in the Barbarian Tribe’s coming-of-age ceremony,” Lu Yang muttered in realization. He hadn’t seen Man Gu in some time and was puzzled why a simple family visit would take so long.

He had heard of the Barbarian Tribe’s coming-of-age ceremony. It required those on the cusp of adulthood to be thrown into the most perilous wilderness. Surviving past seven days would count as passing, but those who managed to slaughter demon beasts would earn an even higher evaluation. Rankings were also determined by the quantity and quality of their kills.

“The Barbarian Tribe still upholds this tradition?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sounded faintly surprised. This was a tradition I had left with the Ancient Barbarian Tribe. I didn’t expect it to endure to this day.

“The Corpse-Driving Sect’s grand tournament has concluded. The victor, Huang Ming, just turned eighteen and is at the Basic Golden Core Stage. He has already been taken in as the sect leader’s final disciple. The runner-up, Zhao Po, also just turned eighteen and is at the Basic Golden Core Stage.”

Lu Yang lingered on this piece of news for a few extra seconds. Reaching the Basic Golden Core Stage at just eighteen must mean incredible talent. Even among the Five Great Immortal Sects, such cultivation speed is rare, surpassed only by me and Meng Jingzhou.

“Two geniuses... the Great Era is approaching,” Lu Yang remarked. Had these two been born in the golden age of ancient times, they might even have qualified to serve as stepping stones for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s rise.

“The Seven-Emotions Valley has developed a new curse. Those afflicted will hear the incessant buzzing of mosquitoes while sleeping or in seclusion. It is unavoidable even if one covers their ears, driving victims to become irascible.

“Seven-Emotions Valley—I remember they’re a first-class sect in Wilderness Province specializing in curses,” Lu Yang murmured. His knowledge of the Seven-Emotions Valley was limited.

“The White Paper-Hatted Man (real name unknown, real identity unknown) has a bounty of one million spirit stones. By splitting himself into two people, he feigned his own capture to claim the reward before departing carefreely. Wilderness Province’s authorities have since raised the bounty to two million spirit stones.

“The rising star of the barbeque world, One More Time Barbeque Shop, has thirty branches in Wilderness Province, and their business is thriving. According to the chain, they have a passion for barbecue and hope to spread its flavor across the entire province, with plans for setting up more stores within the province.

“The home of Corpse Drivers, Qingming Chain Inns... Why are there advertisements in this?” Lu Yang was slightly annoyed. I paid for intelligence, so why are there advertisements interspersed inside?

In fact, the information about One More Time Barbeque Shop was also an advertisement, but since Lu Yang took sixty percent of the profits, he let it slide.

“Why is there no intel on battles between Fusion cultivators?” Despite the dazzling assortment of information on Wilderness Province, Lu Yang hadn’t lost sight of his original goal to uncover clues about the walking corpse horde in Jianshi Village.

“Oh, I’ve found it. There really was one recorded fight between Fusion cultivators. It was two months ago.

“Let’s see what happened... Two Fusion cultivators had a falling out in their relationship and filed for divorce, coming to blows fighting over custody of their child.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Rubbing his temples in frustration, he began entertaining the possibility that the walking corpses had simply gotten lost.

1. “Yuanshan” translates to something like “distant mountain.” ☜

Chapter 408: Speedrunning Classic Tropes

Lu Yang had to admit that Wilderness Province lived up to its name. Its fierce and unrestrained local customs alone would take an outsider like me some time to get used to.

“Even the Luodi Merchant Guild has no intelligence on fights between Fusion cultivators. Looks like there really were none.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned that the yang energy stored in the walking corpses could sustain their activities for at most two months. Thus, Lu Yang had gathered all the intelligence on Wilderness Province from the past two months. However, aside from the one marital spat, there were no records of Fusion cultivators’ battles.

“Did it happen in secret, evading even the merchant guild’s intelligence network? Or did these walking corpses simply get lost?” Lu Yang would have suspected the former if he had not read those reports on Wilderness Province. But after reviewing all the information, he now suspected the latter.

“Whatever. For now, let’s focus on solving Old Meng’s problem first. According to the intel, the Seven-Emotions Valley specializes in the art of curses. Should I head there?”

He approached someone in the merchant guild. “Excuse me, do you know where the Seven-Emotions Valley is?”

As Lu Yang had just spent a fortune on their most detailed intelligence package, the merchant guild was naturally pleased to provide this minor information gratis. Moreover, this barely counted as intelligence. Any cultivator past a certain level would know the Seven-Emotions Valley’s location. The merchant guild directly handed Lu Yang a map with the Seven-Emotions Valley marked.

After leaving the merchant guild, Lu Yang heard a piercing shriek.

Following the sound, he saw a young ruffian recklessly galloping through the streets and attempting to abduct a commoner girl. His lackeys and servants cheered while onlookers seethed in silence. It seemed like this bully held considerable influence within the region. The young ruffian laughed uproariously as the girl wept.

“Seriously, this again?” Lu Yang sighed deeply. My romantic peach-blossom luck is getting a little out of hand.

Wait, could this be the repayment for saving Meng Jingzhou’s dog hide from the Immortal Fairy, which was an act of immeasurable virtue and merit?

Forget it. No matter the case, I should settle the situation in front of me first.

“Stop.” Despite Lu Yang’s soft voice, it was particularly conspicuous in such a situation, so everyone heard him.

Ignoring the passers-by’s stunned gazes, he quickly strode forward and helped the girl up.

“You've got quite the guts, outsider! Do you know who I—”

Before the young ruffian could finish, Lu Yang slapped him across the face without even blinking.

The young ruffian was about Lu Yang’s age; he was supposedly not weak with his cultivation at the Great Perfection Qi Training Stage.

Seeing their master get beaten, the lackeys rushed in with various weapons drawn.

Lu Yang waved his hand impatiently, summoning a gale that sent them all flying.

These lackeys were supposedly not weak with their cultivation at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

The crowd was dumbstruck that Lu Yang dared to hit the young ruffian.

“I’ve never seen this person before. Is he an outsider?”

“Definitely! Who in Yuanshan City would dare provoke those from the Gu Family? Especially their eldest young master!”

“Satisfying as it is, I’m afraid this person won’t leave this city alive.”

“To defeat even the Foundation Establishment servants so easily—just who is this young hero?”

“Golden Core Stage! He must be at the Golden Core Stage!”

The commoner girl gazed at Lu Yang with tender affection. “Savior.”

She was quite pretty and could be called a “little beauty.” Noticing the admiration in her eyes, Lu Yang suspected that her next words would be “This humble girl has nothing to repay you except myself.”

“The Gu Family is huge and dominates Yuanshan City. Savior, though your cultivation is extraordinary, going against the Gu Family is still dangerous. Please, flee while you can!”

“Haha, thinking of fleeing? You think you can still leave Yuanshan City alive after beating my son?!” A furious laughter reverberated across half a city as a fuming middle-aged cultivator arrived, glaring daggers at Lu Yang and gnashing his teeth.

“You—”

Lu Yang didn’t give him a chance to utter a second word, casually shooting out a sword ray that pinned the man to a wall.

Afterward, Lu Yang turned to the commoner girl. “Is this the Gu Family’s head?”

She nodded stiffly, stunned by how decisively Lu Yang acted and how powerful he was to have subdued an Advanced Golden Core cultivator in one move. “Family head Gu is fearsome, but what’s more fearsome is his father—”

Before she could finish, they heard another irate roar from afar.

“You dare harm my son and grandson—”

Following the Unbeatable Golden Core’s instructions, Lu Yang drew his Qingfeng Sword and executed the Slashing Word Mantra. Before the other party could finish speaking, he found himself pinned to the wall beside Family Head Gu.

A Basic Nascent Soul cultivator is worthy enough for me to employ my sword techniques.

Lu Yang asked, “Is there anyone else from the Gu Family?”

The commoner girl paused for a long while before stiffly nodding. “Yes, the Gu Family has an old ancestor at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.” She secretly observed Lu Yang. Finding not the slightest change in his expression, she mentally elevated her estimation of his cultivation level.

While she stood dumbfounded, Family Head Gu had secretly contacted their old ancestor for help.

“Young one, you’ve got quite the guts to bully our Gu Family. Even if my people were unreasonable in the first place, only I may discipline them. Why would we need—”

Lu Yang quietly took out the identity jade tablet at his waist.

“—you to step in, Fellow Daoist? I, Gu, thank you for disciplining these good-for-nothing descendants!”

The Gu Family’s old ancestor froze mid-air upon seeing the jade tablet. He then descended from the sky, cupped his fists, and bowed in gratitude.

It was true that Lu Yang couldn’t defeat the Divine Transfiguration-level old ancestor. But why do I need to fight him? Before the leviathan that is the Dao-Seeking Sect, a Divine Transfiguration old ancestor is nothing.

In fact, he wouldn’t even need an elder to intervene. Any senior brother or sister could help Lu Yang restore his dignity—such was the reputation of the Five Great Immortal Sects. It was enough to command reverence from the ancestral clans in these places.

Lu Yang feared neither beating up the young ones nor meeting the old ones.

“Did you hear what the Gu Family’s old ancestor just said? Dao-Seeking Sect? The one in the legends?!”

“It’s the one from the pingshu story, Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

“The leader of the Five Great Immortal Sects!”

The onlookers gasped in awe. No one had expected Lu Yang to have such an illustrious background.

The commoner girl also stared at Lu Yang in astonishment, the admiration in her eyes deepening.

“No need for thanks,” Lu Yang announced loudly. “But do rein in your descendants, Fellow Daoist Gu, lest they bring calamities upon you. After all, the Great Mission Hall in our Dao-Seeking Sect is frustrated over the lack of missions.” His words were for the Gu Family’s old ancestor and the surrounding civilians.

The Gu Family’s old ancestor naturally understood the underlying implication and broke into a cold sweat. He smiled obsequiously. “Of course, of course! Many thanks for your reminder, Fellow Daoist. After this, I’ll definitely tighten the supervision of my descendants. If such incidents happen again, they shall be punished by having their tendons ripped and bones extracted!”

The commoner girl curtsied sincerely. “This humble girl has nothing to repay you—”

“You can just repay me by working as hard as oxen and horses in your next life,” Lu Yang swiftly interjected.

Under everyone’s gaze, he departed Yuanshan City and took the same route he had come by.

“Let’s hope I won’t encounter something like this on the way back.” He felt that this entire trip had yielded little useful intelligence but plenty of incidents.

“Immortals, please bless and protect me... actually, never mind. Immortals’ blessings aren’t reliable. I should rely on myself.”

Chapter 409: When Three Travel Together, Each Has Hidden Motives

Perhaps because his romantic peach-blossom luck had finally run out, Lu Yang didn’t encounter noble young ladies being accosted on the road, female armed escorts getting robbed while delivering goods, or women hosting martial arts contests for marriage.

Marital martial arts contests were the most troublesome. The only option was avoidance. If Lu Yang participated and lost, the Unbeatable Golden Core wouldn’t let him off, and if he won, he would suddenly gain a wife he didn’t know.

No scenario would work out in my favor.

“Hmm, the sky’s cleared up already?”

When Lu Yang was approaching where the carriage was, he saw the mountainous region stretched before him under clear skies; the rain had finally stopped.

“Old Meng probably gave up on heading into the city.”

Lu Yang spotted four figures not far ahead, standing squarely on the only road back.

Quickening his pace, he realized it wasn’t four people, but three cultivators and a walking corpse.

Their argument was carried by the wind and into Lu Yang’s ears.

~~~

“I’ve told you! Every time the three of us try to pass by here, we get stopped by all kinds of incidents. This is a warning! Some great horror is up ahead. We can’t go further!” A delicate-looking cultivator exclaimed frantically, preventing his companions from advancing.

“Brother Ye, these are just coincidences. With how massive the world is, coincidences are possible. I’ve never heard of warnings like this,” a bronze-skinned man contended. He had short hair and looked like someone with a careless and straightforward personality. Turning his head to their third companion, he asked, “Brother Zhao, you’ve traveled extensively and witnessed many things. Have you ever seen anything like this?”

Brother Zhao had a well-proportioned build, though his complexion was pale, as if he was perpetually ill. His brows were tightly knitted. He seemed to have heard of something similar, but as soon as the words reached his mouth, they seemed to be forgotten again.

~~~

Lu Yang stepped past them without a word and proceeded ahead.

“Hey hey hey, this brother here! You can’t walk past up ahead!” The short-haired man tried to stop Lu Yang.

“Can’t walk past?”

“There seems to be something supernatural at work up ahead. Just moments ago, the three of us kept running into strange mishaps that prevented us from moving forward.”

The delicate-looking man chimed in. “Brother Wenren is right. When I wanted to proceed further, my cultivation technique malfunctioned. It took me an hour of meditating to recover.

“After that, we ran into a lost old man and escorted him home.

“Upon returning here, we realized we’d left something behind at his house, so we ran back to retrieve it.

“When we came back here again, several boulders rolled down from afar and blocked our path. By the time we moved them away, we finally sensed that something was amiss. It felt as if an invisible force was blocking our path ahead.”

Brother Zhao suddenly seemed to have recalled something. “I remember now!”

“What did you remember?” His other two companions pressed.

“I’ve heard the elders mention situations like this. When some experts gather to discuss the Dao or duel, they will often set up arrays beforehand to drive others away. That way, others won’t be able to proceed forward and will be forced to take detours. However, such occurrences are rare. After all, sparring in the mountains would require them to restore the landscapes once their battles concluded, which was too troublesome. It was more common for them to duel on open plains or in the skies.

“Experts are likely battling in the area ahead. Didn’t we see it just now? Dark clouds congregated, and lightning flashed across the sky, followed by thunder rolls. It must be experts borrowing the powers of heaven and earth in battle!” Brother Zhao grew more solemn as he spoke, convinced that his reasoning was perfectly logical.

The delicate-looking man and the short-haired man, aware of Brother Zhao’s extraordinary background, nodded in agreement.

“When experts fight, it’s best to steer clear if possible. Since we can’t go through the mountains, we’ll have to take the long way around.”

Lu Yang studied the trio for a long while before suddenly asking, “Which of you is a woman disguised as a man?”

At these words, Brother Ye, the delicate-looking man, had a flood of emotions flickering across his visage. Meeting Lu Yang’s unwavering gaze, he gave in. “How did you tell?”

“Brother Ye, you...” The other two stared at him in shock.

Brother Ye removed a jade pendant from his neck with a bitter smile. His Adam’s apple was smoothed away, and his originally delicate features became alluring, revealing large, limpid eyes. His hair lengthened to his waist, and his chest swelled beneath his robes.

Watching Brother Ye transform from a man into a woman, his companions gaped in astonishment.

The three hadn’t known each other long; they had met while roaming the jianghu. Believing it was safer to travel together and finding their temperaments compatible, they chose to team up.

Yet, after all they had been through, “Brother Ye” had been a woman all along?!

“Brother Ye, no wonder you never bathed with us, always insisted on separate rooms at inns, and blushed whenever we told bawdy jokes, even begging us to stop!

“Wait, does that mean the woman I saw bathing in the lake that night was also you?!”

Brother Wenren pieced things together. When they were camping in the wild, he had gone to relieve himself by the lake in the dead of the night. Under the moonlight, he saw a slender woman bathing, looking like an immortal fairy of the lake. Unfortunately, the dim light didn’t allow him to have a clear view of her face.

The next day, when he had recounted it with his companions, Brother Ye laughed it off and said he must have dreamed it.

“I lied,” Brother Ye—or rather, Young Miss Ye now—admitted with her cheeks flushed with shame. “I’m actually from the Ye Family of Liang Province.” Disguised as a man, she had journeyed from Liang Province to Wilderness Province, befriending these two along the way.

The Ye Family of Liang Province was a locally renowned ancestral clan. Among their ancestors were high-ranking regional governors and great cultivators.

“I got this jade pendant from my mother. She said that it never failed her when she wandered the jianghu disguised as a man and met my father. I have no idea how this senior brother managed to see through it today.”

Lu Yang simply smiled without answering, not wanting to betray Meng Jingzhou.

To Young Miss Ye, however, it looked like a mysterious smile.

Young Miss Ye sighed inwardly. As I thought, jianghu people are inscrutable and profound. Even a random passer-by could see through my disguise.

With her identity exposed, Young Miss Ye stopped dwelling on the matter and turned to Brother Wenren with a gaze full of tender affection. “Brother Wenren, I like you. Do you still remember when we encountered those plundering cultivators? You took that slash for me and saved my life! I’ve liked you ever since!”

Brother Wenren hadn’t expected this confession from his good brother and was at a loss for what to do. Fortunately, he steadied himself quickly and removed his thumb ring with a soft sigh.

His body underwent transformations: his arms became slender, his short hair cascaded past his shoulders, and the robes over his chest were stretched tight over newly curved fullness. Only his bronze complexion remained, giving him a healthy glow.

“I’m sorry. I’m also a woman disguised as a man.

“Do you remember me refusing your treatment and insisting on healing myself after taking that slash for you? This is why.”

Young Miss Ye, “...”

Heartbreak came so swiftly.

Lu Yang, Young Miss Ye, and Young Miss Wenren turned to the sickly Brother Zhao, their intentions almost written across their faces: it’s your turn.

Brother Zhao flew into a rage. “I’m a man!”

So, out of us three travel companions, I’m the only honest one!

Chapter 410: You’re the Same Lu Yang Who Dared to Beat Up Even the Judges?

Brother Zhao was a jianghu veteran. While Young Miss Ye and Young Miss Wenren were wandering the jianghu for the first time, he had done so for two to three years.

During their travels, his rich experience made him the de facto big brother of their trio. Yet, never in his wildest dreams had he imagined that out of “three brothers,” he would turn out to be the only man!

How am I supposed to show my face if word gets out?

Lu Yang patted Brother Zhao’s shoulder to console him.

Though Brother Zhao did not feel consoled.

My walking corpses are still best—at least, they won’t lie to me.

Young Miss Ye’s eyes reddened as she gazed at everyone with reluctance. “My family allowed me to leave home, but only on the condition that I never reveal my true gender. If I’m exposed, I must return immediately.”

Initially, she thought that even if her identity was exposed, confessing to Brother Wenren would make it worthwhile. If he accepted, she could have let him marry into the Ye Family and enjoy a life of luxury as a live-in son-in-law.

In hindsight, I had painted a picture that was too rosy. Not only has my identity been exposed, forcing me to return as agreed, but my heartfelt confession was also rejected on the spot.

Her cheeks burned red. Even if her family didn’t demand that she return, she was embarrassed to stay here any longer.

Young Miss Wenren wore a similar expression as she bid farewell with a downcast tone. “I’m from the Wenren Clan of Liang Province. My situation is roughly the same as Young Miss Ye’s. The clan elders assured me that this thumb ring is a spirit treasure of supreme quality and impossible to see through unless I remove it willingly. Now that I have, I have no choice but to return home.”

When Lu Yang asked which of them was a woman disguised as a man, her expression had also shifted, thinking he had seen through her. She had been about to remove her thumb ring to lift her disguise and confess to Brother Ye, only for him to beat her to it.

Not that the outcome would have been different.

Wenren Family of Liang Province? Lu Yang had heard snippets of information about this clan. They were a branch divided from the Barbarian Tribe, and they changed their surname from “Man” to “Wenren” when they migrated to Liang Province.

Those who have traveled near the Western Region would discover many people with bronze complexions there. If one seriously looked into it, Young Miss Wenren might even be related to Man Gu.

“You’re from the Wenren Family?” Young Miss Ye was surprised. As a fellow member of a Liang Province ancestral clan, she had naturally heard of the Wenren Family.

“Mmm, I’m Wenren Hui.”

“Shall we return together? For companionship?”

“Sure.”

“Shall I escort you two?” Though Brother Zhao had been deceived, he still carried himself with the bearing of a big brother.

“No need, no need.” The two women hastily declined. Having deceived him all this time, they couldn’t bring themselves to trouble him any further.

After seeing the two women off, only Lu Yang, Brother Zhao, and an unresponsive walking corpse remained.

“Right, I haven’t introduced myself yet. I’m Lu Yang of the Dao-Seeking Sect.” Lu Yang had just recovered from the astonishment of discovering the two women’s disguises.

Brother Zhao widened his eyes, staring at Lu Yang incredulously. “You’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect?!” I didn’t expect such an impressive background. No wonder he could see through the disguises that had eluded me.

“Wait, Lu Yang? The same Lu Yang who made a dazzling show of strength at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, crushed all challengers, seized first place, and dared to beat up even the judges?!” Brother Zhao was floored.

Every cultivator of the younger generation had heard of Lu Yang’s name. As someone from the Five Great Immortal Sects, he already drew plenty of attention. Add to that Lu Yang’s magnificent feat of fighting Foundation Establishment opponents as a Golden Core cultivator and beating up the judges, it was hard not to notice him.

Lu Yang had been cultivating recently and had not left the sect. Otherwise, he would have realized just how much the outside world was gossiping about him and Meng Jingzhou.

“Hold on, what do you mean by I dared to beat up even the judges? ...Though it seems like it’s not entirely wrong.” I had clearly challenged fellow prodigies from immortal sects! How did the rumors distort that into beating up the judges?

Who spread this rumor?! I’ve got to hand it to them!

“You may not have heard of me, Senior Brother Lu. I’m Zhao Po of the Corpse-Driving Sect,” Zhao Po humbly said. Though he was considered exceptional among the younger generation, he paled in comparison to Lu Yang.

“I’ve heard of you. Corpse-Driving Sect’s Number Two.”

Lu Yang recalled a mostly useless intelligence in the report he had purchased from the merchant guild. The Corpse-Driving Sect’s grand tournament has concluded. The victor, Huang Ming, just turned eighteen and is at the Basic Golden Core Stage. He has already been taken in as the sect leader’s final disciple. The runner-up, Zhao Po, also just turned eighteen and is at the Basic Golden Core Stage.

“Second place in the sect’s grand tournament,” Zhao Po corrected Lu Yang.

“More or less the same. Let’s go, my brother Meng Jingzhou is ahead. You probably have heard of him.” Lu Yang grinned, not expecting to run into someone from the Corpse-Driving Sect here. This saves me lots of trouble.

Zhao Po lit up. I didn’t expect a random passer-by to be the Lu Yang, and soon, I’ll meet the Meng Jingzhou, both of whom are currently in the spotlight.

Though my little team disbanded right after Lu Yang appeared.

“But aren’t there experts battling ahead? Can we pass?”

“What battle? That’s just Old Meng’s curse. All women will be kept away from him. That’s why you couldn’t advance!” Lu Yang’s grief twisted into laughter.
