Zhao Po was intimidated by the curse. “There’s such a curse? Is it from the Seven-Emotions Valley? That’s not right either. How would they dare target a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple?”

“It’s...complicated. We came to Wilderness Province to fix this problem.”

When the two arrived at the carriage, the rain had cleared, and Meng Jingzhou had cleared the path blocked by the mudslide. Now, he was happily enjoying his barbeque meal.

“Haha, Old Meng, I’m back! What an adventure this journey was! What’s that? You’re asking me what happened? Then I’ll have to tell you properly!” Lu Yang didn’t care whether Meng Jingzhou asked and launched into the tale of his journey.

“Let me tell you, it’s really a pity you couldn’t go! After I set off, I first ran into two noble young ladies being kidnapped. I played the hero rescuing the damsels in distress, and they wanted to repay me by promising themselves to me in marriage. Then, I met a heroic female armed escort who got ambushed by robbers, and I saved her too. She was extremely grateful and hinted that I could go to the armed escort agency to marry her. After that, I came across a martial arts contest for marriage. I must admit, the girl was quite the beauty.

“When I arrived at the nearest city, I encountered a young ruffian harassing a woman on the streets. How could I let that slide? I decisively stepped in and beat both the younger one and the older one, sorting out the entire family until they submitted to me obediently. The woman I saved even said that she had no way to repay me and wanted to offer herself in marriage too.

“Say, how could this journey have been so so so eventful? Don’t you agree, Old Meng?!” Lu Yang shook his head, looking like he wished for more.

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes were burning red with envy.

Zhao Po stood silently to the side, weighing whether he should spectate or intervene if a fight broke out.

I heard they’re both at the Basic Golden Core Stage, and so am I. Surely I can hold them back if it really comes to a fight...right?

Chapter 411: Looks Like the Seven-Emotions Valley’s Strength Is Not to Be Underestimated

“Why didn’t I encounter any of this?!” Meng Jingzhou lamented regretfully, convinced that he had missed out on tremendous fortuitous opportunities.

Damn Lu Yang, stealing my fortuitous opportunities! This grudge is irreconcilable!

“It’s all fate. Just accept it,” Lu Yang consoled.

“F*ck off!” Meng Jingzhou snapped. Why do all the good things happen to Lu Yang?

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had zero intention of fighting at all; Zhao Po had been worried for nothing.

“Who did you bring back?” Meng Jingzhou tilted his chin at Zhao Po.

Dreading another “Corpse-Driving Sect’s Number Two” quip from Lu Yang, Zhao Po hurriedly introduced himself. “I placed second in the Corpse-Driving Sect’s grand tournament. The name is Zhao Po. Basic Golden Core Stage.”

Meng Jingzhou was stunned. Zhao Po seems our age, or at most a year older. Yet with such talent, he’s only second in the Corpse-Driving Sect?

If Zhao Po comes to the Dao-Seeking Sect, he’d easily rank sixth.

“You’re only second in the Corpse-Driving Sect with your level?”

At the mention of this topic, Zhao Po chuckled bitterly. “I hate to admit it, but Senior Brother Huang Ming is indeed a bit stronger than me, and his combat instincts far outclass mine. Even if we fight again, I’d still lose. During that battle, I exhausted every trump card, yet he remained unfazed and showed no signs of weariness, looking like he was holding back other moves.

“Senior Brother Huang Ming has always been more outstanding than me. He was always far ahead on every mission outside. While others were still searching for clues, he’d already slain the mastermind.

“It's just that Senior Brother Huang Ming lost his parents at a young age and grew up an orphan. He's always been withdrawn and unwilling to interact with others.” Zhao Po shook his head regretfully. I’d hoped to exchange cultivation insights with Senior Brother Huang Ming, but unfortunately, he isn’t willing to talk to me, the runner-up.

“Now that the sect leader has taken him in as a disciple, I’m afraid meeting him will be even harder.”

“That strong?” Lu Yang elevated his evaluation of Huang Ming. He’d assumed that Huang Ming and Zhao Po were at a similar level. But hearing what he said, it sounds like there’s a massive gap in their abilities?

“Enough about me. I heard Senior Brother Meng is cursed and can’t get close to women?”

Meng Jingzhou pondered a moment. “Feels like I also couldn’t get close to women before the curse either.”

Zhao Po comforted him. “Don’t lose heart, Senior Brother Meng. As a sage once said: Those destined for greatness must first endure torment of their mind and spirit, toil of their muscles and bones, hunger of their body, and deprivation of their everything. Thwarting their every effort tempers their resolve and resilience, awakening abilities once impossible.”[1]

Meng Jingzhou chuckled, liking Zhao Po more by the second. “Well said, truly a prodigy from the Corpse-Driving Sect! You’re much better with words than this grandson Lu Yang! You’re my friend from now on! When you go to the imperial city next time and feel like you lack troubles, just drop my name—Meng Jingzhou!”

Zhao Po, “...”

Why do I feel like that last part sounds off? Did I mishear?

“To clarify, my curse prevents me from getting close to women. I heard that many cultivators in Wilderness Province excel in the curse arts, and since the Corpse-Driving Sect is a large sect in the province, we were planning to head to your esteemed sect and check if there is any solution to this curse.”

Zhao Po contemplated and earnestly replied, “In that case, I’d recommend Senior Brother Meng to go to the Seven-Emotions Valley.”

“Seven-Emotions Valley?” Like Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou’s knowledge of the Seven-Emotions Valley was simply its existence.

“Our sect specializes in orthodox Corpse-Driving Techniques, but when it comes to curses, we are far beneath the Seven-Emotions Valley’s level of mastery. Here in Wilderness Province, the Seven-Emotions Valley is the first suspect for any curse. However, they’re considered semi-secluded, so outsiders know little about them.”

Lu Yang nodded, confirming his idea. “Looks like the Seven-Emotions Valley’s strength isn’t to be underestimated. They are probably on par with your sect, right?”

Zhao Po was stunned. How did Senior Brother Lu know about this? Even I had learned it from the elders after winning second place in the sect’s grand tournament and rising in status.

“The weaker sects would have long been wiped out.” Zhao Po acknowledged Lu Yang’s point.

“Let’s head to the Seven-Emotions Valley. It’s close anyway.” Lu Yang referenced the map and calculated that they should reach in less than half a day based on the old horse’s speed.

“It’s right here.” Lu Yang pointed to the location on the map and showed the old horse, who snorted in acknowledgement.

Zhao Po was shocked by this scene. To him, the old horse was just another ordinary horse. Why does it seem to understand humans so well?

Perhaps this is a secret best left unasked. He wasn’t one to pry. It’s perfectly normal for cultivators to have secrets. When I sensed something amiss with Brother Ye and Brother Wenren during our travels, I didn’t ask—and thus unfolded the scene of two women disguised as men secretly in love with each other and bullying the honest person.

The three boarded the carriage, and Zhao Po made the walking corpse squat atop the carriage to scan the surroundings and intimidate robbers and rascals.

Corpse Drivers held an exalted status in Wilderness Province. When wanderers met their end in foreign lands, it fell to these Corpse Drivers to drive their corpses back to their hometown for a proper burial. Bandits and outlaws who spotted a walking corpse here would immediately realize there was a Corpse Driver inside the carriage and voluntarily abandon targeting them.

Inside the carriage, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou asked some questions related to Corpse-Driving Techniques.

“I’ve long found it strange. Walking corpses lack spirit intelligence and are essentially objects. Why not transport them in storage rings instead of staying at inns?”

“Factually speaking, walking corpses are indeed objects that can be placed in storage rings. However, we Corpse Drivers believe that walking corpses possess life, just in a state imperceptible to cultivators. Since those are lives, we must accord them the same treatment as we would with other living beings—letting them eat, live, and travel with us, and even using the word ‘please’ when asking them to battle.” Zhao Po smiled bitterly. “It’s precisely because of our unique perspective on life and death that rumors in the outside world spread, claiming that the founder of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed came from our Corpse-Driving Sect.”

Zhao Po explained various aspects of Corpse Drivers to the two, which were far more authentic than others could share.

In less than half a day, the trio and one corpse successfully arrived at the Seven-Emotions Valley.

“I have a friend in the Seven-Emotions Valley who’s a true lineage disciple and extremely adept at removing curses. When I was cursed, I sought my friend for help.

“Senior Brother Meng, what level is your curse? If it’s anything at the Nascent Soul level or below, my friend can lift it. If it’s at the Divine Transfiguration level, there’s still a chance, and even if it can’t be removed, it can be alleviated.”

Meng Jingzhou hesitated before saying, “A conservative estimate would be at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation level.” After all, I’d evenly split the curse with Sect Leader Qiu, which reduced its potency.

Zhao Po leaned back slightly, his expression becoming solemn with respect. When I made enemies while traveling, they were usually old ancestors at the Golden Core Stage. The probability of bumping into Nascent Soul-level old monsters was already slim, much less Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

Should I say ‘as expected of a peerless prodigy from the Dao-Seeking Sect?’ Even the curse he’s afflicted with is at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation level.

What on earth had he done to get hit by a curse of this level?

Even slapping the Seven-Emotions Valley’s leader twice probably wouldn’t warrant a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation-level curse.

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, This barely scratches the surface. For us brothers, the enemies we make start at the Fusion Stage—anything below that isn’t worth our attention.

1. This is adapted from a quote from Gaozi by Mengzi (Mencius). ☜

Chapter 412: Foolish Old Man Yugong Moved Mountains to Fill the Sea and Create New Land

“That should be the Seven-Emotions Valley up ahead. Let’s stop here first. The two of us will go in and bring someone over to check Old Meng’s condition.” Lu Yang was worried that proceeding further might trigger all kinds of mishaps to block them from moving forward.

I don’t wish to experience a landslide and eating dirt with Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth a second time.

Knowing that Lu Yang made sense, Meng Jingzhou could only seethe silently as he let them alight from the carriage, while he remained behind to keep the old horse company.

~~~

After trekking two to three li, the two humans and one corpse arrived at a canyon that appeared cleaved by a heavenly sword. Its walls were steep and smooth, devoid of any protrusions or indentations. If this was nature’s fine handiwork, then its chisel was far too divine.

Noticing Lu Yang scrutinizing the canyon, Zhao Po explained, “The Seven-Emotions Valley wasn’t always named so—it used to be called the ‘Seven-Emotions Sect.’ One sect leader found the term ‘sect’ too commonplace in the Central Continent, making their name inconspicuous. Hence, the Seven-Emotions Sect invited an expert in the Sword Dao to cleave the plains with one strike, bifurcating it into this canyon. With that, they rebranded themselves as the ‘Seven-Emotions Valley’ and even duly registered the name change with the imperial court.”

“I didn’t know such a method existed. This is eye-opening. They’re pretty by-the-book, knowing to formally register the name change...” Mid-sentence, Lu Yang jolted in realization. “Wait, doesn’t the imperial court mandate that cultivators restore altered terrain? Shouldn’t this situation with the Seven-Emotions Valley require approval?”

“Correct. That’s why the Seven-Emotions Valley remains an unauthorized construction to this day.”

Lu Yang mused, This is my first damned time hearing that a canyon is considered an “unauthorized construction.” A true hallmark of the cultivation world.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grumbled in his mental space. “Your Great Xia rules are so stringent in this aspect. Back in ancient times, we didn’t have these many tedious regulations. We were free to alter terrains as we liked.

“I recall one family living in the mountains for generations. It was always inconvenient for them to travel out as two big mountains blocked their path, and they were forced to take lengthy detours to reach the outside world.

“That family had a child who was resolved to move those two mountains at their door. Some people jeered at him, saying ‘How could a young weakling like you, who can’t even lift a rock, possibly move two mountains?’

“That child replied, ‘Even if I can’t do it now, there’s still the future. I can cultivate until the Qi Training Stage, and if it doesn’t work, then to the Foundation Establishment Stage, and if it doesn’t work, then to the Golden Core Stage, and if it still doesn’t work, then to the Nascent Soul Stage. With infinite cultivation realms, I’ll surely reach a realm where I can move the mountains one day!’

“The child set out to train under a master, and by the time he returned, he was already an old man. Those who knew him called him Yugong—the ‘Foolish Old Man.’ With his heaven-shaking and earth-shattering cultivation, he unleashed Heaven-Earth Manifestation and moved Mount Taihang and Mount Wangwu away from his house, hurling them into the sea.

“From then on, the Foolish Old Man Yugong helped other people staying in the mountains to move the mountains away from their doorstep, and dumped them into the ocean.

“Through his tireless efforts in helping others relocate mountains, the vast oceans gradually became filled with mountains over time.

“The tale of the Foolish Old Man Yugong moving mountains to fill the sea and create new land has morphed into the idiom ‘Foolish Old Man filled the sea.’[ref]If you find the idiom familiar, it’s because it’s adapted from the idiom ‘Foolish Old Man moved the mountains.”[/red] It describes how one must persevere in their cultivation to overcome any obstacle.”

Lu Yang rubbed his temples painfully, feeling that his memories were in disarray.

However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t finished with her story. “You probably know that seawater cannot disappear but can only be relocated. As Yugong filled the ocean, the water overflowed and caused catastrophic floods.

“Fortunately, the Nine-Layers Immortal had already created Xirang Soil, which expands upon contact with water. He used it to block the deluge, preventing widespread disaster. This incident became known as ‘an immortal’s flood-taming’ by later generations.”

Lu Yang’s senses returned to the present, and only then did he notice the crowd size and the long queue stretched before the Seven-Emotions Valley’s entrance. At this rate, when will it be our turn?

“What’s going on here? Did all these people get afflicted by the Seven-Emotions Valley’s curses?” Are the Seven-Emotions Valley’s curses transmitted airborne now? Is that why there are so many victims?

“Not exactly. At least half of the people in line were cursed by others and have come here seeking help. To hone their disciples’ curse-breaking abilities, the Seven-Emotions Valley stations disciples at the canyon entrance to hold consultations and remove curses on the spot.

“Don’t let the crowd fool you. These are mostly minor curses: toothaches, gout—that sort of thing.

“That said, queuing is pointless for us. These disciples holding consultations can barely handle Foundation Establishment-level curses. Senior Brother Meng would only have a chance of fixing his curse with the valley leader’s intervention.”

Suddenly, someone in the queue transmitted their voice to Lu Yang and Zhao Po. “Young Brothers! Here to remove your curses? I can give you my spot. You just have to pretend you’re my relatives. I'm only asking for five hundred spirit stones! Deal or not?”

Following the voice, Lu Yang’s eyes twitched when he saw the person who had transmitted an auditory message to them and told them to cut the queue.

It’s that white paper-hatted man who pretended to be the innkeeper!

The fact that he dares to appear here openly suggests that he has absolute confidence in escaping even if he gets discovered.

Lu Yang strode over, a smirk playing on his lips. “Still remember me?”

The white paper-hatted man studied Lu Yang’s face and seemed to be struck with a realization. “I remember now! You were that guest at my inn!”

Lu Yang refuted inwardly, That was clearly an abandoned inn. Since when did it become yours?”

The man was baffled. “Why don’t I see your brother and that old horse with you?”

Lu Yang’s heart tightened. Did this man deliberately mention the old horse because he managed to discern that it’s extraordinary?

“Immortal Fairy, what’s this man’s cultivation?”

“Hard to tell. This is just a clone, and I can’t ascertain his specific cultivation. He’s probably cultivating a spell similar to Myriad-Forms Body Transformation, which lets him split himself into myriad copies to train his mental strength.

“Consider me unlucky. I’m leaving.” The white paper-hatted man vanished on the spot. Despite his low cultivation, he has a dragon-horse as his mount and possesses terrifyingly solid foundations—a clear sign of his complicated background.

Although I haven’t seen the other one before, the walking corpse following him is refined with the Corpse-Driving Sect’s methods, which implies that the other person is from the Corpse-Driving Sect.

With the mysterious Lu Yang and Corpse-Driving Sect’s disciple Zhao Po, they could easily bring trouble upon him. Best to escape first.

The white paper-hatted man performed his escape technique right before Lu Yang, but the latter still couldn’t make out how the man had fled.

Zhao Po also recognized the man. “Is that the white paper-hatted man from the wanted posters?”

“You’ve heard of him too?”

“Yes, I have. Back when we were traveling the jianghu, we brothers...and sisters wanted to hunt him for the bounty, but we could never track him down.” Zhao Po was about to make a move and capture the man, but when he noticed Lu Yang’s solemn demeanor, he realized the other party was far more complicated than he had assumed, so he held himself back from acting on impulse.

Chapter 413: Seven-Emotions Valley’s Businesses

The white paper-hatted man fled without a trace. Knowing this was no ordinary foe they could capture, both Lu Yang and Zhao Po didn’t take it to heart.

Zhao Po took out a small gong and struck it gently, producing a melodious chime. “This is how I contact my friend. If she’s in the valley, she’ll come out to meet us shortly.”

Before long, a slender woman walked out from the Seven-Emotions Valley. Spotting Zhao Po, her eyes brightened momentarily before she expertly concealed her delight, adopting a slightly disdainful tone. “What curse have you fallen victim to this time?”

Unbothered by her attitude, Zhao Po smiled and made introductions. “This is my new friend, Lu Yang from the Dao-Seeking Sect. He would like to ask for the valley leader’s help.

“This is Luo Yu, a true lineage disciple of the Seven-Emotions Valley. Her shifu is the valley master.”

“Lu Yang?!” Luo Yu was astonished to hear Lu Yang’s name. “The same Lu Yang who seized first place at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, then proceeded to beat up the judges for good measure?”

Lu Yang thought, With my numerous strengths, I don’t need to become famous in this manner...

“A friend of mine is suffering from a curse which is hard to speak of. It’s extremely difficult to remove, so we’d like to request the valley leader’s assistance.”

Luo Yu looked at Lu Yang with pity in her eyes. Yet another curse victim claiming it’s a “friend.”

“Shifu will emerge from seclusion soon. But I can’t be sure whether she’ll agree to lift your curse. Come in first.”

“It’s not me. It’s my friend,” Lu Yang corrected.

“Don’t worry, I understand.”

Following Luo Yu through the array’s entrance, they entered Seven-Emotions Valley.

Luo Yu suddenly asked, “By the way, is there someone named Xie Shanren in the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Yes, that’s our Fourth Elder. Is there a problem?”

Fourth Elder rarely left the sect, and the outside world wasn’t aware of his name.

“There is a small problem. When my shifu was young, she liked a man named Xie Shanren. The two had met by chance, and she fell in love at first sight. They often sat together, discussing the Dao and conversing joyfully for hours. My shifu even taught him curse-breaking techniques to prove her feelings and devotion. Yet in the end, Xie Shanren didn’t accept my shifu’s affections, cast her aside, and left Wilderness Province to return to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Based on how my shifu mentions him all year around, I can see she hasn’t let him go. As for whether it’s love or love turned into hatred, I’m not certain.”

Lu Yang broke into a cold sweat. No wonder Fourth Elder didn’t direct us to Seven-Emotions Valley but instead recommended us the Corpse-Driving Sect, despite the Seven-Emotions Valley’s expertise in curses. So, this is the reason.

But I have already stepped into Seven-Emotions Valley. Leaving now would be disrespectful. I hope Lord Valley Leader will be magnanimous and not take offense with a little Dao-Seeking Sect disciple like myself.

Lu Yang felt that he had made too many sacrifices to solve Meng Jingzhou’s curse. Even a father couldn’t have done more than this.

“Do friends like to be each other’s parents?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked Lu Yang, seemingly reminded of something.

“I can’t say it’s all of them, but some do.”

“I see.”

“Did you think of something, Immortal Fairy?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, revealing a guileless smile. “When I first cooked for the Qilin Immortal, he called me ‘Mother.’ So, it was because he considered me a friend! Looks like having meals together really does strengthen bonds.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s smile was much more pleasing than Yun Zhi’s icy countenance, but Lu Yang knew better than to be fooled by her innocent smile.

“Could you elaborate on that occasion?”

“After I challenged beyond my level and fought the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal, I felt bad about it, so I invited them for a meal. Initially, they were wary of me, thinking I wanted to poison them. But later, when they witnessed my smooth cooking process, which had no signs of adding poison, they felt reassured to dig in.

“The Qilin Immortal took one bite, cried ‘Mother,’ and passed out—probably because he was too weak to handle the nourishment.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal passed out too.

“Since the Qilin Immortal was born from the convergence of heaven and earth’s fortune and has no parents, he must have hallucinated me as his mother.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. The Qilin Immortal is also a pitiful person.

Lu Yang suspected the Qilin Immortal might have been trying to yell ‘motherf*cking poison’ but fell unconscious after just uttering the first word, which resulted in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s misunderstanding.

Though later generations had a hard time appraising the young immortals’ strength, Lu Yang had his own method. Since the Qilin Immortal could still say a word before collapsing while the Heaven Mandate Immortal couldn’t even speak, the former’s cultivation is likely superior.

In the real world, the three were traversing the Seven-Emotions Valley, and Lu Yang observed many visitors seeking help to break their curses. These were all complex curses that the disciples holding consultations couldn’t solve.

“Curse Master, whenever I meditate at night, I hear mosquitoes buzzing beside my ears and feel unbearable itchiness. I heard you’ve developed a new curse with these effects. Have I been afflicted with such a curse?”

“Fellow Daoist, it’s true that we Seven-Emotions Valley developed this curse, but I detect no indications of curses on you. The visible mosquito bites are probably due to actual mosquitoes around you.”

“Impossible! You must have cursed me!”

The Seven-Emotions Valley disciple sighed softly. The cost of creating that curse is exorbitant. With how low your cultivation is, why would anyone waste it on cursing you?

“Never mind. Place this item beside you during your seclusion, and there will no longer be any ‘curse.’”

“What is this?”

“Mosquito-repellent incense. Three hundred spirit stones per coil.”

~~~

“Curse Master, all my life, no female cultivator has ever liked me. Every time I confess, I get rejected, without exception. My peers of the same age are already married, while I don’t even have a girlfriend. Am I cursed?”

“Fellow Daoist, your situation isn’t due to a curse. Your charisma isn’t in question—only your spirit stones. We Seven-Emotions Valley offer lending services. Would you want to borrow spirit stones from us? The annual interest rate is just twenty percent.”

~~~

“Curse Master, after killing someone, vivid images of their bloody final moments haunt me. They scream and curse me to never be at peace. Now, I even have nightmares of them bleeding and crawling toward me, demanding my life. I’m too scared to sleep.

“Recently, I’ve been getting chills down my spine, as if someone’s following me. But when I turn around, nothing’s there.

“When I was in seclusion, eerie laughter would ring in my ears, as if it was mocking my pathetic state. I scurried away in panic, but the voice kept echoing in my ears.

“Sometimes, a red figure would even appear in my vision, only to vanish again when I rub my eyes to take a closer look.

“Have I been cursed?”

The Seven-Emotions Valley disciple studied the man’s darkened forehead, puffy eyes, and panicked gaze before nodding lightly. It’s a rare case of a genuine curse. “You’re indeed cursed, and it’s even the Wrongful Death Curse, one of the toughest curses to lift.

“Is there a way to solve it?”

“Of course. There is no curse our Seven-Emotions Valley can’t remove. However, this kind of curse is too difficult for me to remove. Hold on a bit, let me get my senior brother to help.”

Not long after, the disciple called his senior brother over and pointed at the other party. “Senior Brother, that’s the killer right there! I couldn’t take him down alone, so let’s work together to haul him to the authorities!”

Chapter 414: How Could I Not Know Whether Someone Likes Me?

Lu Yang retracted his gaze. The Seven-Emotions Valley’s range of businesses is really wide—from curse removal to selling mosquito-repellent incense, lending services, and apprehending murderers. The variety had broadened his horizons.

Luo Yu explained, “That’s because we had no choice. Most people can’t distinguish between ordinary troubles and actual curses. They all come rushing here, shouting about being cursed and asking us to help.

“We feel bad turning them away after their long journey, so we find alternative ways to solve the problem. The loan service, for instance, was recently established.

“Previously, someone came looking for us and claimed he was short on money, but every merchant guild rejected his loan applications, responding that he already had outstanding debts and couldn’t borrow until he paid back in full. He asked us whether he was afflicted with a curse that made him sleepwalk to the merchant guild to take loans.

“After multiple verifications confirmed no curse, we checked the laws and discovered that anything above thirty-six percent annual interest constitutes usury. Hence, we had no choice but to offer him a loan at exactly thirty-six percent.

“And that was how our loan services began.

Lu Yang, “...”

Had no choice, huh?

“Let’s not talk about ordinary people; even those with some understanding of curses struggle to differentiate. Zhao Po is a perfect example. As a disciple of the Corpse-Driving Sect at the Basic Golden Core Stage, he often can’t discriminate between curses and ordinary phenomena.” Luo Yu rolled her eyes at Zhao Po, who let out a sheepish chuckle.

Amused, Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message to Zhao Po. “Does Junior Sister Luo like you?”

“Impossible! That’s because you don’t know what she’d done to me.

“Once after departing Seven-Emotions Valley, I felt restless and constantly thought of Luo Yu to the point of losing appetite and sleep, so I went to look for her and described my symptoms, asking if she had planted a curse on me.

“She said yes.

“When I was recounting my situation to her, she blushed and stomped her foot upon admitting that she had planted a curse on me. I bet she was embarrassed and furious that I uncovered her curse scheme,” Zhao Po declared confidently. “To think I treated her as a friend! Yet she did that to me! She even refused to lift the curse when I told her to!”

“Are you sure it wasn’t because she likes you?”

Zhao Po waved his hand, his smile radiating conviction. “What are you talking about? I’ve roamed the jianghu for two to three years; I’m a seasoned old jianghu person. How could I not know whether someone likes me?”

Inside Lu Yang’s mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded vigorously. “What an incorrigible lass! This boy is already silly, yet she still cursed him! You never know what lies underneath a person’s appearance!”

Lu Yang, “...”

You two make me doubt my own judgment.

“How did you and Junior Sister Luo get to know each other?”

“That was a year ago, when I just reached the Foundation Establishment Stage. I heard about a large snake terrorizing a cold pond, so I headed there to exterminate it. Coincidentally, Luo Yu was also searching for that snake, though she wanted to kill it for its gallbladder to be used as a medium for creating curses. We hit it off right away and decided to join forces, slaying it after a fierce battle.

“Upon death, the snake’s belly exploded and released a poisonous mist of love poison that enveloped us.

“Fortunately, I was well prepared and had us consume detoxification pills beforehand, so we were unscathed.”

The group traversed a long corridor to a sealed stone door, where the valley leader was in seclusion.

“Based on experience, Shifu’s seclusion should have ended.”

“What experience? Does the valley leader have a fixed schedule for seclusion?”

“No, it’s just that whenever Shifu claims to be in seclusion, she’s actually slacking off in her cave abode to avoid handling sect affairs. If anything requires her attention, we can just look for her directly; it doesn’t matter whether she’s in seclusion.”

Luo Yu knocked on the stone door.

“Shifu, you have guests.”

An ethereal voice replied, “I’m in seclusion.”

“They’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

As soon as the words left her mouth, the three felt their visions blur as a fragrance assaulted their nostrils. A female cultivator wearing a white veil appeared before them, though her veil was see-through; Lu Yang could see a peerlessly beautiful woman behind the veil.

“Shifu, your seclusion is over?” Luo Yu covered her mouth as she giggled.

“My seclusion is over.”

The valley leader was dressed in white and carried an elegant demeanor with an air of steadiness. She sized up Zhao Po and Lu Yang, swiftly ruling out the former. “I can’t tell what golden core you’ve formed. Are you the Dao-Seeking Sect disciple?”

Lu Yang cupped his fists and bowed respectfully. “Greetings, Valley Leader. I am Lu Yang from the Dao-Seeking Sect, disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

“So you’re the old Taciturn scoundrel’s disciple. You look more pleasing than him. You may call me Valley Leader Shuang. Did Xie Shanren send you?”

Despite her calm tone, Lu Yang sensed murderous undercurrents. However, he didn’t have a clear picture of the situation, so he could only brace himself. “I was en route to the Corpse-Driving Sect when I heard of the Seven-Emotions Valley's reputation and came to visit you.”

“Corpse-Driving Sect? Why were you looking for them? That old Taciturn scoundrel died, and you’re planning to refine him into a walking corpse?”

“I have a friend who suffers from a curse that is extremely hard to break, so Fourth Elder recommended that we head to the Corpse-Driving Sect to solve this problem.”

“Hand it over.” Valley Leader Shuang suddenly extended her hand.

“What?” Lu Yang was bewildered.

“Since Xie Shanren told you to visit the Corpse-Driving Sect, he would have written a recommendation letter to prove your identities. The letter would have also described your friend’s curse. Let me take a look.”

Lu Yang retrieved Fourth Elder’s recommendation letter from his identity jade tablet and passed it to her with both hands.

With a single thought, the valley leader made the letter float into the air and open itself. She silently read the contents and revealed an intrigued look, mumbling to herself, “A curse produced from karmic backlash... This curse is something I’ve never seen before... Interesting...”

However, as she read further, her brows knit tightly, and her expression changed, looking like she was angry. With a cold snort, she threw the letter to the ground.

Lu Yang felt a sinking feeling in his gut and discreetly peeked at the letter’s contents. Fourth Elder is truly a Confucian cultivator. His handwriting is so nice. It exudes fairness and poise, making it comfortable to look at.

The letter’s content was fairly ordinary—it confirmed his and Meng Jingzhou’s identities to the Corpse-Driving Sect and explained how the curse came about and what it did.

Except the final line.

It wrote: Remember, DO NOT advise Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to seek help from the Seven-Emotions Valley. If they absolutely must go, avoid the she-devil Shuang Feiyan at all costs!

Lu Yang, “...”

Can I still walk out of Seven-Emotions Valley alive today?

Chapter 415: Fourth Elder and Seven-Emotions Valley Leader’s Past

Shuang Feiyan, Valley Leader of Seven-Emotions Valley, and a top-tier curse master, was one of the few people in Wilderness Province who must never be provoked. She possessed multifarious strange curses which were insidious and unavoidable. Whoever crossed her had to be prepared to face every curse imaginable.

A few centuries ago, a sect had secretly insulted Shuang Feiyan. When she learned of it, she swapped the genders of every member, only allowing them to return to normal after half a year. To this day, that sect remained a laughing stock across Wilderness Province.

Lu Yang didn’t know Shuang Feiyan’s stories, but even his butt could figure out that he must absolutely not provoke a curse master. I may be knowledgeable about dark and embarrassing ancient secrets, especially those regarding the immortals, and I’ll surely shoulder great responsibilities in the future, but that doesn’t mean that I have to face the wrath of a top-tier curse master right now.

Who could withstand that?

“Don’t be scared! With me here, I guarantee no curse can hurt you!” Inside his mental space, the source of curses herself declared with conviction.

Lu Yang panicked even more.

Zhao Po appeared equally nervous. Unlike Lu Yang, he knew what Shuang Feiyan was capable of. She’s the kind of horror that can make children cry at night. Even if the Corpse-Driving Sect and Seven-Emotions Valley have ties, whether their relationship matters depends on Valley Leader Shuang’s mood.

Fortunately, Valley Leader Shuang didn’t intend to take her anger out on juniors. Her expression shifted several times before she finally sighed heavily.

“I was about your age when I first met Shanren. That day, Shanren was passing by Cang Mountain when he heard cries for help. Mountain bandits were causing trouble. He stepped forward to save everyone, and that’s how we met.”

Lu Yang nodded inwardly. A classic tale where the hero saves the damsel in distress. Fourth Elder sure is lucky with the ladies.

“As the boss of the mountain bandits, when I saw Shanren’s elegant demeanor and refined speech, I could tell that he was from a big sect or clan. Thus, I captured him to be my bandit husband.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does it not sound quite right?

“I was a bandit who only robbed the rich to help the poor. It was mainly because I found there were too many mountain bandits in Wilderness Province to wipe out. So I figured, why not become one myself? If I expand my influence until there’s no more room for the other bandits, wouldn’t the bandits be completely gone?

“But I digress. After capturing Shanren, I wanted to marry him. However, he’d rather die than consent, so I had no choice but to give up for the time being.”

Lu Yang mused, I’ve heard about Wilderness Province’s bride-kidnapping customs, but I didn’t expect myself to hear about it firsthand today.

“I didn’t give up on Shanren entirely. His cultivation wasn’t weaker than mine, and I had only caught him by surprise. To prevent him from escaping, I planted a curse on him.

“Knowing he couldn’t break the curse for a while, Shanren stayed by my side obediently. When I relayed my meticulously crafted bandit-eradication plan to him, he agreed it was sound. And thus, he followed me to rob the rich to help the poor together, and we earned a mighty reputation for ourselves. The jianghu called us the Bandit Couple!

“Of course, during that period of time, he kept trying to escape and undo the curse, but he never succeeded.

“This persistent personality of Shanren was what I liked about him.”

Lu Yang realized that this was how Fourth Elder had built his foundations in curse-breaking techniques. No wonder Fourth Elder only knows how to remove curses but not cast them. It’s because he was on the receiving end.

“Cang Mountain was a good place. Shanren and I captured many cultivators who had made their name in their youth, such as the current sect leader of the Corpse-Driving Sect and the chieftain of the Barbarian Tribe. After hearing my plan, they found it a good idea, so they swore a blood oath, joined my bandit stronghold, and honored me as Big Sis Boss!

“With help from the three of them, we Cang Mountain bandits spread our influence rapidly, and surrounding bandits had to submit to us. I gave defeated bandits two choices: be refined into walking corpses or be planted with my curses. They were all wise to choose the latter and became my subordinates.

“Just like that, we gradually expanded our influence, and dozens of mountains were eventually under our control.

“In the end, we ruled nearly half of Wilderness Province’s forces. Ask anyone in the jianghu—who hadn’t heard of the Cang Mountain Four Dragons?

“Back then, the leader of the biggest bandit faction was Zhen Shanhu.[1] When he saw how fast our influence was expanding, he preemptively attacked to crush us before we grew stronger with fully-fledged wings.

“Zhen Shanhu was at the Apex Nascent Soul Stage, and none of us was his match in a one-on-one fight. But together, the four of us could defeat him!

“After Zhen Shanhu lost, he fled in disgrace and spouted threats, mentioning something about having a Fusion rogue expert backing him and that offending him was equivalent to offending that expert, telling us to wait for death. It was something along those lines, though I can’t remember the specifics.

“Obviously, we knew we stood no chance against a Fusion cultivator. We had no choice but to call in our elders.

“When that rogue Fusion cultivator appeared and prepared to show off and intimidate us, the then-Valley Leader, First Elder of the Corpse-Driving Sect, and First Elder of the Barbarian Tribe all showed up.

“He was so scared that he turned on his heel and fled, but no matter how fast he ran, how could he possibly outpace our elders? He was merely at the Basic Fusion Stage, while our elders were all at the Advanced Fusion Stage. Besides, our elders had already set up an inescapable net, just waiting for him to walk into the trap himself.”

Lu Yang could imagine the despair in that situation. He was just a Basic Fusion cultivator trying to help his subordinate eliminate some rivals when suddenly, big shots backing them emerged one after another.

“That rogue Fusion cultivator’s escape techniques were impressive. He knew that getting caught by us meant certain death, so he burned his essence blood to escape from the gigantic net we’d cast.

“Right then, a child blocked his escape route. It was your grand-shifu, the then-sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Among our elders, his combat prowess ranked the highest. Once he made his move, that rogue Fusion cultivator wouldn’t be able to escape even if he burned every last bit of his life force.

“From then on, we unified all bandit forces across Wilderness Province. Afterward, our respective elders dragged us back for disciplinary confinement.

“Originally, Shanren was supposed to be taken back to be grounded too, but your grand-shifu said that Reflection Confinement Cliff had no more space, so he locked me and Shanren together in Seven-Emotions Valley’s confinement chamber instead.

Lu Yang had heard of Reflection Confinement Cliff before. It was the Dao-Seeking Sect’s designated area for confining oneself and reflecting on one’s mistakes. However, I’ve always been an obedient and well-behaved kid and have never been punished, so I didn’t have to go to such a place.

Come to think of it, Big Senior Sister had once tried to confine Shifu there for neglecting his cultivation, but unfortunately, his cultivation was too high, and since he often went there, locking him up there was useless. That was why she ended up confining Shifu right at his home.

“Who was in Reflection Confinement Cliff then?” Lu Yang asked.

“Your shifu and the other eight. Apparently, your shifu had taken his seven senior brothers and sisters to wreak havoc in the imperial capital, teaching the scions of nobles a lesson and making their lives miserable. If you ever visit the imperial capital, you best not say that you’re the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Others rely on their elders to back them up, but why do my elders only make enemies for me?

1. His name translates literally to “suppress the tiger in the mountain.” ☜

Chapter 416: Valley Leader Shuang: Curses Are Useless on Me

It wasn’t Lu Yang’s first time hearing of the Dao-Seeking Nine’s reputation. Their name served as a reminder that being a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect was a double-edged sword. It could strike fear into weaker cultivators—those at the Divine Transfiguration or Void Refinement stages—but when facing Fusion-stage experts with ties to major factions, odds were they had crossed paths with the Dao-Seeking Nine before. And in eighty percent of those cases, it meant a grudge.

And if he went to the imperial capital, that eighty percent would likely become a hundred percent.

At least Meng Jingzhou has the Meng Family backing him in the imperial capital, so he should be safe.

On the contrary, with the Taciturn Daoist Priest as my shifu and Meng Jingzhou as my good brother, visiting the capital might as well be a trip to the underworld.

As the heart of the Central Continent, the imperial capital was the culmination of the Great Xia Dynasty’s one hundred thousand years and the world’s current most formidable cultivator city. Aside from the people of the Central Continent, even those from the Demon Region, the Golden Buddhist Kingdom, and the sea tribes yearned to visit and admire the scenery of the imperial capital.

Only Lu Yang didn’t want to go there.

He seemed to be reminded of something and counted on his fingers. “Why do I feel like I have so many enemies? I know the Four Ancient Immortals’ dark embarrassing histories, so they’ll definitely not spare me, and Shifu’s enemies will all become mine, which is to say that both ancient and modern experts have a grudge with me?!

“That shouldn’t be the case though. I joined the world’s strongest sect, became the sect leader’s youngest disciple, and have the most powerful ancient immortal inside me. Shouldn’t I be all-powerful, with no gods or buddhas standing in my way, surrounded by beauties, hugging one to the left and one to the right, and living the dream of having multiple partners? Why do I end up with only the downsides?” Lu Yang was grateful that his fate profile was tough enough to block so many perils.

“After we were grounded, my shifu sealed my and Shanren’s powers. Trapped in the confinement chamber, we could only see each other through the small iron-grated window. During our confinement, we discussed the Dao; I explained the principles of curses, and he explained the quotes of sages, leading to mutual improvement.”

Lu Yang wondered, Are you sure you two were even having the same conversation?

Valley Leader Shuang’s tone had softened. Aware of how troubles stemmed from words, Lu Yang wisely held his tongue.

Wrapping up her story, Valley Leader Shuang sighed. “Even until the end, Shanren didn’t accept my feelings for him. After I reached the Fusion Stage, I went into seclusion and researched curses to make him love me unwaveringly. Unfortunately, he never visited me.”

Lu Yang shuddered. I’ve long heard that studying the texts of sages can avoid calamities. It’s indeed true.

“Very well, since I’m fated with the Dao-Seeking Sect, I’ll help you.”

Before Lu Yang could be happy for Meng Jingzhou, he heard Valley Leader Shuang add, “However, judging by the contents of Shanren’s letter, your companion’s curse is of a very high level and exceeds my capabilities. Moreover, this is considered karmic backlash, not purely a curse technique.”

“Should we seek help from someone else then?”

“No need for now. Since you’ve come to Seven-Emotions Valley, we can’t let you leave empty-handed. If word of this gets out, how could we still proclaim our expertise in curses? Although I can’t remove the curse, resolving part of it is still possible.”

“For instance?”

“For instance, I can change your companion’s curse from being ‘unable to approach women' to ‘every woman he approaches loathes him.’”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does that sound even more tragic?

“Well? Shall I do that?”

“Let me ask him what he thinks about it first.” Lu Yang felt it wasn’t his place to decide for Meng Jingzhou.

“Fair enough. I’ll ask him myself.”

Lu Yang’s hesitation made Valley Leader Shuang ask, “What’s wrong?”

“Old Meng’s curse makes him unable to approach all women. Valley Leader, you...”

Valley Leader Shuang grinned. “Is that all you’re worried about? Although he’s cursed, as a top-tier curse master, I’m immune to all curses. His curse can’t affect me. Let’s go together.”

She instructed Luo Yu and Zhao Po to remain behind while she and Lu Yang went to look for Meng Jingzhou. Flying out of Seven-Emotions Valley with Lu Yang, she headed in the direction he indicated.

When they arrived at the designated location, Meng Jingzhou and the old horse were nowhere to be found. Only a simple circle drawn on the ground remained.

“What’s this circle?” Valley Leader Shuang was baffled.

“I drew it,” Lu Yang replied. “I was worried Old Meng might wander everywhere, so I drew a circle at this spot for him to stay within this boundary. I wonder where he’s gone.”

Valley Leader Shuang was slightly knowledgeable about karmic techniques. She pinched her fingers for a quick divination and pointed in a direction. “He should be in that direction. Let’s go.”

The two set off again in search of Meng Jingzhou. Despite flying for a long time, there was not even a trace of his shadow.

“Strange. At my flying speed, we should have caught up to him very quickly.” Valley Leader Shuang performed a divination with her fingers again and obtained another result. “I see, so that’s how it is. He changed direction midway. This way now.”

According to the new results, they flew swiftly once more, but their repeated searches for Meng Jingzhou yielded no success.

Just as Valley Leader Shuang was prepared to calculate Meng Jingzhou’s coordinates again, Lu Yang kindly suggested, “Why don’t you give me his location? I’ll go find Old Meng myself.”

If we continue chasing him like this, we’ll be out of Wilderness Province.

Valley Leader Shuang was a bit embarrassed. “That works too. He’s to the west.”

Lu Yang headed west alone and eventually found Meng Jingzhou collapsed in a remote mountain forest, with the old horse leisurely drinking from a spring nearby.

“You alright?”

Meng Jingzhou wheezed weakly, “Do I look alright to you?” He complained indignantly, “I have no idea what happened just now. Out of nowhere, a tornado appeared, and I happened to be right at its center! It swept me up and carried me away while the old horse just trotted along behind me without a care!

“When the tornado finally stopped, a walking corpse that went berserk started chasing me! As its original cultivation when it was alive was too high, there was no doubt I couldn’t defeat it, so I ran for my life. I nearly died from exhaustion, but thanks to my abundant spirit energy, I outlasted the walking corpse’s energy. Yet the old horse simply watched the whole time without helping!

“I was relieved to have avoided the clutches of the walking corpse, but before I could catch my breath, perhaps I had circulated it too quickly when escaping, my body went out of control and kept running for who knows how long before my rampaging spirit energy stabilized.

“Before I could even take a Great Rejuvenation Pill, I spotted two Divine Transfiguration cultivators battling overhead. Their battle range was enormous and could have easily caught me in the crossfire. Fortunately, as a physique cultivator, I could still run fast without spirit energy, so I fled westward nonstop until I finally reached this place. And then you came.

“What rotten luck... By the way, how did you find me all the way out here?”

Lu Yang was embarrassed to explain that it was because Valley Leader Shuang had been chasing him the whole time, so he sidestepped the question. “I found someone in Seven-Emotions Valley who can help alleviate your curse to some extent.”

“How so?”

“Would you like having women look at you with disgust?”

“?”

Chapter 417: Who in This Wide World Doesn’t Have a Grudge Against Your Shifu?

“Do you like having women look at you with disgust?”

Meng Jingzhou suspected that Lu Yang was seriously ill. Ever since they entered Wilderness Province, it feels like Lu Yang’s condition has been deteriorating rapidly.

“Here’s the situation. I found Valley Leader Shuang Feiyan of Seven-Emotions Valley. She has some connection with Fourth Elder and is willing to help resolve your karmic backlash, but her abilities are limited, and she can only alleviate part of it.”

On his way to find Meng Jingzhou, Lu Yang had considered that if Valley Leader Shuang’s cultivation wasn’t sufficient to fully resolve the curse, perhaps someone like the previous valley leader or the Grand Elder of Seven-Emotions Valley could simply step in.

Valley Leader Shuang had responded, “Do you think everyone senior to me is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?”

Lu Yang continued, “Valley Leader Shuang can modify the karmic backlash from ‘unable to see women’ to ‘all women you see will detest you.’ As for fully resolving it, we’ll have to continue thinking of a solution.”

Meng Jingzhou’s expression turned peculiar. “Why do I feel like that isn’t any better?”

“How could you say it’s not any better? Previously, you couldn’t even enter a brothel, but now you can!”

“Use a normal analogy next time, thanks.”

Squatting on the ground, Meng Jingzhou pondered. If partial mitigation works, I won’t have to hide in the backwoods listening to Lu Yang flaunt his romantic peach-blossom luck every day. I’ll be able to enter cities freely without worrying about sudden disasters forcing me to scurry everywhere.

“Fine. I’ll have to trouble Valley Leader Shuang then. Umm, how should I communicate with her?”

Lu Yang sighed. Since Valley Leader Shuang and Meng Jingzhou can’t meet, and we can’t count on the old horse, I’ll have to be the messenger.

Resigned to his fate, he retraced his steps to find Valley Leader Shuang resting in meditation beneath a tree.

“Found your companion?”

“Yes. He’s willing to receive your treatment.”

Valley Leader Shuang nodded, but soon frowned as another issue occurred to her.

“Is something wrong?” Lu Yang asked.

“His curse is extremely hard to resolve. Even partial mitigation will be challenging. I need to examine his specific condition to determine the method.”

“But you two can’t meet, right?”

“Precisely the problem.”

Having lived for over two millennia, Valley Leader Shuang didn’t take long to devise a solution. “I have an idea! I can perform Suspended Thread Pulse Diagnosis.[1] But the lush vegetation here would interfere with the diagnosis result. Why don’t you bring your companion to Seven-Emotions Valley’s entrance? There’s no obstruction there.” With that, she flew back to Seven-Emotions Valley to prepare the necessary tools.

Lu Yang returned to the barren mountain to fetch Meng Jingzhou and had the old horse send them to Seven-Emotions Valley. This time, the horse didn’t dawdle, swiftly delivering them to the entrance with spatial spells.

The visitors seeking to dispel their curses had dispersed, and the disciples holding consultations had moved their stools back into the valley, allowing Meng Jingzhou to approach unimpeded.

Lu Yang entered Seven-Emotions Valley to retrieve the magical treasures for the Suspended Thread Pulse Diagnosis.

Suspended Thread Pulse Diagnosis was an old diagnostic method that originated in the Great Qian Dynasty. It was used when imperial consorts were ill, but since they were the emperor’s women, male imperial physicians could not make physical contact with them.

Therefore, the imperial physicians thought of a solution. They tied one end of a thread to the imperial consort’s wrist and held the other end of the thread, interpreting the sensation, pulse condition, spirit energy, and sundry other factors through the thread and diagnosing the illness with their medical expertise.

The wiser imperial physicians were skilled in escape techniques, stealthily examining the imperial consorts in the night without a single soul knowing.

“I understand the reasoning, but why did you wrap me up so tightly? Didn’t you say that Suspended Thread Pulse Diagnosis only requires a thread tied around the wrist?” Meng Jingzhou was enraged. He was bound in white silk thread from head to toe, with only his mouth uncovered.

“Shut your mouth, shut your mouth.” Lu Yang proceeded to gag him with more threads.

“What else can I do? Your karmic backlash isn’t ordinary. How could a single thread be enough if you want a successful diagnosis? We’ll need to wrap your whole body for better results. Just bear with it. This is Valley Leader Shuang’s idea.”

Losing the battle, Meng Jingzhou could only obediently wait for Valley Leader Shuang’s diagnosis.

Lu Yang stepped into Seven-Emotions Valley and found Valley Leader Shuang seated in meditation, a cluster of threads clasped in her hand. He held his breath, not daring to disturb her concentration.

“Double Single’s Golden Core? Quite the bold one.”

“You can recognize Singel’s Golden Cores?” Lu Yang was astonished. It was the first time someone outside the Dao-Seeking Sect could identify Meng Jingzhou’s golden cores.

“I met someone with a Single’s Spirit Root in my youth. He was rather talented, but not like your companion here.

“This bloodline and surname...so, he’s from the Meng Family.” A nostalgic smile played across her lips.

“This karmic backlash is interesting. It’s more severe than what Shanren described, but luckily, it’s still within my expectations.” An idea to mitigate part of the karmic backlash crystallized in Valley Leader Shuang’s mind.

“Have you studied curse principles?”

“No.”

“Curses possess both spiritual and corporeal attributes. To dispel a curse, we begin with the body, but the soul must also be treated.

“Here are toad skin, dried centipedes, powdered poisonous bugs... Feed these to the Meng boy in sequence. Remember, it has to be eaten raw to neutralize the physical part of the curse. Then, use this set of Seven-Star Silver Needles to pierce him and let his blood out. Perform this bloodletting three times. The Seven-Star Silver Needles are capable of connecting to the soul and alleviating the soul part of the curse.

“Have you memorized everything?”

Lu Yang verified, “Let me confirm it again. Are you sure the toad skin and everything else must be consumed raw?”

“You can eat it cooked too, but eating it raw is more efficient.”

“Higher absorption efficiency?”

“Higher time efficiency. It saves cooking time.”

“Fine, I’ve remembered.” As Lu Yang turned to leave, Valley Leader Shuang stopped him.

“Wait, there’s one more thing I need to confirm with you again.”

“Please speak.”

“Is the old Taciturn scoundrel really still alive? I know some sect leaders like to conceal their deaths for fear of causing chaos. If he’s truly kicked the bucket, just tell me. I’ll personally take you to the Corpse-Driving Sect to learn how to refine walking corpses.”

“You have a grudge against my shifu?”

Valley Leader Shuang let out a string of glacial laughter. “Who in this wide world doesn’t have a grudge against your shifu?

“Back when your shifu was in jail, Shanren and I went to visit him. When your shifu saw me, he said he was immune to curses and that I could test it out if I didn’t believe him. I naturally didn’t believe him, so I cast several curses on him. After that, your shifu was released on medical parole.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Later, this incident came to light, and the authorities arrested both your shifu and me on charges of prison escape.”

“...My shifu is still alive and in good health. He was recently locked in prison. I’ve no idea whether he’s out yet.”

“What a pity.”

1. Men and women were not allowed to come into contact in ancient China, especially in the case of noble women and men. As such, when a male physician treated a female patient, they either placed a handkerchief over the wrist or, in extreme cases, tied a thread around her wrist and sensed their pulse from afar, thereby avoiding physical contact. This is quite popular in novels, and it didn’t happen in history, but as for the effectiveness... There are two pictures below for your reference. ☜

Chapter 418: Didn’t You Say the Curse Doesn’t Affect You?

“By the way, I have a question I’d like to consult you, Valley Leader.”

“Go ahead.”

“After modifying Old Meng’s curse to make women detest him, will the curse affect you?”

Valley Leader Shuang was visibly displeased that Lu Yang was doubting her ability. “Previously, I didn’t get to examine that Meng boy’s curse up close, which resulted in a miscalculation and caused him to run away from me for half a day. Now that I have secured an accurate and thorough diagnosis of his condition through the Suspended Thread Pulse Diagnosis, after my treatment, the curse will have weakened to a point that it doesn’t affect me.”

Lu Yang breathed a sigh of relief. That’s good then.

~~~

“Valley Leader Shuang said you need to eat toad skin, dried centipedes, powdered poisonous bugs... Everything must be eaten raw for higher efficiency.” Lu Yang played the Valley Leader’s authority card to order Meng Jingzhou.

Untangling himself from the white threads, Meng Jingzhou’s face turned green upon seeing the bizarre medicinal ingredients. Are these meant for human consumption?

“Are you sure eating it raw has higher efficiency?”

“Those aren’t my words. It’s Valley Leader Shuang who said so.”

With no other choice, Meng Jingzhou followed his doctor’s advice. His scalp tingled, and he fought the urge to retch as he forced every item down in sequence. Though they were clearly lifeless, the moment they entered his stomach, it felt as if they had come alive, churning violently like a stormy sea within him.

Zhao Po watched beside him silently. Is this how these two Dao-Seeking Sect geniuses compete? By mutual scheming and sabotage?

“There’s still the needles and bloodletting.” Lu Yang produced the Seven-Star Silver Needles that Valley Leader Shuang had lent him.

The needles were probably powerful magical treasures, as evident by how Lu Yang didn’t need to infuse any energy and effortlessly pierced them through Meng Jingzhou’s defenses into his arm. Considering Meng Jingzhou’s absurdly strong physical defensive power as a physique cultivator, even Lu Yang didn’t dare guarantee that he could break through his defenses in such a short time.

“Ss! Can’t you warn me before piercing me?!” Meng Jingzhou grimaced in pain more acute than anything he had felt in years.

Had it been a legitimate physician performing the bloodletting, it would have been painless. Unfortunately, Lu Yang was not a legitimate physician—in fact, he wasn’t even a physician.

“Immortal Fairy, do you know how to use needles?” Lu Yang recalled he had a theoretical golden finger cheat in his mental space.

“Bloodletting? I’m familiar with this! Demon beast meat reeks when blood isn’t drained properly. If you use my bloodletting method, I can assure you that not a single drop of blood will remain.”

Lu Yang felt that Meng Jingzhou’s life wasn’t a necessary sacrifice for this procedure.

As Lu Yang plucked out the needle, Meng Jingzhou’s blood gushed out like a geyser. The needle seemed to carry a healing-suppressing property. The self-healing ability that Meng Jingzhou was proud of was useless, and he could only wait for the wound to heal slowly.

The drops of blood that fell onto the ground were no ordinary blood—they were a great Golden Core cultivator’s blood that encompassed precious spirit energy. Moreover, it was the blood of a Golden Core cultivator with Double Single’s Golden Cores, imbued with the purest yang energy and more effective than any pure-yang medicine.

The insects seemed to have mysteriously sensed how precious the blood was and swarmed in to feed on Meng Jingzhou’s blood and were rejuvenated after the feast.

What these unsuspecting insects didn’t know was that they would never be able to encounter female insects ever again.

Yet in this moment, nobody knew about this, including Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and the insects themselves...

After the wound healed, Lu Yang pierced the needle again, plucked it out, let the blood out, and waited for the wound to heal, only to pierce the needle again. After repeating the process three times, Meng Jingzhou felt the lingering unease in his heart ease slightly, and his face lit up with joy.

“It actually works!” Although the curse isn’t completely dispelled, dispelling part of it is a massive improvement. Coming to Wilderness Province is indeed the right choice. It’s much more reliable than the elders’ medical consultation.

When Valley Leader Shuang deemed the time right, she walked out from Seven-Emotions Valley and finally saw Meng Jingzhou. “You’re the Meng boy?”

The moment Meng Jingzhou laid his eyes on Valley Leader Shuang, he was convinced that the lighter feeling in his heart wasn’t his hallucination. His curse had truly been partially mitigated. “Valley Leader, I am Meng Jingzhou of the Meng Family and a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Valley Leader Shuang snorted. “As I thought, you’re from the Meng Family.”

A sense of foreboding welled within Lu Yang. He hastily stepped forward and cupped his fists. “Many thanks for treating my companion, Valley Leader Shuang. May I ask what our next step should be so that we can fully cure Old Meng’s curse?”

Valley Leader Shuang was upset. “I shouldn’t have treated you just now. That old Taciturn scoundrel had sabotaged me before, and you people from the Meng Family aren’t much better. Scram!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Didn’t you say the curse doesn’t affect you?

Valley Leader, can you be more reliable?

Now that things had come to this, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou couldn’t press further and had to depart Seven-Emotions Valley first.

In the carriage, Zhao Po broke the silence. “Why don’t we visit the Corpse-Driving Sect? The elders and the sect leader are familiar with Wilderness Province and know many top-tier curse masters and practitioners of esoteric arts. Who knows, they might have a solution?”

“Seems like our only option.”

~~~

As the three humans, one walking corpse, and one horse approached a city for respite, they heard a boisterous commotion nearby.

“Everyone, everyone, I am Qing Luo, the new sect leader of the Cloud Terrace Sect. According to our sect’s rules, any woman who becomes the sect leader must choose a husband through a martial arts contest.

“Therefore, I have set up an arena stage here. All are welcome to challenge me in a duel. Anyone who can defeat me will be my ideal husband!”

At the age of eighteen,[1] Qing Luo was pure and pretty. She had big, limpid eyes that sparkled with untainted beauty, and her tenacious spirit made her even more endearing. Having publicized the martial arts contest for marriage early, most people here were already aware and had come to win her hand in marriage.

However, there were also people who were unaware, such as Lu Yang’s trio.

“Cloud Terrace Sect? I haven’t heard of it before. Brother Zhao, do you know?”

Zhao Po racked his mind and finally found some information regarding the sect from a corner of his mind. “The Cloud Terrace Sect is a very small sect that is barely worth mentioning. Its influence is limited to a city, or perhaps even smaller than that. The cultivator with the highest cultivation in their sect is likely only at the Golden Core Stage. The Cloud Terrace Sect is most known for a particular ancestral rule: if the sect leader is female, she must choose a man stronger than her as husband. This is probably what’s playing out before us now.”

Minor sects like the Cloud Terrace Sect were as innumerable as the hair of oxen in the Great Xia Dynasty.

One shouldn’t be misled by how Lu Yang frequently brushed shoulders with Golden Core and Nascent Soul cultivators and made enemies that started at the Fusion Stage and all the way up to immortals. That was because Lu Yang was a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect and had access to matters far beyond.

What was the Dao-Seeking Sect? They ranked first among the Five Great Immortal Sects and gathered peerless geniuses across the continent. Anyone from the sect could easily make a name for themselves in the Central Continent.

In reality, most cultivators struggled to reach the Foundation Establishment Stage in their whole lives, and the Golden Core Stage was all the more an unattainable goal. This was how Golden Core ancestral clans and sects emerged.

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up at the sight of Qing Luo, feeling a flutter in his heart. He felt that his romantic peach-blossom luck was finally coming.

1. This chapter states sixteen, but the next chapter states eighteen, so I have changed it to eighteen here for consistency. ☜

Chapter 419: Ancestral Rules Must Not Be Defied

“Both of you, don’t go onto the stage. Lu Yang, you brat have had such an eventful journey. It’s my turn to have some good luck!” Meng Jingzhou stopped Lu Yang and Zhao Po, though neither had intended to take the stage in the first place.

Meng Jingzhou was about to step onto the stage, but someone else was faster. It was a steady-looking middle-aged man with a long beard and a scholarly bearing.

The long-bearded man was renowned locally, and someone beneath the stage recognized him. “It’s Great Teacher Xiang from the Soaring Dragon Academy! He founded the academy and has mentored numerous scholars, even producing a provincial-level graduate![1] His disciples are spread across Wilderness Province, with some even serving in the imperial capital!”

“That’s not all! He’s also an orthodox Confucian cultivator. I heard one of his former students mention that he had already reached the Basic Golden Core Stage five years ago. I’ve no idea whether he has broken through since. Countless Golden Core ancestral clans have tried to send their descendants to study under him and offered him extravagant gifts without stint, but he refused them all!”

“What? Basic Golden Core Stage five years ago? How are the rest of us supposed to compete? There’s no way Immortal Fairy Qingluo could defeat him!”

The cultivation world liked using the term “Immortal Fairy” to praise female cultivators for their beauty, talent, or strength. After all, in the public’s perception, there were no female immortals, so the term was tossed around freely.

Lu Yang never used “Immortal Fairy” to compliment anyone, not out of caution, but because he didn’t consider it a compliment...

“Don’t panic! Immortal Fairy Qing Luo is remarkably talented. At just eighteen, she’s already at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage and the youngest sect leader in Cloud Terrace Sect’s history. Against a Basic Golden Core cultivator, she might still stand a chance!”

“That’s great... wait, doesn’t that mean we don’t have a shot either?”

Great Teacher Xiang stood on the stage, his lips curved into an elegant smile. “Sect Leader Qing, please.”

Qing Luo sighed softly. “Great Teacher Xiang, did you not see the rules? Participants must be twenty or below. You’re already in your forties. Even if I’m seeking a husband, shouldn’t he at least be around my age?”

Reeling from the traumatic blow, Great Teacher Xiang was seized by a burst of inspiration and composed poetry on the spot. “When I was born, you weren’t born yet; when you were born, I was already old.[2]

“Exactly, so could you please step down from the stage? I only paid for the venue for one day; time is limited.”

Great Teacher Xiang staggered off the stage, his spirit thoroughly crushed.

The subsequent cultivators who went up the stage were more reliable. All of them were talented youths around the age of twenty, including a few women disguised as men for their travels in the jianghu.

“This Qing Luo has a pretty good foundation. Although there are flaws, given the environment she cultivated in and the lack of proper guidance, reaching this level of Foundation Establishment is extremely rare and impressive. She must have had a fortuitous encounter or is simply a genius.”

“She’s indeed not bad. Even in our Corpse-Driving Sect, she’d qualify as a true lineage disciple and compete for the top eight—maybe even the top four—in the sect’s grand tournament.”

Lu Yang and Zhao Po assessed Qing Luo’s talent in whispers.

“Why not recruit her into your Corpse-Driving Sect? It’s a waste for a talent like her to remain in such a small place.” Lu Yang chuckled.

“It depends on her choice. I can try, but it’s not guaranteed to work. I have met many who refuse to abandon their own sects, saying it’s the place that took them in and raised them and that they won’t forsake them.

“Besides, due to our sect’s cultivation technique, our faces are so pale that we look like we have been dead for days. Some cultivators refuse to join us because of that and opt for other first-class sects instead.” Zhao Po pointed at his own face, which was paler than any woman’s. Whether orthodox or unorthodox, all Corpse Drivers shared the same ghostly complexion.

Lu Yang nodded in agreement. When he first met Zhao Po, he had mistaken him for a walking corpse.

Just like the two had observed, Qing Luo’s foundation was solid, and she hardly met an equal among her peers. Her cloud manipulation technique was divinely skillful, effortlessly defeating one ambitious young challenger after another.

Finally, it was Meng Jingzhou’s turn.

With a confident smile, he stepped onto the stage with such composure that his mere presence seemed to exert an overwhelming pressure.

“I am Meng Jingzhou, disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

The moment those words left his mouth, the spectators’ pupils widened, and the crowd erupted in murmurs.

“Dao-Seeking Sect? The head of the Great Five Immortal Sects?!”

“I heard that anyone who walks out of there is a peerless genius. Even a restaurant owner from there could establish their own sect outside and become an ancestor!”

“Why does the name Meng Jingzhou sound so familiar?”

“It sounds like the Meng Jingzhou from the Qing Province Grand Ceremony.”

Hearing Meng Jingzhou’s name, Lu Yang’s expression changed drastically, and he blurted out, “The same Meng Jingzhou who had already formed his golden core but still participated in the competition for the golden core cultivation insights among the rewards?”

“Why did I hear that he simply likes to bully those at lower cultivation realms?”

“Didn’t he go to the Qing Province Grand Ceremony to make a scene?”

“That shouldn’t be the case, right? He has no grudge against Qing Province. He simply wanted to challenge the judges.”

Lu Yang went with the flow and added, “Yet he voluntarily jumped off the stage to concede defeat before even sparring with the judges.”

The crowd buzzed with differing accounts, but without exception, everything they said was true.

Qing Luo had an odd expression as she looked at Meng Jingzhou with distaste. Clearly, she had heard of his reputation.

After the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s deeds had torn through the Central Continent like a whirlwind and became widely circulated among low-level cultivators. However, the further the tales traveled, the more the details became warped.

Listening to the chatter, Meng Jingzhou’s face turned black. My reputation has been trampled on just like this. “A cultivator must remain steadfast in their Dao heart. The opinions of the outer world are but fleeting clouds to me. That said, why did one of those voices sound so familiar?

“Forget it! I’ll win this match first!” Meng Jingzhou gestured for Qing Luo to make the first move.

Since Meng Jingzhou fit the rules and criteria, Qing Luo had no grounds to refuse. She struck first, summoning auspicious clouds behind her that morphed into hatchets, yue-axes, sabers, and forks—eighteen types of weapons in total—all extremely sharp as the barrage shot toward Meng Jingzhou!

This move alone was enough to give challengers a bitter lesson, causing them to lose at the first strike.

“Amazing cloud manipulation technique!” Meng Jingzhou’s eyes gleamed. Facing the storm of weapons, he assumed a stance for fist techniques.

“Crushing Fist!”

The moment the eighteen weapons met his fist seals, they dissolved into warm, fluffy clouds.

Qing Luo was undeniably strong. Unfortunately, her opponent was Meng Jingzhou. Even if she had been at the Golden Core Stage, she still wouldn’t stand a chance against him.

In just three punches, Meng Jingzhou forced out all of Qing Luo’s trump cards, leaving her no choice but to admit defeat.

“I lost.” Accepting her loss, Qing Luo gritted her teeth at the sight of Meng Jingzhou. “Ancestral rules must not be defied. According to the ancestral rules, the person who defeats me shall be my husband.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes brightened. “Then...”

Qing Luo’s gaze hardened as if she had made a major life decision. “In that case, I have no choice but to abolish this ancestral rule!”

1. There are different stages to the imperial examination, and juren is someone who has passed the exam at the provincial level. ☜

2. There seems to be a typo here, but I’ve adapted it slightly to fit the context. This verse is from an anonymous poet in the Tang Dynasty. As you can probably tell, it’s about how two people who love each other can’t stay by each other’s side for long due to their large age gaps. You may see this phrase in stories with age gaps too. ☜

Chapter 420: Meng Jingzhou’s Romantic Peach-Blossom Luck

Below the arena stage, Lu Yang doubled over with laughter, tears rolling down his cheeks.

Zhao Po wanted to laugh too but found it improper to mock Meng Jingzhou, so he could only try his best to hold it in.

Meng Jingzhou’s face darkened. She’s even abolished the ancestral rule. What else can I say?

With the ancestral rule abolished, Qing Luo was freed from the restraints and felt as if heaven and earth had suddenly expanded before her. She withdrew from the stage without hesitation and headed back to her estate.

Meng Jingzhou leaped off the stage and glared fiercely at Lu Yang, who was still laughing, and Zhao Po, who was struggling to keep his laughter in.

The three humans, one corpse, and one horse entered the city. Perhaps because Meng Jingzhou’s romantic peach-blossom luck had been suppressed far too long, it was now unstoppable as it suddenly erupted all at once.

First, they encountered a woman selling herself to bury her father. Despite dressing in mourning clothes made of coarse hemp, her beauty still shone through. She claimed that she was willing to sell herself as a servant or concubine to bury her father. When she spotted Meng Jingzhou, she timidly called him “Young Master,” making his heart itch.

Although she had no cultivation and had missed the golden period for cultivating, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recognized something special about her at a glance. “Interesting. This lass possesses the extremely rare Illusion-Shattering Dao Physique. Though she appears frail now, her Illusion-Shattering Dao physique is actually amassing strength. In six months to a year, her Dao physique will fully awaken, and she’ll soar to the sky in one go, quickly catching up to her peers’ cultivation speed.

“If some discerning old fellow were to take this little lass as a disciple and train her for a few years, her achievements would be even greater.”

The world knew of Nine Great Immortal Physiques, including Tao Yaoye’s Metamorphic Immortal Physique and Sixth Elder’s Immaculate Immortal Physique.

Apart from these, the Thirty-Six Dao Physiques were also widely recognized. While Dao physiques couldn’t compare to immortal physiques, those with Dao physiques still qualified as prodigies worthy of a spot in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era and becoming the left- and right-hand men of geniuses like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou!

Meng Jingzhou was unaware of the girl’s background or physique. He simply found her pitiful and attractive, so he bought her.

Then, he got scammed.

The girl took the spirit stones, claiming that she was going to bury her father, then never returned.

When the trio went to report it, the authorities said that the girl was a repeat offender. They would open a case but advised them not to be hopeful, for she was notoriously hard to catch.

~~~

“Little beauty, just submit to this young master! I’ll give you endless wealth and glory!” A lecherous laughter rang out, clearly not belonging to a good person.

Meng Jingzhou perked up. I’m familiar with this scenario! Lu Yang had bragged about similar encounters and left him envious for a long time.

“Stop right there! How dare you harass decent women in my presence?!” Meng Jingzhou stepped forward with an air of righteousness, ready to act in the name of justice.

Afterward, he beat up the young master and his entire family. Even their old ancestor wailed in grievance, promising never to repeat their misdeeds.
