The little beauty tearfully thanked Meng Jingzhou. “This humble woman will work like an ox and a horse to repay your kindness in my next life, savior!”

Then, she fled without looking back, unwilling to spend another moment with him.

~~~

As the trio sought lodging, an argument reached their ears.

“Lü'er, don’t you know my feelings for you? I really like you! Why do you keep refusing my love? Have I done something wrong?” A gloomy-looking nobleman in luxurious clothes persistently pressed a woman in light green for answers.

Unable to endure the nobleman’s pursuit any longer, Lü'er’s eyes lit up when she spotted the extraordinary aura of Meng Jingzhou’s trio.

“I really can’t accept your feelings. I already like someone else!”

The nobleman shook his head. “Lü'er, don’t lie. I don’t believe it.”

She pointed to Meng Jingzhou. “It’s him. He’s the one I like. We’ve already pledged our lives to each other!”

Meng Jingzhou thought that his romantic peach-blossom luck was finally here and even flaunted it to Lu Yang and Zhao Po by transmitting to them auditory messages.

Lu Yang cautioned Meng Jingzhou against acting recklessly and analyzed the situation for him. “That gloomy nobleman is clearly ruthless and looks like a local tyrant, someone not to be trifled with. He wants to claim Lü'er as his own, but Lü'er doesn’t like his type and finds a shield.

“It’s true that you’re not afraid of such local bullies, but Lü'er doesn’t know that. Since you two are strangers, she doesn’t know your identity or strength compared to that brooding nobleman. To block his advances, she pushed you to the front, forcing you to bear all the pressure.

“Under such circumstances, do you think she actually likes you?”

~~~

At the inn that night, a woman in stealth attire smashed through Meng Jingzhou’s window. She wore a veil, revealing only catlike emerald eyes. Her eyes glazed with the desire of spring, and she breathed heavily like she was poisoned and required masculine yang energy to neutralize it to avoid the risk of exploding from within.

Since only Meng Jingzhou was present in the room, only one solution remained.

The woman shot Meng Jingzhou a disgusted look, fished out a detoxification pill from her storage ring, and swallowed it. The effects kicked in immediately, and she swiftly departed with the wind.

In my line of work, I must naturally head out fully prepared.

Throughout the whole process, Meng Jingzhou didn’t even have a chance to speak.

~~~

After resting for the night, the three were prepared to set off. When they were about to check out, a fairly attractive young miss from an affluent family specifically approached Meng Jingzhou for help, as if she had seen her knight in shining armor. “Excuse me, may I ask if you’re not from around here?”

“Yes.”

She exhaled a sigh of relief. “That’s great, Mother won’t know you! Here’s the situation. My mother has been pushing me to marry, but I’m not willing, so I lied about having a boyfriend. I’ve gotten away with it all this while, but today she insisted on meeting my boyfriend. Can you pretend to be my boyfriend? I'll pay!”

Meng Jingzhou readily agreed.

“What’s going on?” Zhao Po was surprised.

“Who knows?” Lu Yang shrugged, not paying much attention.

Strangely, the meeting with the parents proceeded smoothly. Meng Jingzhou showcased his family background, character, cultivation, and sect—all ideal husband material. However, the young lady’s mother refused to agree, finding Meng Jingzhou displeasing to the eye no matter how she looked at him. Finally, she chased him out and exhorted her daughter to cut all ties with him.

Later, the young miss secretly explained to Meng Jingzhou, “I’m sorry. When I saw you for the first time, I already found you quite off-putting. My mother is similar to me, so she’d probably feel the same way and would definitely not approve of you as my boyfriend. This way, she’ll stop pestering me about marriage!

“This is the payment we agreed upon. Let’s never meet again.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Motherf*cking curse! It’s not any better than before!

Throughout the journey, Meng Jingzhou’s romantic peach-blossom luck never stopped, finally running out at the end, and the trio successfully arrived at the Corpse-Driving Sect.

Chapter 421: Man Gu’s Passion For Learning

The capital of Wilderness Province was Hanshui City, the most important and prosperous city in Wilderness Province. The Corpse-Driving Sect lay in the Yin-Corpse Mountain Range beyond the city walls, where yin energy thrived and made it ideal for nurturing corpses.

To Corpse Drivers, the Yin-Corpse Mountain Range, where the Corpse-Driving Sect was located, was sacred ground.

As they entered the Corpse-Driving Sect’s territory, despite the blazing sun, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou couldn’t sense a trace of warmth, only a bone-chilling cold.

On the other hand, Zhao Po showed a comfortable expression, enjoying the atmosphere.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was not surprised. “It’s not just Corpse Drivers. Anyone practicing yin-attribute cultivation techniques would find this place comfortable. Moreover, there’s no thunder when it rains here, so it’s very safe.”

Yin-attribute cultivation techniques were related to ghosts, souls, and corpses. This was what the Nine-Netherworlds Creed specialized in. Practitioners feared thunder the most, for lightning represented pure yang energy, the natural bane of these cultivators. One of the twenty-four solar terms was called Jingzhe (Awakening of Insects) and described the petrifying power of thunder on yin beings.

“Senior Brother Zhao, you’re back!” Two disciples stationed at the gate hurriedly bowed at Zhao Po’s return. Each had their own walking corpses, which stood guard alongside them.

Ranked second among the young generation of disciples, Zhao Po was practically an idol-like figure among his peers. Unlike the top-ranked Huang Ming, Zhao Po was kind and helpful. Many had received his aid, and he was well-liked and well-connected in the Corpse-Driving Sect.

“Senior Brother Zhao, these two are...”

“They are fellow Daoists from the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, here to visit our sect.”

The two disciples at the entrance were floored. “The Dao-Seeking Sect again?!”

“Again?”

“Senior Brother Zhao, you may not be aware, but while you were away, another fellow Daoist from the Dao-Seeking Sect arrived. He’s a barbarian and was here to study Corpse-Driving Techniques.”

“Is his name Man Gu?” Lu Yang interjected.

“Yes, that’s him!”

“Why is Man Gu learning Corpse-Driving Techniques? Isn’t he a Confucian cultivator?” Meng Jingzhou was perplexed.

“Who knows?”

After the two disciples on duty reported their arrival to the sect, an administrator of the sect emerged to personally greet them.

Lu Yang stated their purpose. “Could we trouble you to pass on the message? We’re here to visit your esteemed sect leader.”

The administrator revealed a troubled look. “Our sect leader has cultivated until a critical point and has gone into seclusion since he accepted Huang Ming as his disciple. He’s unable to meet anyone.”

“I see, no matter then. We can visit the elders instead.” Their objective was to seek a solution for Meng Jingzhou, so consulting any senior would do.

“In that case, I’ll take the two of them. My shifu is the First Elder,” Zhao Po offered with a smile.

After the sect’s grand tournament, Huang Ming became the sect leader’s disciple, while Zhao Po became the First Elder’s disciple, so he technically outranked the administrator slightly.

“I’ll have to trouble you then, Junior Nephew Zhao Po.”

“Not at all, Junior Uncle Mo.”

The three humans, one walking corpse, and one horse entered the Corpse-Driving Sect. After finding a place for the old horse, they went to look for the Corpse-Driving Sect’s First Elder.

“What a fragrant smell.” Zhao Po sniffed the air, detecting an unfamiliar fragrance.

“It’s indeed quite fragrant. And very familiar too.” Meng Jingzhou also sniffed the air, recognizing the familiar aroma of barbeque.

“It must be Man Gu.” Lu Yang chuckled.

Those capable of producing such a barbeque flavor were only the three of them, the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups, and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s members.

In other words, aside from the diabolic creeds, only the three of them could.

“Let’s go and take a look.” Meng Jingzhou momentarily forgot about his curse.

The three followed the aroma—or more accurately, the crowd—to find Man Gu.

The disciples were clustered together, though it was unclear what they were doing. The aroma had wafted out right from the center.

“Make way, make way!” The three squeezed their way to the front row and saw Man Gu.

Man Gu was sitting cross-legged on the ground, murmuring incantations.

Two lamb corpses danced over a bonfire, basting each other with spices. The fragrance from the mutton and spices mixed perfectly, and as the flames licked the meat, a mouthwatering aroma assaulted the nostrils.

The roasted lamb corpses glistened with an irresistible luster, whetting everyone’s appetite.

“Disassemble!” At Man Gu’s command, the lamb corpses disassembled themselves into bite-sized portions for everyone.

This was the moment the disciples had been waiting for. They dug in ravenously and showered endless praises.

“I’ve never tasted a roasted whole lamb this good! Look at this skin! It’s so crispy and has a charred aroma. And this meat! One bite fills my mouth with juices!”

“That’s not all! The roasted whole lamb I’ve eaten before was always unevenly cooked. Some parts were burned, while others remained half-raw. But look at Fellow Daoist Man Gu’s version! That’s amazingly fragrant! Even the bones are infused with flavor!”

“I have to give it to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Say, why haven’t we thought of using Corpse-Driving Techniques for barbeque? The results are spectacular!”

“That’s why they can qualify to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect, while we can’t. The difference in our level of thinking is completely different.”

“And it’s not just about the level of thinking. Fellow Daoist Man Gu is also very talented. Look at us, we take three to five years to learn Corpse-Driving Techniques, but he grasped the basics in just half a month. Even his zeal for learning surpasses ours.”

Man Gu was very humble. “Fellow Daoists, you flatter me too much. My meager skills pale significantly to my two senior brothers, especially Senior Brother Lu Yang. If he learns Corpse-Driving Techniques and combines them with his Three Esse True Fire, the flavor of this roasted whole lamb could reach even greater heights!”

The crowd couldn’t imagine just how delicious that would be.

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Man Gu, you brat! So this is why you’ve come here to Corpse-Driving Techniques. It’s because you still haven’t forgotten what you said in the jungle.

When Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, and Man Gu were training in the jungle, they slaughtered numerous demon beasts. At the time, Man Gu discovered that roasting whole demon beasts could easily result in uneven cooking, so he proposed using Corpse-Driving Techniques for barbecue.

This method had even received high praise from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—the Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s biggest backer.

“Man Gu’s picking things up fast. Not only can he command the lamb corpses to stand over the fire for roasting, but he can also make them disassemble themselves.”

The two had learned from Zhao Po that Walking Corpse Disassembly was a combat technique that was notoriously hard to master.

“Man Gu, it’s been a long time!” The two called out to him, their lips curling into grins despite themselves.

Hearing the familiar voices, Meng Jingzhou’s head jerked his head up, his eyes lighting up at the sight of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “Brother Lu, Brother Meng! What brings you here?”

“Old Meng’s finally getting retribution for having done too many bad deeds,” Lu Yang replied with a mischievous smirk.

“Bad deeds?” Man Gu was baffled. Brother Lu and Brother Meng are my role models and amazingly good people. How could they do any bad deeds?

“Old Meng has been cursed. He has no fate with women now.”

Man Gu suddenly understood. Brother Meng must be demonstrating his commitment to cultivation! That’s why he has deliberately unlocked the full potential of his Single’s Spirit Root to endure a curse!

While I have been studying Corpse-Driving Techniques here, Brother Lu and Brother Meng must have been cultivating diligently and making every second count.

In contrast, I was getting proud just because I learned a bit of Corpse-Driving Techniques, yet it doesn’t even boost my cultivation. Compared to Brother Meng, I’m simply squandering my time.

Man Gu felt extremely ashamed.

Chapter 422: Man Gu: Is the Heavenly Court Creed Still Recruiting?

“In other words, Brother Meng, you’re suffering from a karmic backlash that makes women involuntarily hate you, which is why you came to Wilderness Province to seek a solution?” Man Gu finally summarized after hearing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s explanation.

As expected of Brother Meng! He operates on a whole different level. How could ordinary Golden Core cultivators encounter something like karmic backlash?

After the roast lamb was divided, the trio moved a short distance away from the other Corpse-Driving Sect disciples to catch up.

“What about you? How did you end up here at the Corpse-Driving Sect? Did you come alone?”

“You know that I returned home for the coming-of-age ceremony, right? After it ended, I mentioned I wanted to study Corpse-Driving Techniques at the Corpse-Driving Sect for better barbecue results, so the tribe leader sent me here and took the chance to visit Sect Leader Lu. But since Sect Leader Lu was in seclusion, the tribe leader didn’t disturb him. He left me here and went back.”

The sect leader of the Corpse-Driving Sect, Lu Baqian,[1] was at the Advanced Fusion Stage.

“I was initially hoping to spar with Huang Ming of the Corpse-Driving Sect, but he seemed to be away on a mission and hasn’t returned.”

As the “Big Senior Brother” of their generation, Lu Yang was concerned about Man Gu’s safety. “I heard that the Barbarian Tribe’s coming-of-age ceremony is very dangerous and requires you to fight Golden Core demon beasts.”

Man Gu scratched the back of his head with a guileless grin. “It wasn’t that dangerous. After all, the three of us had already infiltrated a diabolic creed at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage and hunted Golden Core demon beasts in the jungle at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.”

True... Compared to these two events, Man Gu slaughtering Golden Core beasts at the Golden Core Stage is as safe as strolling back to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Right then, Zhao Po walked over. “My shifu is usually cultivating, but he happens to be free now.”

“Then let’s go.” Meng Jingzhou beamed, feeling that his luck was gradually turning better. However, he soon grew wary and asked, “Is your shifu male or female?”

“Male.”

“Wonderful.”

Having learned enough Corpse-Driving Techniques for barbecue purposes, Man Gu saw no need for further study and tagged along to meet the First Elder. He chuckled. “Seeing you two reminded me of something fun. There’s a new barbeque shop in Hanshui City called ‘One More Time Barbeque Shop.’ Same name as ours! But they are a chain store and even claimed they had inherited some ancient secret recipe. I was hoping to try it but haven’t gotten the time to do so.” He shook his head regretfully.

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

“Actually...that shop you saw is somewhat connected to us.” Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message. I can’t talk about this in front of Zhao Po, lest he misunderstands and thinks we’re from diabolic creeds.

“I haven’t had the chance to tell you before you returned home, but while you weren’t around, Old Meng and I made contact with the Nine-Netherworlds Creed...”

After listening to the full tale, Man Gu’s jaw hung slack as his brain struggled to process the information.

I’d simply gone home, yet Brother Lu and Brother Meng had already established the Heavenly Court Creed, recruited Big Senior Sister, the sect leader, elders, and Tao Yaoye, and then got the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to run a barbeque chain.

I wasn’t away for that long either—not even two months...

No wonder Brother Lu and Brother Meng are geniuses.

“Don’t worry, you’re considered our ‘technical partner.’ You’ll get ten percent of the barbeque shop’s profits.” After all, the barbeque shop’s recipe is built on the Barbarian clan’s ancestral recipe.

Man Gu didn’t care about the profits. After all, he was the sole remaining Ancient Barbarian, and the whole Barbarian Tribe treated him like he was a golden goose. He had no shortage of spirit stones—just rarely any occasion to spend them.

“Is the Heavenly Court Creed still recruiting?” Man Gu wanted to get closer to his two role models.

“Absolutely! Our Heavenly Court Creed needs geniuses like you!” Lu Yang was all smiles. Even if Man Gu hadn’t brought it up, I would have proposed it myself.

And thus, all top five disciples of Lu Yang’s cohort had now joined the Heavenly Court Creed.

The group ventured into the deepest part of the Corpse-Driving Sect, where the atmosphere had grown increasingly gloomy and cold.

Deep inside a palatial yet empty hall sat an old man, his eyes frosty and devoid of emotions.

“Shifu, these two are Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, the visitors from the Dao-Seeking Sect I’ve mentioned. As for Fellow Daoist Man Gu, you’ve probably already met him.”

“Greetings, First Elder!” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou bowed, paying respects as juniors.

“Alright, there's no need for such formalities between us. Old Taciturn’s disciple, Meng Family boy, we actually share some connections.” The old man chuckled, warmth returning to his aged eyes. “My surname is Gai. Just call me Elder Gai.”

Lu Yang handed him the introductory letter addressed to the Corpse-Driving Sect. “This is a letter for you from Fourth Elder.”

“It’s been ages since I’ve seen Xie Shanren’s letters. His handwriting truly delights the eye and is worth a fortune. This letter alone can earn a sport in an auction... Hmm, you’ve opened this letter?” Elder Gai was displeased. These juniors really don’t know etiquette. How could they casually open letters between seniors?

“We didn’t open it. It was Valley Leader Shuang,” Lu Yang explained helplessly.

“She-devil?” Elder Gai’s hands trembled at the mention of Valley Leader Shuang. He hastily scanned the letter repeatedly with his spiritual consciousness, fearing she might have left some curse to sabotage him.

There was precedent for such cases.

“Thank goodness, the letter is safe... What’s going on? Explain everything to me slowly.”

“Fourth Elder told us to come to Wilderness Province to find a way to resolve the curse. He suggested we consult your esteemed sect first, but it was our first time here, and we were unfamiliar with the place. When we heard that Seven-Emotions Valley is impressive in the art of curses, we decided to make a trip there first...”

Elder Gai’s eyelid twitched uncontrollably. Newborn calves do not fear tigers—these youths don’t know what fear is! You are old Taciturn’s disciple, yet you went looking for Shuang Feiyan with Xie Shanren’s recommendation letter. It’s like you weren’t happy about being alive!

Especially at the end of the letter, Xie Shanren refers to Shuang Feiyan as ‘she-devil,’ a nickname only used in private. No one dares say it to her face.

For this boy to stand before me completely unscathed...he certainly has extraordinary luck.

“Old Lu can handle the matter of your curse, but you’ll have to wait. He’s currently in seclusion and attempting to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Once he succeeds, your curse will no longer be any trouble.”

“Break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” The group gasped in unison.

Sect Leader Lu was similar in age to the Taciturn Daoist Priest and other elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect. In fact, most sect leaders and elders of various factions were of roughly the same seniority, secretly competing to see who would break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage first. They hadn’t expected Sect Leader Lu to pull ahead.

Lu Yang was the first to respond, stepping forward with cupped fists. “Shall I inform our elders so that they can celebrate with Sect Leader Lu?”

Given the friendly terms between the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Corpse-Driving Sect, Sect Leader Lu’s breakthrough to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage was considered a grand joyous occasion. It was only proper for the Dao-Seeking Sect to send representatives to congratulate them. However, his and Meng Jingzhou’s statuses weren’t sufficient to officially represent their sect.

Elder Gai waved his hand. “No need. Before his seclusion, Old Lu specifically instructed me not to tell anyone about his breakthrough. He wants it to be a surprise. I have told you, but keep it to yourselves.”

1. A direct translation of his name would be “road eight thousand.” ☜

Chapter 423: Ghost Calamities

“Old Lu should break through in three to five days. You just have to wait.

“Recently, Hanshui City has seen multiple ghost calamities. If you’ve nothing much to do these few days, you could catch ghosts around the city. They can be converted to contribution points when you return to the sect. I’ll write you a letter of proof.” Elder Gai chuckled, showing considerable favor to these three juniors.

“Ghost calamities?” Lu Yang was bewildered. With a provincial governor overseeing Hanshui City and the Corpse-Driving Sect’s support, what kind of ghosts would dare show themselves?

Elder Gai sighed. “Wasn’t the previous provincial governor reported and arrested? A whole group of officials was also implicated, leading to a major reshuffling of personnel in Wilderness Province’s bureaucracy.

“Right when this happened, numerous ghost calamities emerged throughout Hanshui City. Even rules can’t suppress them completely. It’s probably due to Fusion cultivators opposing us in secret.

“The newly appointed provincial governor could barely stabilize his footing before this crisis hit. His countermeasures weren’t appropriate, and the ghost calamities couldn’t be contained.

“Since the Nine-Netherworlds Creed specializes in commanding ghosts, the provincial governor suspects they are secretly responsible. Strict investigations are ongoing, though they have yet to produce significant results.

“The Corpse-Driving Sect is a renowned major sect in Wilderness Province. We should naturally take responsibility by encouraging disciples to handle these ghost calamities. These ghost scourges are not low-level enough for you to manage. Of course, you can also choose to stay here and study Corpse-Driving Techniques. The choice is yours.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged glances, spotting the suspicion flashing in each other’s eyes.

How could the Nine-Netherworlds Creed be secretly responsible? They’re too busy running the barbeque business to stir up trouble. Are they dissatisfied with how much money they’re raking in?

No matter who has caused the ghost calamities, as Dao-Seeking Sect disciples, we ought to deal with it.

After the group bid goodbye to Elder Gai, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s voice echoed in Lu Yang’s mind. “That old man just now wasn’t a living person but a walking corpse. The craftsmanship is pretty brilliant.”

“Who?” Lu Yang thought he had misheard.

“The old man we just met.”

Lu Yang’s mind raced through countless possibilities before locking onto the most chilling one. Elder Gai had died, yet no one knew, and someone refined his corpse to create the illusion that he’s still alive.

“Brother Zhao, I saw that Elder Gai seemed a bit...unusual,” Lu Yang probed cautiously.

Zhao Po gave him a thumbs-up. “Keen eyes, Brother Lu! You actually saw through that! The one seated just now wasn’t my shifu but a walking corpse he refined.”

“What’s this about?” Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu perked up with interest.

Zhao Po explained cheerfully, “Since we Corpse Drivers constantly come into contact with corpse energy and deathly energy, our bodies lose the yin-yang balance, where yin energy rises while yang energy weakens, causing us to become frail. Even ordinary cultivators have stronger physiques than us, much less physique cultivators like Brother Meng.

“A Corpse Driver’s entire cultivation is reflected in their refined walking corpses. For safety reasons, once Corpse Drivers reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage, they stop showing up in person, letting the walking corpses do so in their stead. It’s not just my shifu who does that. All the elders in the sect interact with the outside world through walking corpses. No one knows where their true bodies are.

“Besides, most Corpse Drivers dislike socializing, fear strangers, and are reticent. Using walking corpses to act on their behalf suits them perfectly, so why wouldn’t they do that?” Corpse Drivers interacted with corpses all year round and were mostly introverted. Zhao Po was an outlier.

“So that’s how it is.” Lu Yang realized he had overcomplicated matters.

“Shall we visit our sect’s study hall first, or should I accept some missions, and we can go settle the ghost calamities together?”

Lu Yang’s lips curled into a smirk as he declared solemnly, “Settling the ghost calamities naturally takes priority! Old Meng has a Single’s Spirit Root and Double Single’s Golden Cores—any ghost that sees his pure yang body will flee without a trace! With Old Meng stepping in, taking care of these ghost calamities will be easy!”

Although Lu Yang rarely complimented him and was speaking the truth, Meng Jingzhou just couldn’t bring himself to be happy. You’re the one with a Single’s Spirit Root! Your whole family has Single’s Spirit Roots!

Sometimes, Meng Jingzhou genuinely wanted to pummel Lu Yang with a set of the Single’s Curse Fist, but he didn’t dare to do so. His instincts warn him that if he went through with it, it would exacerbate his karmic backlash. It’d be truly irreversible then.

Hmph, Lu Yang? Just you wait, I’ll let you have a taste of fist techniques once I ascend to an immortal!

“Does that mean we can accept any Golden Core missions?” Zhao Po pondered. With us four Golden Core cultivators stepping in, we can easily sweep through the Golden Core ghost calamities missions.

Lu Yang waved his hand. “Be bolder and think bigger. We can take on Nascent Soul missions too.”

Zhao Po was stunned, but he soon understood. If the four of us join hands, dealing with Nascent Soul ghosts should be no problem. “Alright, I’ll get the Nascent Soul missions then. Please wait here briefly.”

After Zhao Po stepped away, Lu Yang fished out his Nine-Netherworlds Token to contact Vice Creed Leader Shi.

One of the Heavenly Kings of our Heavenly Court Creed has come across ghost calamities in Hanshui City of Wilderness Province. The provincial governor suspects your creed’s involvement—is this your doing?

After waiting a while, there was still no response. Lu Yang thought Vice Creed Leader Shi was busy and didn’t pay attention to the Nine-Netherworlds Token. Just as he was about to stow it away, it heated up and displayed lengthy text.

Lu Yang didn’t know what to say. “So it wasn’t because he didn’t see my message—he was too busy scribbling away like a madman.”

Vice Leader Shi’s response read:

This is pure slander! Those bastards from the imperial court are placing the blame on us and dumping a basin of poop on our heads again! Our creed leader fully agrees with what you have proposed, Young Creed Leader Lu. With the Nine-Netherworlds Creed shortage of powerful cultivators, we should concentrate on cultivation to increase the number of cultivators from the Fusion to the Transcendent Tribulation stages. All our creed’s activities have come to a standstill while we focus on opening chain stores and expanding our franchise to earn money. This is the creed leader’s decision.

~~~

At a branch of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, Vice Creed Leader Shi fumed after reading Lu Yang’s question. “We don’t even have time to earn money, so where would we find the time to cause ghost calamities? What would we gain? This is not the first or second time the imperial court is slandering us! Whenever there are unexplained incidents, they’ll pin it on us diabolic creeds! As if we’d have spare time for this!” He ranted while replying to Lu Yang. If the Heavenly Court Creed misunderstands that our creed didn’t care about the big picture and acted on our own, it will jeopardize future collaboration.

After he was done, he felt the need to explain a bit more to Lu Yang, but found that the Nine Netherworlds Token was no longer working. “Five-day cooldown? So troublesome.”

Vice Creed Leader reclined against his chair and gazed at the ceiling when he suddenly slapped his forehead. “Hai, why am I worrying about this? Isn’t the creed leader in Wilderness Province?”

Producing another Nine-Netherworlds Token, he relayed Lu Yang’s message and asked the creed leader how he intended to handle the issue.

The creed leader’s reply came swiftly:

I’m in Hanshui City.

Chapter 424: Lu Yang: It’s My Turn to Shine

“To the southeast of Hanshui City, a couple resided in a small village called Baishui Village, where. One early morning, the husband Liu San woke up and realized his wife hadn’t woken him up as usual. He tried calling his wife a few times but to no avail, so he began searching for her. In the end, he discovered his wife had drowned in a water basin.

“The coroner noted that there were no signs of struggle when the wife died, as if she had willingly drowned herself. Baffled, he reported it to the higher-ups, and after a round of investigation, the authorities concluded that it was the work of Drowned Ghosts.

“Drowned Ghosts refer to those who drowned with resentment in their hearts and happened to encounter yin energy at death, becoming ghosts that haunt the world. They typically inhabit bodies of water—rivers, lakes, and oceans. Coincidentally, there is a frigid pool near Baishui Village. The water is so cold that long-term consumption would make mortals ill, and the yin energy is extremely dense, suitable for Drowned Ghosts to dwell.

“A Golden Core senior brother passed by on the way back to his sect. Hearing about this matter, he headed to the frigid pool and sent a walking corpse to go underwater and capture the Drowned Ghost. However, that Drowned Ghost proved formidable and was at least at the Half-Step Nascent Soul Stage or even the Basic Nascent Soul Stage.

“With Hanshui City plagued by excessive ghost calamities, the authorities and sects were stretched too thin to deploy additional forces to deal with the Drowned Ghost.

“Well? Shall we take on this mission?” Zhao Po summarized the mission he had found and asked Lu Yang’s trio.

Meng Jingzhou felt that a mere Drowned Ghost posed no challenge. “That doesn’t sound difficult. Do you have anything more challenging?”

“There’s a female ghost seeking a ghost marriage—”

“The Drowned Ghost then,” Meng Jingzhou hastily interrupted. You must be joking. With my current state, female ghosts will either find me an eyesore and not even show themselves, or find me an eyesore and slap me to death.

“Alright then, let’s set off.” Zhao Po distributed one talisman to each of the three before departing.

“What are these talismans?”

“These are Soul-Dispelling Talismans. They are specially crafted by our sect and distributed to every disciple who deals with the ghost calamities. The sect discovered how tough it was to eradicate ghosts permanently. Even if the malevolent ghosts are beaten into a weak state, without appropriate countermeasures, it’s still hard to kill them. Working with the talisman masters and ghost-catching Daoist priests, they created these talismans overnight.”

The disciples of the Corpse-Driving Sects were Corpse Drivers and practiced yin-attribute cultivation techniques similar to malevolent ghosts. They could defeat ghosts but struggled to kill them.

“Once we defeat the Drowned Ghost, we can activate this talisman to finish it off!”

“Your sect’s really thought of everything.” Lu Yang chuckled as he stowed away the Soul-Dispelling Talisman. Actually, this is hardly necessary for us. With Meng Jingzhou—the bane of ghosts—here, we can even burn the ghosts to death. Both the Pure Yang True Fire and the Three Flavor True Fire suppressed malevolent ghosts.

~~~

The frigid pool was diagonally across Hanshui City from the Corpse-Driving Sect. After the group set off, they directly traveled through Hanshui City and passed by One More Time Barbeque Shop, which was still in its soft opening phase.

Hanshui City was still flourishing and bustling with people, largely unaffected by the ghost calamities. One reason was the sheer number of people in Hanshui City, which generated overwhelming yang energy, deterring ghosts from entering and wreaking havoc. The second reason was that even returning home wasn’t necessarily safe. A single door couldn’t block malevolent ghosts bent on causing trouble, so public spaces became comparatively safer.

Following the location in the mission description, the four people and one walking corpse passed by Baishui Village and reached the frigid pool.

Standing beside the pool, the four could sense its chilliness. The frigid pool was surrounded by mountains on three sides and shielded from sunlight all year round. Dense vegetation covered the area, with several old locust trees particularly conspicuous. These various factors had resulted in water turning frigid.

Though the water was crystal clear, one still couldn’t see the bottom and determine the Drowned Ghost’s position.

“How strange. Why is there not a single fish?” Meng Jingzhou was puzzled. Logically speaking, such places should be teeming with fish. I wouldn’t be surprised even if a giant fish weighing 180 jin appears here.

“Were they all eaten by ghosts? Since when do ghosts eat fish?”

Lu Yang pushed aside Meng Jingzhou, stopping his endless stream of questions. He crouched down and observed the frigid pool. “Stop caring about whether you get to eat fish. Ask about it only after we’ve caught it. Now, the real question is: who can swim and lure the malevolent ghost out?”

The four exchanged glances. Lu Yang had a Sword Spirit Root, Meng Jingzhou had a Single’s Spirit Root, Man Gu was an Ancient Barbarian, while Zhao Po was a Corpse Driver—none were swimmers.

“I’ll do it! I’ll get my walking corpse to go down!” Zhao Po lit three incense sticks and bowed to the walking corpse thrice. As the walking corpse absorbed the scent, its pallid skin gained a hint of ruddiness, and its hollow eyes flickered with a trace of spiritedness.

The walking corpse jumped into the frigid pool, sending ripples across the previously still surface. Evidently, the walking corpse had found the Drowned Ghost and was in the middle of a battle.

A ghost’s strength stemmed from the fear in living beings’ hearts and the frailty of their souls, but neither of these had the slightest effect on walking corpses.

Zhao Po’s forehead glistened with cold sweat as his teeth chattered uncontrollably. Since he could sync with his walking corpse’s senses, he could feel how powerful the malevolent ghost was, and the pressure on him multiplied.

“Brother Zhao?” Lu Yang asked in concern.

“The intelligence was wrong! The Drowned Ghost down there is not at the Half-Step or Basic Nascent Soul stages, but at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage! The walking corpse also sees a female corpse, likely the wife from Baishui Village who drowned!

“It’s luring the ghost up now. Ready yourselves!” Zhao Po hollered.

Lu Yang’s trio immediately assumed combat stances, poised to unleash devastating attacks the moment the Drowned Ghost surfaced.

With a thunderous explosion, a figure leaped out of the water.

“Three Flavor True Fire!”

“Pure Yang True Fire!”

“Tyrannical Barbarian King Fist!”

The three’s simultaneous assaults nearly struck home before Zhao Po frantically yelled, “Stop stop stop! That’s not the Drowned Ghost but my walking corpse!”

Hastily redirected, the attacks crashed into the cliffside, sending boulders tumbling in a deafening avalanche.

“Where’s the Drowned Ghost?” Lu Yang was perplexed.

Zhao Po revealed an embarrassed grin. “I was too loud when shouting to ready yourselves just now. The Drowned Ghost heard it and knew there was an ambush, so it fled back.”

“That complicates things. Now that he’s wary, he won’t take the bait again.” Man Gu was troubled and at a loss for what to do.

Meng Jingzhou suggested, “Why don’t we drain the water with our storage rings?”

“Zhao Po shook his head. “That won’t do. This frigid pool has already become the Drowned Ghost’s territory. Storage rings can’t absorb owned items.”

Lu Yang flashed a confident smirk. “Leave this to me. It’s time to showcase the unique art I’ve diligently practiced for days!”

Meng Jingzhou inquired curiously, “What shady and heretical spells have you picked up this time?”

“This mighty ability is famous! You’ll recognize it right away!” Lu Yang adopted an air of mystery that only scratched Meng Jingzhou’s curiosity.

“Quick, show it to me!”

Lu Yang paced by the edge of the pool, channeling his powers to stir a breeze beneath his robes, such that his fluttering robes gave him the image of someone about to metamorphose and ascend to an immortal. “Listen well, the malevolent ghost down there! This humble Daoist is giving you one last chance. If you still don’t emerge, don’t blame me for resorting to my methods!”

The water remained completely calm.

Lu Yang had already expected no response from the Drowned Ghost. He flipped his palm and pressed it against the water's surface before lifting it sharply. The water formed a waterspout that whirled into his palm, revealing the Drowned Ghost right at the bottom of the frigid pool.

Turning around, Lu Yang gently flung his sleeves in an unfettered manner. “Behold the technique I’ve finally mastered after days of diligent practice—”

At the sight of this scene, Zhao Po stood transfixed with his mouth agape, unable to utter a word for a long while. “Th-this is the legendary Sleeve Cosmos!” He absorbed the entire pool of water with a mere flick of his sleeve. What else could this be if not Sleeve Cosmos?

“...Right, this is Sleeve Cosmos!”

Chapter 425: Arhat Fist’s Stellar Results

Before Zhao Po could recover from his astonishment, the four of them sensed a vast and sinister spirit energy rising from the depths of the pool.

A drenched malevolent ghost whose feet were tangled with algae flew out, looking at Lu Yang with a tinge of wariness in his frosty gaze. “Good good good! To have mastered Sleeve Cosmos at such a young age! Truly a remarkable genius befitting the treasure-laden Great Xia Dynasty!” The Drowned Ghost’s face was deathly pale as it stared fixedly at Lu Yang, convinced he was the greatest threat.

There was no fluctuation of magical treasures, which means it must have been a spatial spell. Since he absorbed the entire pool into his sleeve, it could only have been Sleeve Cosmos! To have mastered such a difficult spell at the Golden Core Stage—what kind of peerless genius is this?!

Lu Yang’s eyes narrowed slightly as he bellowed, “Oh, is that to say you’re not a malevolent ghost native to Great Xia? Where did you come from, and why have you appeared in Hanshui City?!”

The Drowned Ghost sneered, brushing off Lu Yang’s interrogation. “Why should I tell you?” These young fellows are talented in spells, but with a major cultivation realm separating us, what makes them think they can defeat me?

They have no idea where they stand.

With that, the Drowned Ghost turned and fled.

Let’s be real—why choose fight when I can choose flight?

“Trying to run? Take my fist!” Meng Jingzhou struck first, unleashing the Arhat Fist. Buddhist chants reverberated as Pure Yang True Fire wreathed his knuckles, pulsing with power.

“Damn, it burns!” The Drowned Ghost hadn’t expected such speed from Meng Jingzhou. A moment of carelessness, and he suffered the blow head-on. Buddhist cultivation techniques and Pure Yang True Fire were supremely effective in countering ghosts. With both combined, the Drowned Ghost stood no chance!

“A Golden Core cultivator displaying combat power of a Nascent Soul cultivator? And this move... You’re not from the Corpse-Driving Sect!” Underestimating his enemies had cost the Drowned Ghost the initiative. “Looks like I won’t be able to leave unless I deal with you brats!” The Drowned Ghost gnashed his teeth, reluctant to stir trouble.

“Hmph! You drowned a mortal in a water basin, yet you still want to flee?”

“Damn it! What’s it to you if I drown some mortal? You Great Xia cultivators are a pain!” The Drowned Ghost cursed out loud. Water was his domain, but Lu Yang had taken it away. He didn’t want to fight under such circumstances.

But since I can’t escape now, I might as well just fight!

“Abyssal Swamp!” An inky water domain as thick as blood spread from the Drowned Ghost’s feet, reaching the four in the blink of an eye.

A bone-piercing cold crept from the soles of their feet to their skulls, and moving required tremendous effort. Worse, contact with the inky water domain made one’s breathing labored, as if one was suffocating.

Golden Core cultivators could do away with breathing by sustaining themselves through internal circulation, so they shouldn’t feel any suffocation, yet the inky water domain could drown them regardless.

Lu Yang pressed his index and middle fingers together and shouted, “Break!”

The inky water domain receded, and everyone regained their senses. It had been an illusion, a common method of Drowned Ghosts, and Lu Yang’s cultivation technique happened to counter illusions!

With the illusion shattered, countless waterweeds tried to ensnare them. This was precisely why the Drowned Ghost had drowned; now, it had become one of his abilities.

“Sweep!” The Qingfeng Sword stabbed the ground, and boundless sword energy severed the roots of the waterweeds.

“Attack together! Slashing Word Mantra!”

“Arhat Fist!”

“Tyrannical Barbarian King Fist!”

The three struck the Drowned Ghost simultaneously. He swayed slightly, leaving an afterimage as his true body flashed behind Man Gu. A chunk of waterweeds appeared in the ghost’s hand and coiled around Man Gu’s neck.

This kid looks simple and gullible—he should be the easiest target.

Man Gu didn’t bother looking behind as he jerked his head backward and smashed the Drowned Ghost dizzy, forcing him to release his grip on the waterweeds.

The battle resumed, with three peerless prodigies besieging an evil Nascent Soul ghost, leaving Zhao Po unsure how to step in and help. There’s no way I can intervene—it’s a battle at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“Aren’t we all supposed to be Golden Core cultivators?” Zhao Po wondered if his Golden Core cultivation was fake.

“Arhat Fist!” Lu Yang also unleashed his own version, infused with Three Flavor True Fire.

The Drowned Ghost was prepared and dodged repeatedly, but Lu Yang weaved Shrinking Earth into his fists, tunneling around in the soil unpredictably, and one punch landed square on the ghost’s shoulder.

Unable to care about the pain from the true fire and fist techniques, the Drowned Ghost realized something far more terrifying.

“My hair!”

The Drowned Ghost’s distinctive sodden and clumped hair was now falling out uncontrollably under the effects of the Arhat Fist.

“Hmm, it works on ghosts too.” Lu Yang was slightly surprised. He purely wanted to use Buddhist spells to restrain the evil ghost, not planning for him to lose his hair.

“Eighteen Successive Hammer Strikes!” Man Gu whipped out a giant hammer that blared Words of Sages while he madly pummeled the Drowned Ghost.

“You’re a damned Confucian cultivator?!” The Drowned Ghost’s expression shifted drastically at the vast righteous qi naturally emitted from the giant hammer.

Prolonged studying of Confucian classics could nurture a righteous aura of a gentleman. Although Man Gu’s learning progress had been slow, his attitude was commendable. Thus, his persistent studying had endowed him with the vast righteous qi of a gentleman.

The trio’s attacks brimmed with potent yang energy, causing the lingering yin aura above the pool to grow increasingly sparse. If the fight went on, they might even completely disperse the accumulated yin energy!

The Drowned Ghost flew into a rage. I’ve painstakingly found this perfect haunt, only to have these three ruin everything. “You...cough...don’t...cough...force me...cough... Stop fighting, I surrender!” He spat out.

Had the battle been one-on-one, Lu Yang would have used his Unbeatable Golden Core to expedite the process. But three against one? It was complete domination; he didn’t need to use his Unbeatable Golden Core at all.

The Drowned Ghost sprawled limply on the ground, looking like he had given up on life.

Arhat Fist, true fire, vast righteous qi... The Drowned Ghost wondered if he’d forgotten to check the almanac today. There are only these few ghost-countering methods in existence, yet I’d somehow encountered every single one.

No home-field advantage, specialized anti-ghost methods, and geniuses who can fight above their level—if I could still win, that’d be the true ghost![1]

“That’s it? We won?” Zhao Po approached with his walking corpse, still trying to process what had happened. The battle had begun and ended so quickly that I couldn’t keep up at all.

Zhao Po did not lack talent, but he was still a step behind Lu Yang’s trio in ability, and many steps behind in experience. Although he often roamed the jianghu and had experienced much of its affairs, it paled in comparison to the three who casually infiltrated diabolic creeds and challenged beyond their level.

Lu Yang fished out the Soul-Dispelling Talisman, sending the Drowned Ghost staggering backward in terror.

“Wait, wait! No matter what I’ve done, I don’t deserve this kind of punishment!”

Lu Yang was unmoved, his hands not pausing. “You drowned a person, yet you have the face to claim that you don’t deserve this kind of punishment?”

“It’s fake! All fake! She’s not dead. Look at the bottom of the pool if you don’t believe me! She’s well and alive!” the Drowned Ghost shrieked in panic.

Lu Yang peered downward and indeed saw a living woman below. Looks like the walking corpse had jumped to conclusions and mistakenly assumed she was dead.

Channeling his spirit energy outward, Lu Yang formed a giant hand to retrieve the woman, placing her beside the Drowned Ghost.

“Alright, time to talk. What’s going on?”

1. The expression here mainly means that it’d be extremely strange if he could still win, something like “if pigs fly,” but the character for “ghost” is used here, so I tried my best to integrate it. ☜

Chapter 426: What Would a Ghost Need Money For?

“Which faction do you belong to, malevolent ghost? Are you from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” Zhao Po interrogated the Drowned Ghost by borrowing the trio’s authority like a fox exploiting the might of a tiger.

The Drowned Ghost shook his head vigorously, emphasizing he had no malicious intentions. “I ended up here purely by accident. Really.

“I was originally a fisherman from the East Sea. After drowning, my resentment turned me into a grievous soul. By chance, my corpse came across a Yin-Wind Stone, and I became a Drowned Ghost.

“The East Sea is boundless, teeming with countless living beings. Thus, I secretly fed on the yang energy from the various races in the sea, gradually elevating my cultivation. From a Drowned Ghost who couldn’t face sunlight, I advanced to a Qi-Training Drowned Ghost with some self-protection ability.

“Once I could protect myself, I grew complacent. When I wandered the East Sea, I leaped out of the water to scare people from time to time. My courage grew, and I wanted to venture into the deeper waters I’d never dared approach in life. Right after I left the safe shallows, I encountered a fish king that was one hundred jin in weight. It simply opened its mouth, and I almost got sucked in.

“I knew that wouldn’t do, so I fled back to safe waters, swearing never to leave again! In the safe zone, I slowly cultivated, swallowing yang energy from schools of fish and occasionally stealing offerings from fishermen. We fishermen had traditions of making offerings to the East Sea, but since I’d drowned anyway, it was evident that those rituals to the East Sea didn’t guarantee one’s safety, so I had no qualms about eating the offerings.

“Eventually, I lost track of my cultivation realm, so I mindlessly cultivated without interacting with anyone. One day, I ran into a cultivator who wanted to capture and refine me. I chased him away effortlessly and took his storage rings and some cultivation manuals. After studying the cultivation techniques, I realized I had already reached the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. At the time, I’d been dead for two hundred years.

“With clearer directions in my cultivation, I continued cultivating. Eight hundred years passed, and I finally reached the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage. All this time, I never once left the safe sea region.

“My plan was to venture out after reaching the Divine Transfiguration Stage, but who would have expected what happened next? Someone ambushed me and knocked me out with a single slap, and when I woke up, I was already in this deep pool.”

Lu Yang interrupted the Drowned Ghost’s account. “In other words, you’re saying you have no idea who brought you here?”

“Yes, I have no idea.”

“Does that person have any distinguishing features?”

“Stronger than me.”

“...Continue your story.”

“It took me days to understand my situation. It turned out that this was near Hanshui City in the Great Xia Dynasty’s Wilderness Province, the western edge of the Central Continent and countless li away from the East Sea.

“With my situation, I couldn’t exactly board a flying vessel or something, so I could only stay here. While scouting the area, I met a married couple in Baishui Village. The man was called Liu San, and the woman was called Huang Zao’er—this woman right here.” The Drowned Ghost pointed at the unconscious woman lying beside him.

“At first, the two of them were very scared of me. But once they realized I meant no harm, they grew bold. They asked if I could fake Huang Zao’er’s drowning to help them commit insurance fraud, offering me a share of the payout. I was penniless and in urgent need of money then, so I agreed.

“With my abilities, faking Huang Zao’er’s drowning was extremely easy. Even the coroner couldn’t discern it. After obtaining the payout, Huang Zao’er was ‘buried,’ but she was actually hiding here with me. The husband and wife intended to leave Baishui Village once the heat died down and start anew in another city.

“But I totally didn’t expect that it’s the height of a crackdown on ghost disturbances and that the imperial court is partnering with some Corpse-Driving Sect to target ghosts like me.

“I didn’t want to stir up trouble, so I’d flee at the sight of people or scare them off if escape wasn’t possible. A few days ago, I frightened away a Golden Core cultivator. And now, the four of you Golden Core cultivators show up!” The Drowned Ghost looked utterly aggrieved. This measly bit of insurance payout nearly cost me my life!

The four weren’t about to take the Drowned Ghost’s side of the story at face value. Lu Yang asked, “Why is Huang Zao’er unconscious?”

“I did that. Keeping her awake and living freely in the water drained too much power. Knocking her unconscious and encasing her in a protective bubble was more efficient.”

“Wake her.”

“Roger.” The Drowned Ghost complied, flicking a glowing finger to wake Huang Zao’er up.

Still muddle-headed and clueless about what was going on, Huang Zao’er was overwhelmed to suddenly find herself surrounded by four people and a walking corpse. Having never faced such an intimidating lineup before, she answered every question, largely corroborating the ghost’s account—she and her husband had conspired with the Drowned Ghost to commit insurance fraud.

“Wait, that doesn’t add up.” Meng Jingzhou narrowed his eyes, spotting the loophole in the Drowned Ghost’s confession. “What would a ghost need money for?”

Ghostly entities’ thick yin energy made mortals instinctively feel uncomfortable, which made them overly conspicuous. Even entering a city was extremely challenging and required significant effort to conceal themselves, let alone purchasing items on the streets.

As for visiting merchant guilds, that was all the more impossible. These guilds were filled with cultivators who could see through the ghosts’ disguises at a glance.

Besides, how much could a mortal’s insurance payout be? Summing them up might still not be worth a few spirit stones. He’s an almighty Intermediate Nascent Soul ghost who once stirred up waves in the East Sea. What use would he have for this paltry amount of money?

Look at Little Five, Little Six, and Little Seven. These three alluring ghosts go from house to house and serve households the whole night without charging any money.

“How audacious! You still dared lie to us!” Meng Jingzhou’s body erupted in true fire as he glared at the Drowned Ghost with ire.

“I really didn’t lie! Even ghosts have uses for money!” the Drowned Ghost wailed in protest. “Look, I was a fisherman, drowned in the sea, and have lived there forever—I’m a seawater ghost! Now, I’m stuck in this frigid pool. Although the yin energy is sufficient, it’s still freshwater. I’m not used to living here.

“So I had Liu San and his wife use the insurance payout they scammed to buy salt and pour it into the pool. That way, the pool would turn from freshwater to saltwater!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Man Gu, “...”

Zhao Po, “...”

This was their first time hearing that water ghosts were categorized into seawater and freshwater ghosts.

Lu Yang secretly transmitted an auditory message to Zhao Po. “You’ve got many ghosts in Wilderness Province. Have you ever heard of water ghosts being categorized into seawater and freshwater ghosts?”

“Our Wilderness Province is separated from the East Sea by an entire continent. This is my first time meeting an East Sea ghost.” Zhao Po felt like his knowledge wasn’t cutting it anymore.

Man Gu was used to such situations and even took pride in them. Following Brother Lu and Brother Meng really allows me to broaden my horizons everywhere I go.

Meanwhile, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was rolling about on her bed, kicking her feet in laughter at Lu Yang’s lack of imagination. “That's because you haven’t seen enough! Have you forgotten the two types of first-grade golden cores I told you about? One is called ‘Three Rivers Five Lakes Golden Core,’ and the other is called ‘Boundless Sea Golden Core.’ The key difference is that one uses saltwater and the other uses freshwater!

The Drowned Ghost was still desperate to prove the veracity of his words. Your Excellency, didn’t you absorb the pool water with Sleeve Cosmos earlier? Just taste it and you’ll know!”

Lu Yang’s face darkened. “Then where has the fish in the pool gone?”

“It was so salty that they died.”[1]

1. The original expression is often used when saying a dish is too salty. Here, it also takes on the literal meaning. ☜

Chapter 427: Strong Huang Ming

Having pieced together the whole story, Lu Yang and his two junior brothers stayed behind while Zhao Po took his walking corpse to Baishui Village and captured Liu San, who was packing his belongings to flee. Corpse Drivers held special status in Wilderness Province, and Zhao Po was among the most orthodox of them, making him the most suitable candidate to seize Liu San without many obstacles or questions.

“Hey hey hey! What are you doing?”

Lu Yang flashed a standard eight-tooth smile. “Sending you to the yamen.”

“I told you I didn’t kill anyone!”

“Who said only murder gets punished? Insurance fraud is a crime too. You even turned the pool into saltwater and choked the fish to death. Charging you with the additional crime of environmental damage is totally justified!”

“Great Xia even puts ghosts on trial?”

Lu Yang grinned proudly. “Not just ghosts! Even the Sect Leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Minister of Justice got thrown in prison when they broke the law!”

Zhao Po was flabbergasted. I’ve never heard of something like this.

Don’t the Five Great Immortal Sects have enforcement authority? How could their leaders be arrested?

And the Minister of Justice knows the law best, yet he still knowingly broke it?

Is this a secret only known to immortal sect disciples?

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu stared at Lu Yang in surprise; they hadn’t known about this matter either. Only the Xia Emperor, the entire Ministry of Justice, Yun Zhi, and Lu Yang were privy to this.

“Put on trial? Junior Brother Zhao Po, is this how you complete missions assigned to you by the sect?” A cold voice sounded from above.

A man hovered in the air with an arrogant expression. Next to him was a walking corpse shrouded in black robes.

“Senior Brother Huang Ming?” Zhao Po immediately recognized the person who had defeated him and became the sect’s top disciple.

Huang Ming slowly descended with his walking corpse, scowling at Zhao Po with discontent. “The sect’s mission requirements should be the complete eradication of ghosts. Why are you sparing this one? If you’re too soft-hearted to kill a living being, let your senior brother do it in your stead!” He suddenly produced a Soul-Dispelling Talisman, aiming it at the Drowned Ghost.

Zhao Po reacted faster. He strode forward and stood in front of the ghost, preventing Huang Ming from making a move. “Senior Brother Huang, ghosts too can be good and evil. This Drowned Ghost hasn’t committed any heinous crime to warrant death!”

“Preposterous! I don’t care about good and evil ghosts and whatnot. I only know that the sect demands the elimination of all ghost calamities!” Huang Ming narrowed his eyes. “Zhao Po, you insist on obstructing me?”

As conflict threatened to break out, Lu Yang interposed himself between the two. “Fellow Daoist, you’re senior and junior brothers of the same sect. There’s no need to make things this tense, right?”

Huang Ming remained unmoved. “And who are you?”

“I’m Lu Yang of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Huang Ming sneered. “I was wondering who it was. Turns out you’re that Dao-Seeking Sect who bullied weaker opponents at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony. What, does the Dao-Seeking Sect want to meddle in the affairs of our Corpse-Driving Sect now?

“I’m disciplining a junior brother in the capacity of a senior brother. What right does an outsider like you have to interfere?!”

Man Gu bristled at his words, but Meng Jingzhou restrained him.

Meng Jingzhou sensed that Huang Ming seemed to be unusually hostile toward them.

Lu Yang maintained his perfect smile. “We were the ones who captured this Drowned Ghost, so his disposition is naturally ours to decide. On the contrary, Fellow Daoist, for you to suddenly swoop in and pick our fruits, doesn’t that show a lack of upbringing?”

“Heh, four Golden Core cultivators had to join hands just to subdue one Intermediate Nascent Soul Drowned Ghost? And you feel no shame to brag about it? If it were me, I alone would have sufficed! Yet people call you the number one of our generation? I fail to see anything special.”

Lu Yang's smile didn’t waver. “Oh, is that so? Looks like you’re very confident in your cultivation, Fellow Daoist.”

“Test me and you’ll know.”

No sooner had he spoken than Lu Yang unleashed an Arhat Fist strike at Huang Ming.

Clang!

The walking corpse moved faster, crossing its arms like an iron tower to block the blow.

Lu Yang was slightly surprised. Although I didn’t use my full power, a Golden Core cultivator shouldn’t have been able to block this strike.

The walking corpse roared, its body swelling as it attempted to grapple with Lu Yang.

Rather than engaging with the walking corpse directly, Lu Yang stomped the ground. His body vanished underground before reappearing behind Huang Ming.

Better to deal with the walking corpse’s master than fight with the walking corpse!

“Arhat Fist!”

“Yellow Springs Palm!”

Huang Ming seemed to have anticipated Lu Yang’s move, accumulating power in his palm and turning around to deliver an attack.

The fist and palm collided, sending shockwaves through the air. Both parties couldn’t withstand the brunt and staggered backward as the forces of the fist and palm raged through their bodies. The two simultaneously made the same decision, expelling the forces by striking with their palms backward.

Lu Yang’s eyes narrowed with interest. It’s my first time meeting an opponent with such rich combat experience.

“How is this possible?!” Zhao Po stared at this scene in disbelief. Corpse Drivers are typically weaker than average in physique. I’ve seen Brother Lu’s fist techniques. Yet Senior Brother Huang Ming’s palms could trade blows palm-to-palm with Lu Yang!

“You’re not at the Basic Golden Core Stage, are you? Intermediate Golden Core Stage?” Lu Yang smirked, recalling Zhao Po mentioning that both he and Huang Ming were at the Basic Golden Core Stage.

“How did you tell?”

“I put my full strength into this fist strike. If a Basic Golden Core cultivator could withstand it, I would have cultivated in vain.”

Huang Ming snorted without confirming. I didn’t expect Lu Yang to be so tough to deal with, or should I say, troublesome.

“My hair!”

Just as Huang Ming was about to make another move, he noticed strands of hair floating down like snow.

“Fist and Spell As One?!” Huang Ming soon recognized this. I didn’t expect someone at the Golden Core Stage to have achieved this.

He didn’t care about his hair; he only cared about Lu Yang’s talent.

“What’s Fist and Spell As One?” Zhao Po was utterly lost.

Meng Jingzhou studied Huang Ming with his brow knitted, remaining silent. Combat experience aside, Huang Ming’s knowledge doesn’t seem to be what the Corpse-Driving Sect could have nurtured, especially considering he only became Sect Leader Lu’s disciple recently.

Where did such knowledge come from?

The two fought again, displaying momentum that exceeded their cultivation realms. Lu Yang attacked with Three Flavor True Fire, while Huang Ming countered with Dingmao True Fire.[1] The temperature spiked, forcing the Drowned Ghost to keep retreating.

“Six Ding Six Jia True Fire!"[2] Zhao Po gasped. Among the 108 True Fires, twelve were grouped as a main category, and they were collectively referred to as the Six Ding Six Jia True Fire, with the Dingmao True Fire being one of them!

Neither the Yellow Springs Palm, which can resist Brother Lu, nor the Dingmao True Fire had been displayed at the sect’s grand tournament.

Zhao Po knew that Huang Ming hadn’t used his full strength at the tournament, but he assumed his trump card was hidden within the walking corpse, not Huang Ming himself.

Lu Yang grew more curious about Huang Ming’s background. The gap between the first and second disciples in the Corpse-Driving Sect is quite big, huh? Beyond the Five Great Immortal Sects, I’ve never met someone who can match me to this extent.

Their battle intensified as they unleashed various spells, techniques, and mighty abilities. Their fists and palms struck thunderously, yet neither gained an advantage.

Gradually, the outcome of the battle revealed itself. Lu Yang’s foundation was more solid, and when it came to endurance battles, no one at the same cultivation realm could beat him.

Huang Ming was enraged. I’ve never been defeated ever since my debut. Who would’ve thought I’d face my first loss today?

No way I’m gonna let that happen!

His tiger-like eyes radiated majestic might as a surge of invisible mental force coalesced into an arrow aimed at Lu Yang.

However, Lu Yang’s mental power was remarkably strong, let alone with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in his mental space. In a competition of mental strength, he would be unfazed even if a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator was here.

A tiny shield materialized at Lu Yang’s brow, deflecting the arrow.

Realization dawned upon the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “I know now! He’s not a peer of the same age but a great cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew!”

1. Dingmao is one of the Six Ding. It is also the name of the fourth year of the sixty-year cycle. ☜

2. The Six Ding and Six Jia refer to twelve warrior/protective gods. ☜

Chapter 428: Dispersing One’s Cultivation to Cultivate Anew

“Dispersing one’s cultivation to cultivate anew?” It was Lu Yang’s first time hearing of this term. The literal meaning is quite easy to grasp though.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied with composure and conviction. “That’s right. Many cultivators receive no guidance at the start of their cultivation, making their cultivation journey rough and their foundation unstable. The consequences may not be severe at lower cultivation realms; at worst, they get outmatched in a battle by someone like you, whose foundation is solid enough to challenge those beyond your level. But once they reach higher cultivation realms, the problems become glaring. They hit bottlenecks easily, stagnating for centuries or even millennia without the slightest progress in their cultivation.

“And at that point, they face a choice—dispersing their cultivation to cultivate anew.” When it came to cultivation knowledge, no one could rival her.

“To disperse one’s cultivation is akin to reincarnation, where one retains their memories but reverts to being an infant, starting over from scratch. With the memories of their cultivation from their last life, they can avoid many mistakes, know how to solidify their foundation, and seize opportunities they once missed due to their overly high cultivation or old age. For outsiders, there’s no way for them to tell if someone has reincarnated and cultivated anew. Even examining their bone age or other methods cannot reveal anything.

“However, dispersing one’s cultivation to cultivate anew comes with three problems. First, it has strict cultivation requirements. One must be at the Fusion Stage and at their peak. That is when their essence, qi, and consciousness can fuse and ensure their true spirit doesn’t extinguish after dispersing their cultivation. If one attempts to disperse their cultivation in old age when their essence, qi, and blood are disoriented, the only outcome is failure, where their soul dissipates and can’t be saved.

“Second, when you cultivate anew, you’re as defenseless as a newborn, incapable of even eating and crawling. Even if you survive infancy, the cultivation world isn’t safe. You never know when you might provoke enemies and meet an untimely end while growing up.

“Third, one’s innate talent and spirit root cannot be guaranteed. For instance, if you used to possess a Dual Spirit Root, but upon beginning anew, you might end up with Triple or even Quadruple spirit roots. Under such circumstances, even with your past cultivation experience, reaching your former heights would be challenging.”

Lu Yang nodded. The concept sounds similar to Li Haoran’s situation, but it’s not exactly the same. At the very least, Li Haoran has been reborn as a completely new individual, with his next life’s talent surpassing the previous one. Each has its pros and cons.

No wonder Huang Ming is so hard to deal with. It’s like fighting a Fusion expert who’s suppressed his cultivation realm to my level.

“By the way, did any of the Five Ancient Immortals disperse their cultivation to cultivate anew?”

“No.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy counted on her fingers. “I was born in a small tribe, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was a refugee, the Nine-Layers Immortal was the first successor of the Lianshan Clan, the Qilin Immortal was nurtured by heaven and earth, and the Epoch Immortal was a Jianmu World Tree that gained sentience.”

Lu Yang asked, “Can you tell who Huang Ming was in his past life, Immortal Fairy?”

She shook her head. “No, I can’t. If not for that mental attack far beyond this cultivation realm, I couldn’t have determined that he’s a reforged cultivator starting afresh.”

Lu Yang pondered. Does the Corpse-Driving Sect know about Huang Ming’s rebirth? Why did he choose to cultivate in the Corpse-Driving Sect? With such talent, he could’ve joined one of the Five Great Immortal Sects. Is he scared of something? Or is there something special about the Corpse-Driving Sect?

“Never mind, let’s not think so much for now.” Lu Yang grinned with excitement as he unsheathed his Qingfeng Sword. This is my first time facing a reforged cultivator—time to get serious.

Huang Ming gazed at Lu Yang solemnly with not a trace of complacency left, as if he was facing a formidable enemy. As a cultivator who had dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew, he couldn’t tolerate defeat at the hands of a junior. That was why he had made an exception by employing the Mental Arrow.

It’s absolutely impossible for an Intermediate Golden Core cultivator to withstand the Mental Arrow, even those who specialize in cultivating their mental power!

How did he do it? Could it be...he’s like me, also a reforged cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew?

Little did he know that when Lu Yang was at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage and had just resurrected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, she had forced him to open a mental space, causing his mental power to be far stronger than his peers of the same age. Subsequently, with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy constantly messing around in his mental space, its size and resilience grew exponentially.

When it came to mental power, no one at the Golden Core Stage could beat Lu Yang.

“Slash!” Lu Yang roared, unifying his essence, spirit, and consciousness. Sword qi brutally erupted like a shining silk, and the dazzling blade carved a ferocious arc in the air as it slashed toward Huang Ming.

Watching from the sidelines, Zhao Po felt his hair stand on end. Even witnessing the sword attack from the side, he could sense its terrifying power. Is this really a sword move that an Intermediate Golden Core cultivator can execute?

The Drowned Ghost also got a fright. Only now did he realize Lu Yang had been holding back during their early battle. Otherwise, this strike alone would have been enough to leave me severely wounded and passed out! freeweɓnøvel~com

The sword strike came too fast and furious for Huang Ming to dodge. If he resisted it head-on, however, defeat would be inevitable. Gritting his teeth, Huang Ming focused on a thought. In a flash, he vanished and was replaced by his walking corpse.

He had switched places with the walking corpse in an instant!

“Corpse Swap Transportation?!” Zhao Po gasped in shock. I didn’t expect Senior Brother Huang Ming to have mastered even a secret spell like this! One can only master it at the Nascent Soul Stage.

Huang Ming panted heavily, swallowing a Qi Restoration Pill to replenish his spirit energy. Forcibly casting the secret spell had instantly drained his remaining spirit energy.

The walking corpse took the full brunt of the sword strike and was cleaved cleanly in two. However, countless crimson threads sprouted from the severed sections and wove together until the puppet returned to normal.

No longer holding back, Huang Ming controlled his walking corpse to attack Lu Yang simultaneously.

Most Corpse Drivers had weak physical bodies and could only engage in combat by controlling their walking corpses. However, Huang Ming possessed both a strong physique and mental power, allowing him to fight personally while controlling his walking corpse, eliminating the typical weakness of Corpse Drivers.

His combat power skyrocketed!

Zhao Po stared blankly at the scene. Every one of Huang Ming’s methods had overturned his understanding. So the gap between us is actually this vast?

“Hah! Now this is interesting!” Despite the fight becoming a two-on-one, Lu Yang showed no intention of backing down. Like a warrior god, he grew more ferocious the more he fought.

“No wonder you could become a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect! You do have some skill. But this is as far as you go!” Huang Ming’s wolf-like eyes gleamed with ruthlessness and resolve.

“With your talent, you’ve probably never tasted defeat among your peers, have you? Today, I’ll let you experience it!” A contemptuous smile played on Huang Ming’s lips.

“Red spider lilies bloom; the cosmos is reshaped!” This was his final and strongest trump card. If I still lose, there’d be no point in having dispersed my cultivation and cultivating anew to compete for clout in the upcoming Great Era—I might as well end my life now.

Brilliant crimson spider lilies blossomed, while Huang Ming and his walking corpse had their eyes turn bloodshot. Their auras surged like bamboo shoots clambering upward, and their nails elongated, resembling the sharp claws of wild beasts. Under such a momentum, even the ground trembled, as if an earth dragon was turning in its sleep and shaking the mountains.

“Two against one! Let’s see how you win now!” Huang Ming’s face twisted, confident that victory was in his grasp.

“It’s indeed getting rough if this keeps up,” Lu Yang muttered before shrinking into the earth. He retrieved the Twin Lotus Seed and activated the Tree Planting Mantra.

Under Huang Ming’s stunned gaze, amid the field of red spider lilies, a lotus bloomed, and from it emerged two Lu Yangs. One wielded the Qingfeng Sword, while the other wielded the Mingyue Sword.

Lu Yang’s mouth curled into a leisurely smile.

“Now it’s two against two.”

Chapter 429: Huang Ming’s Identity

Huang Ming was a Fusion expert who had dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew. Despite having navigated the cultivation world for over two thousand years, this was his first time seeing a Golden Core cultivator capable of performing a clone technique.

And what an unconventional method it is too.

Before Huang Ming could process this, the Qingfeng and Mingyue swords came roaring toward him like twin jiao dragons traversing the East Sea with carnage in their wake.

Lu Yang wasn’t sure whether the walking corpse could return to normal if he bisected it again. Rather than gambling on unknowns, he decided to aim straight for Huang Ming.

I don’t believe you can regenerate like your walking corpse.

Huang Ming frantically directed his walking corpse to attack, but Lu Yang’s clone intercepted it with the Mingyue Sword, while Lu Yang himself engaged with Huang Ming.

Both parties were locked in another stalemate, but it didn’t take long for Huang Ming to realize he was at a disadvantage. Lu Yang’s mental power is stronger than mine, and he controls his clone with higher precision. In the battle between my walking corpse and his clone, my walking corpse has been retreating again and again.

Once the clone obtains victory, I’ll be caught in a one-against-two predicament myself.

Lu Yang’s soft chuckle drifted into Huang Ming’s ear, freezing his blood. “Do you seriously not know that you’re not supposed to get distracted in battle?

“Break!” Lu Yang executed the Breaking Word Mantra. Sword qi surged forth and pierced the heavens, its resplendent rays weaving a lethal tapestry.

A blood-red light barrier materialized before Huang Ming. This was his ultimate defensive move. Against Lu Yang’s all-out Breaking Word Mantra, however, it held for barely half a breath before shattering.

Squelch!

Huang Ming’s attempt to activate Corpse Swap Teleportation again was ultimately a split second slower, and the blade pierced through his right shoulder. With such severe injuries, he would need at least half a month of recuperation to recover.

Despite consuming a Qi Restoration Pill midway through the battle, he still found his spirit energy running dry as the fight drew to a close.

In contrast, Lu Yang hadn’t touched a single restorative pill from the start until the end. This was due to the strength of the Unbeatable Golden Core and eating tofu every day when he began cultivating.

Prolonged consumption of tofu can adjust a cultivator’s balance of the five elements, building their endurance in combat.

“I admit defeat!” Huang Ming spat through gritted teeth, reluctantly swallowing his defeat along with healing pills.

Lu Yang sheathed his sword, amiably striking up a conversation as if he wasn’t the one who had just wounded Huang Ming. “So, what made you decide to disperse your cultivation and cultivate anew?”

Huang Ming sighed. “I was too impatient in my youth and didn’t build my foundation properly, so I hit a wall at the Intermediate Fusion Stage, unable to break through. Since it was a good opportunity to reset my cultivation and start afresh, I seized it and was reborn.

Lu Yang was puzzled. “Then why not join one of the Five Great Immortal Sects? Their abundant resources should be better than the Corpse-Driving Sect’s, right?”

“It’s not easy to enter the immortal sects. They have too many experts who might discover our identities. On the contrary, you’ve got quite the guts. Not only did you sneak into an immortal sect, but you also made yourself so high-profile.” Having seen Lu Yang’s formidable mental power, Huang Ming assumed he was also a reforged cultivator.

Huang Ming continued, “This clone technique of yours is so unique, yet I’ve never heard of it before, and neither were there records of it in history. I believe it must have been lost to time due to a lack of successors. Are you a cultivator from the Great Qian era?”

“No, I didn’t disperse my cultivation to cultivate anew.”

“Stop bragging! How else could you have defeated me? How about this, I’ll level with you. I’m Huang Qin[1] Venerable Lord from the Great Yu Dynasty. What’s your name? Perhaps I’ve heard of your title before.”

Lu Yang simply stared at Huang Ming silently.

Realization also seemed to flicker in Huang Ming’s eyes.

Huang Ming, “...”

Lu Yang, “...”

“You’re a cultivator from the Great Yu Dynasty?!”

“You’re really a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect?!”

Both exclaimed in unison.

Lu Yang had assumed Huang Ming was a reborn elder from the Corpse-Driving Sect, so he had spoken casually. I totally didn’t expect Huang Ming to be a Great Yu cultivator!

Huang Ming was even more shocked than Lu Yang. The combat power Lu Yang had demonstrated had actually been built by himself step by step... Even the Imperial Preceptor couldn’t have achieved this at the same cultivation realm!

Are geniuses of the Great Era truly this terrifying?

Meng Jingzhou realized the severity of the situation at hand. To think that Huang Ming is a Great Yu cultivator.

Man Gu and Zhao Po had never encountered archaic cultivators prior to this, so their reactions weren’t as dramatic as Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Huang Ming quickly responded, his tone growing sinister as his eyes clouded over with not even a sliver of a smile. “Marvelous! Truly a genius of the Great Era! To think you could force me into this wretched state!

“In that case, I can’t spare you anymore! Originally, I planned to silence everyone who heard our conversation, but now, you’ll join them in death!” Huang Ming no longer concealed his killing intent and summoned his companion with a secret spell.

“Fellow Daoist Meng,[2] kill them all!”

“Lu Yang, be careful! A Fusion cultivator is here!” Right as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s warning left her mouth, an oppressive pressure resembling lofty mountains descended upon the battlefield.
