A middle-aged man with mostly white hair appeared in the sky. He ignored Lu Yang and the others and looked down at Huang Ming, a mocking smile curling at the corners of his mouth.

“Fellow Daoist Huang, why are you in such a wretched state?”

“You wouldn’t have fared any better!” Huang Ming retorted. This Lu Yang’s talent is terrifying. Even a reforged Fusion cultivator like myself couldn’t defeat him. If he’s allowed to grow any further, the consequences will be unimaginable!

He must be eliminated—immediately!

“Alright, alright, that’s no problem.” The archaic cultivator known as Fellow Daoist Meng cackled. A few mere Golden Core cultivators? I can wipe them out with a snap of my fingers.

“Him! It’s him!” The Drowned Ghost instinctively shrieked upon recognizing a familiar aura. “He’s the one who knocked me out in the East Sea and dragged me here!”

Fellow Daoist Meng lowered his head, letting out a low chortle upon seeing the Drowned Ghost. “Ah, it’s that Drowned Ghost from the East Sea.”

Lu Yang was stunned. This means that the ghost calamities in Hanshui City were caused by this Fellow Daoist Meng! He captured ghosts from various places and dumped them here. But what does he want to do?!

Fellow Daoist Meng paid the Drowned Ghost no further mind. A Nascent Soul ghost is not worthy of my attention. “I’ll help you kill these people and stage the crime scene to make it look like this Drowned Ghost had taken them down with himself. That way, you can keep your cover in the Corpse-Driving Sect. In return, you have to tell me one of the locations of your hidden treasure spots.”

Huang Ming clenched his teeth, not daring to utter any protest despite the fury simmering within. This is blatant extortion, but there’s nothing I can do.

“Fine!”

“Haha, then I’ll thank you in advance for your gift, Fellow Daoist Huang!”

Having gotten what he wanted, Fellow Daoist Meng no longer held back. His gaze swept over Lu Yang and the others as if they were already dead. “Young fellows, this esteemed one is benevolent and shall allow you to choose how you want to die. Will it be death by having your tendons and skin flayed, being refined into a human pill, or pierced by a hundred ghosts?”

Lu Yang and the rest had their backs drenched in cold sweat, especially Zhao Po; he had never faced such a threatening situation before.

“And how do you want to die?” A sudden voice shattered the deathly tension.

“Who?!” Fellow Daoist Meng was astonished. I hadn’t sensed anyone approaching!

Boom!

A Five-Colored Light Wheel slammed into Fellow Daoist Meng, sending him crashing to the ground and coughing up blood as fear flashed in his eyes.

This single strike was enough for him to sense the vast gulf between their abilities.

The visitor was clad in cyan robes, his hands clasped behind his back. His voice was aloof, and the Five-Colored Light Wheel behind his head resembled a divine aureole.

“Sect Leader of the Five-Elements Sect, Qiu Jin’an.”

1. Huangqin is also a TCM herb. It is sometimes known as a “TCM antibiotic.” ☜

2. It’s a different “Meng.” The surname here is 蒙 (méng), while Meng Jingzhou’s surname is 孟 (mèng). ☜

Chapter 430: Using Five-Elements Spells Before Me?

“Qiu Jin’an? One of the sect leaders of Great Xia’s so-called Five Great Immortal Sects?” Fellow Daoist Meng sneered at Qiu Jin’an’s identity. He climbed up from the ground, though he wasn’t seriously injured. I only got hit earlier because Qiu Jin’an had ambushed me.

If we fight for real, the outcome is still uncertain.

He hailed from the golden age of the Great Yu Dynasty, when the Great Yu Dynasty rivaled even the current Great Xia Dynasty. As one of the few finest Fusion cultivators of that era, his status was no less than Qiu Jin’an’s. To have slumbered for several hundred millennia and awakened to implement his plans in the Great Era, he naturally had his unique strength.

Though Great Xia has numerous powerful figures now, several hundred thousand years have passed. Many cultivation techniques and spells would have been lost to time.

But I possess these very lost arts.

When one side wields lost cultivation techniques and spells and the other doesn’t, it’s obvious who is stronger.

“Sect Leader Qiu?!”

Lu Yang and the others were overjoyed. While these Great Yu cultivators were conceited and ignorant of Qiu Jin’an’s strength, how could they not know?

This is the same Sect Leader Qiu who held his own despite being tormented by the Dao-Seeking Nine since they were young! As the foremost practitioner of five-elements spells, even the Minister of Justice probably can’t defeat him!

Aside from the Taciturn Daoist Priest, the top Fusion cultivator, who dared to claim certain victory over Qiu Jin’an?!

“Qiu Jin’an?!” Zhao Po was floored but instantly relieved. The reputation of the Five Great Immortal Sects resounds through the Great Xia Dynasty, eclipsing our Corpse-Driving Sect.

Stealing glances at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, he realized that though they were pleasantly surprised, their reactions were far calmer than his.

He suddenly recalled Meng Jingzhou’s curse, which was at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation level. Just who did he provoke? Previously, he was puzzled how Meng Jingzhou could make such enemies despite being at the Golden Core Stage.

But now, he was beginning to understand.

We’ve only been together for a few days, and I’ve already crossed paths with an archaic Fusion cultivator.

Man Gu was unshaken, for he had witnessed greater storms and participated in the annihilation of the Everlasting Creed. Those were much bigger than what’s happening now.

The Drowned Ghost was on the verge of dying again from terror. This matter is now far beyond me. Fusion cultivators from the Great Yu era? Sect leader of the Five Great Immortal Sects? These aren’t figures an insignificant water ghost like me should come into contact with.

As for Huang Zao’er, the insurance fraudster, she had fainted long ago.

Amidst their delight, Lu Yang thought of another question. “Wait, why is Sect Leader Qiu here? And how did he arrive at such an opportune moment?”

“Simple. He’s been following you,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said matter-of-factly. Not even Qiu Jin’an’s stealth techniques could escape her notice.

“Following us? Since when?”

“Since you and Meng Jingzhou tried to enter the city but got caught in that landslide.”

“Isn’t that right from the very beginning?!”

“Not quite. The very beginning was when you entered that shady inn,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy corrected the flaw in Lu Yang’s logic.

Fellow Daoist Meng was unfazed by Qiu Jin’an and even wanted to attack. “Juniors of Great Xia, let me show you the might of archaic arts—Sky-Suspended Suns!”

The phantom images of bronze trees slowly materialized behind him. Two blazing suns flickered intermittently, radiating endless light and heat. A mere glance could make one feel like they were melting. At each sun’s core, a Jinwu crow spread its wings and screeched.

With a casual wave, Qiu Jin'an conjured a light barrier to shield Lu Yang and the others.

This was a Fusion cultivator’s killer move. Even brushing past it could potentially obliterate Lu Yang and the others.

Qiu Jin’an pondered, seeming to recall a description of this move in an ancient text, then spoke unhurriedly. “Legends say that ten Jinwu crows roosted upon the Fusang Tree[1] in the ancient era. Every day, one crow would set out for patrol and inspect the world. However, one day, all ten crows flew out together, bringing calamities upon the earth, and an ancient god shot down nine suns with his bow.

“In the Great Yu era, someone studied this ancient tale and found a segment of the Fusang Tree’s trunk. They fused it with the Jinwu Crow True Fire and created a mighty ability called ‘Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns,’ elevating the power of Jinwu Crow True Fire to new heights.

“That person directly became a grandmaster of Fire Dao, founding the Heavenly Blaze Sect, whose fame spread across the world. But later, he disappeared, and the technique ‘Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns’ vanished since then. The Heavenly Blaze Sect clung on for eight thousand years before enemies razed it.

“According to the records, that person’s Daoist title was Meng Tian True Lord.”[2]

Despite having his identity exposed by Qiu Jin’an, Fellow Daoist Meng didn’t panic, the corners of his mouth curling into a cold smirk. “Quite knowledgeable of you. Although I can only manifest ‘Heaven-Patrolling Two Suns,’ once I successfully reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, I’ll be able to cast ‘Heaven-Patrolling Five Suns,’ and at the Great Perfection Transcendent Tribulation Stage, it’ll be ‘Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns,’ recreating the splendor as in ancient times! It’s a pity my cultivation lags behind my theories, but it's more than enough to get rid of you, youngster!

“I hereby establish the rule: I can cast Heaven-Patrolling Three Suns!”

Atop the Fusang Tree, a third sun blazed to life.

Given their proximity to Hanshui City, making too much commotion would inevitably attract the attention of the experts in the city, so Meng Tian knew he had to finish the battle as fast as possible. Hence, he skipped all preliminary attacks and unleashed his strongest move right from the outset! Fusion cultivators couldn’t create rules as they wished, else Meng Tian True Lord might have directly executed Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns.

When Fusion cultivators fought, the rules they set typically fell into two categories: self-enhancement and enemy-restricting.

The strength of self-enhancement rules depended on the Fusion cultivator’s limits, and such rules were a method to stimulate one’s latent power.

On the other hand, enemy-restricting rules were limited by frequency parity. If you restrained the opponent once, they could do the same to you once. As the restriction methods were inexhaustible, a single misstep could spell disaster.

For example, during the battle between the Great Yu Fusion cultivator, who crafted a soul-summoning banner with beasts, and Vice Creed Leader Shi, the rule the former established was: Apart from me, everyone within five hundred zhang shall have their movements slowed.

To which Vice Creed Leader Shi countered with a rule: Within five hundred zhang, no one is allowed to use diabolic artifacts.

This was the manifestation of frequency parity.

The three suns now loomed overhead, and the Jinwu crows shrieked, seemingly heralding a reconstruction of ancient cataclysms.

“Go!” Meng Tian True Lord thrust two fingers downward, aiming at Qiu Jin’an and everyone behind him.

If Qiu Jin’an dodges, those behind him will undoubtedly die. I’m convinced he won’t!

“Ai—” Facing the three suns, Qiu Jin’an let out a long sigh. He stepped forward, while the Five-Colored Light Wheel behind him shone brilliantly and turned into a Five-Colored Divine Light. Anything that belonged to the Five Elements was within the divine light's command.

Swish! The three suns gradually dissolved under the radiance of the Five-Colored Divine Light.

“So, the fabled Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns described to resemble natural disasters only amount to this.”

“How is that possible?!” Meng Tian True Lord’s eyes bulged. My strongest move was nullified just like that?!

He didn’t even establish a single “Rule!”

Before he could process what had happened, Qiu Jin’an’s figure blurred and stomped him into the ground. His foot carried the weight of one hundred thousand mountains, crushing Meng Tian True Lord until his limbs were splayed out.

Qiu Jin’an gazed down at him indifferently. “I’ve never met anyone who dares to use five-elements spells before me, not even those nine fellows from the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

1. The Fusang Tree is a mythical world tree. ☜

2. The name “Meng Tian” directly translates to hoodwinking the heavens. ☜

Chapter 431: Solution to Karmic Backlash

Meng Tian True Lord hadn’t expected himself to be defeated so swiftly. In his eyes, he possessed an arsenal of untransmitted spells. Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns was simply the most devastating among them. However, before he could unleash them, Qiu Jin’an’s Five-Colored Divine Light swept across the three blazing suns and snuffed them out. The canyon plunged back into cool shadows.

Without wasting words, Qiu Jin’an reached for Meng Tian True Lord’s head, planning to search his soul directly to uncover their scheme.

Realizing things had gone south, Meng Tian True Lord couldn’t be bothered about the toll on himself as he gritted his teeth and activated a life-preserving secret spell.

Thump, thump, thump. His heart pounded vigorously, nothing like someone who had just been defeated. The temperature in his heart spiked violently and melted the protective robes around his chest that could withstand part of a Fusion cultivator’s attacks, exposing his bare chest.

Only then did Qiu Jin’an notice that embedded in his heart was not a heart but a dead Jinwu crow!

An arrow pierced through the Jinwu crow, resulting in a mortal wound. Qiu Jin’an suspected that this Jinwu crow was the same one shot to death by the ancient god. No wonder he could comprehend Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns! He must have found the Jinwu crow’s corpse somewhere and grafted it into his own chest, replacing his heart!

Suddenly, the Jinwu crow’s eyes snapped open. Feathers rapidly grew and covered Meng Tian True Lord’s body.

“Oh no, he’s trying to escape!”

Qiu Jin’an stomped down to nail him to the ground, but when he exerted force, he realized that Meng Tian True Lord had turned into Jinwu crow feathers, and his foot passed right through.

Boom! Meng Tian True Lord exploded, and a flurry of Jinwu crow feathers fluttered in all directions.

Qiu Jin’an silently chanted an incantation and summoned a whirlwind to scatter the feathers. But by the time he did so, Meng Tian True Lord had already vanished, leaving behind only a severed branch of the Fusang Tree.

“The two ran away!”

Meng Tian True Lord’s escape technique was unlike anything Qiu Jin’an had encountered, causing him to react a beat slower.

~~~

Wheeze, wheeze. The severely wounded Meng Tian True Lord and Huang Ming disguised themselves as mortals, blending into the crowds of Hanshui City.

“Damn it! How is that Qiu Jin’an this strong?!” Meng Tian True Lord rejoiced at the close shave. Any moment later, and Qiu Jin’an would have searched my soul, and I’d have died at his hand.

Losing the Fusang Tree’s branch means I can no longer cast Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns. My foundation is also shaken and can only be mended with Transcendent Tribulation-tier sacred treasures.

But nothing is more important than surviving.

“That was a bough of the Fusang Tree! You have to compensate me for my loss!” Meng Tian True Lord snarled at Huang Ming. If not for this brat Huang Ming’s hidden treasure spots, I wouldn’t have saved him.

“I’ll tell you two more secret treasure spots! That should make up for your losses!” Huang Ming forced the words out through clenched teeth. I only have four secret treasure spots, and they’re meant to accelerate my rise in the future. When I previously promised one spot, it didn’t matter much, but now that I’m giving up three, I’ll have to spend much effort to search for other cultivation treasures!

That would waste so much time! But it’s not like I can refuse. I’m just a Golden Core cultivator. Even if Meng Tian True Lord is seriously injured, I still wouldn’t stand a chance.

Huang Ming asked with a gloomy face, “So what now? Where do we go?”

“In our state, we’re unable to participate in the subsequent operation for Hanshui City. See that house there? The owner worships a wooden statue to pray for blessings, but it’s actually a sacrificial ghost I’ve placed there. The sacrificial ghost has completely controlled the entire household. We’ll hide there first; no one will find out.”

“Alright.”

The two resisted the impulse to sprint toward the house, matching their strides to the crowd to avoid giving anything away.

“Are you two leaving just like that?” A sudden voice froze them mid-step.

The two raised their heads and saw a man in a white paper hat standing in front of them. Despite the bustling crowd, no one seemed to have noticed him.

“Who are you?!”

The white paper-hatted man cackled coldly, sending chills down their spines. “You Great Yu cultivators have been capturing ghosts everywhere and dumping them in Hanshui City, then framing us Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Even the Heavenly Court Creed suspects we’re the culprits. This is straining the friendship between our creeds. And you’re still asking who I am?”

“Nine-Netherworlds Creed...run!”

“Do you think you can run?”

Three more white paper-hatted men appeared, encircling them. The Four Great Diabolic Creeds didn’t survive for so many years without top-notch escape abilities.

“You Great Yu cultivators have also delayed our business operations. Vice Creed Leader Shi has much to say about this. Let’s settle our new and old scores together.”

The white paper-hatted men seized the two, and they vanished from the spot.

~~~

“What a pity, they managed to escape.” Qiu Jin’an sighed. Catching either one of them could have yielded valuable intelligence.

“Sect Leader Qiu, what brings you here?” Lu Yang asked respectfully.

“Isn’t this the acting sect leader? It’s been a long while,” Qiu Jin’an greeted Lu Yang with an insincere smile. “Acting Sect Leader Lu, you’re still serving as the acting sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Back when the Five-Elements Sect visited the Dao-Seeking Sect for an exchange, they suffered a crushing defeat, and coincidentally, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was the acting sect leader for three days at that time.

During the discussion on the competition arrangements, Qiu Jin’an had assumed Yun Zhi was the acting sect leader and boldly proposed that his eldest disciple duel with the strongest disciple in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Then, Yun Zhi stepped forward and clarified that she wasn’t the acting sect leader then.

Hence, from Qiu Jin’an’s perspective, Lu Yang was the acting sect leader.

Zhao Po was flabbergasted. Sect Leader Qiu’s words revealed some astonishing information. Brother Lu had once been the Dao-Seeking Sect’s acting sect leader? Doesn’t that mean he isn’t just the strongest of the younger generation in combat power, but also the highest in status?!

We’re all peers of similar age, yet why is the chasm between us so wide?

“I stepped down for someone more qualified, and Big Senior Sister took over.” Lu Yang’s blunt honesty threw Qiu Jin’an off guard.

“Alright, enough banter. I’m here to tell Meng boy that I’ve found a way to break the curse.” Qiu Jin’an brought with him a seed of hope.

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up. “Really?”

“How can it be fake? I’ve verified this through numerous channels. It’s extremely reliable.” Qiu Jin’an whispered mysteriously, “Have you heard of the power of national fortune?”

Meng Jingzhou blurted out, “The immortal method?”

Qiu Jin’an froze for a bit. He had prepared an elaborate lecture, planning to flaunt his knowledge. Anyway, they’ll forget afterward. I didn’t expect Meng Jingzhou to know about it.

Technically speaking, he shouldn’t have remembered about the national fortune. But as the leader of an immortal sect, he was often involved in discussions related to the national fortune, and the imperial court gave every immortal sect’s leader a treasure to remember the existence of the national fortune.

“Correct, that’s the one. Are you aware that every provincial governor and commandery governor of Great Xia is protected by the national fortune to prevent anyone from harming them. Do you understand what this means?”

Lu Yang was the fastest in connecting the dots. “It means the national fortune can eliminate karmic backlash!”

“Exactly, it can eliminate karmic backlash. This is an immortal method. One rinse of the national fortune, and everything will be fine!”

Meng Jingzhou was jubilant. This is much more reliable than waiting for the Corpse-Driving Sect’s leader to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

Chapter 432: Number One of the Younger Generation!

“This is information I’ve obtained only after verification through numerous channels. The national fortune’s power is a high-level matter you shouldn’t be privy to now. All you need to know is that using the power of the national fortune can eliminate karmic backlash!” Qiu Jin’an reminded them that their cultivation was still too low to be qualified to learn such secrets.

This is knowledge typically reserved for Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Were I not a sect leader, I wouldn’t have known about the national fortune’s existence.

Lu Yang was in full agreement. “Indeed. The power of the national fortune belongs to the imperial court’s immortals and is connected to Dao Fruits, one of the immortal methods. Those under the protection of the national fortune become immune to poison and disease and can unleash tremendous combat power instantly. This power also possesses memory-erasing properties. Even the Great Yu Dynasty’s imperial preceptors feared it and didn’t dare to oppose it openly!”

Qiu Jin’an froze. Why does Lu Yang seem to know more than I do? Is this really the amount of knowledge Golden Core cultivators should have?

Back in my Golden Core days, I’d barely learned about the Ancient Nameless One who refined the stars into a continent. As for concepts like immortals and Dao Fruits, they were completely foreign to me. Occasionally, I had gone to train in secret domains left behind by Nascent Soul and Divine Transfiguration cultivators, only accessible to Golden Core cultivators.

Moreover, the national fortune has memory-erasing properties, which can only be mitigated with a treasure gifted by the imperial court. Why didn’t this kid Lu Yang forget?

After a moment of contemplation, Qiu Jin’an didn’t dig deeper. There are too many things I can’t figure out in the Dao-Seeking Sect—what’s one more mystery with Lu Yang?

For instance, there’s something I still can’t understand after all this time. The cultivation world is so big, but how did the nine scourges end up together in the Dao-Seeking Sect as the Dao-Seeking Nine?

I can probably only explain it with ‘birds of a feather flock together.’

“After learning this information, I went to the Dao-Seeking Sect to look for you. Those old rascals there told me you’d gone to the Corpse-Driving Sect in Wilderness Province, so I rushed here immediately to inform you, and I arrived just in time to intercept the Great Yu Fusion cultivator.” Qiu Jin’an wore an expression that read, “Thank goodness, I came in time.”

Lu Yang cast him a sidelong glance. What do you mean ‘you arrived just in time?’ The Everlasting Immortal Fairy has already told me you’d been tailing us the whole way and enjoying the show.

The battle between Qiu Jin’an and Meng Tian True Lord quickly drew the official guards from Hanshui City. Judging by the commotion, Hanshui City determined that the involved parties had high cultivation, so the highest official they dispatched was at the Fusion Stage.

“Ah, it’s Fellow Daoist Qiu.” The Hanshui City official recognized Qiu Jin’an and bowed respectfully.

As an official of the imperial court, recognizing the leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects was basic etiquette. After all, these sect leaders wielded both supervision and enforcement authorities and were a double-edged sword.

Once, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had blatantly broken the law. When the official considered covering up due to his powerful background, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was displeased and directly reported it to the Xia Emperor. The official was punished as a result, and the Taciturn Daoist Priest also ended up imprisoned for his crime.

This incident had shocked the court. No official dared show favoritism and bend the law afterward—at least not in front of the Five Great Immortal Sects. After all, there were ruthless people like the Taciturn Daoist Priest who would throw himself into prison.

“You are...” Qiu Jin’an drew a blank.

“I am An Ping, Marshal of Wilderness Province.”

“Ah, Lord An.” Although Qiu Jin’an had never seen him before, he still feigned sudden recognition.

“I saw flames soaring upward and suns suspended in the sky. Could you share with us what happened here, Fellow Daoist Qiu?”

“I ran into a Great Yu Fusion cultivator earlier and exchanged blows with him. After he lost in just two moves, he fled in a panic.

“According to the information he revealed, he’s behind the current ghost calamities in the city, though I’m not sure whether he has accomplices.”

Marshal An’s expression grew solemn. This is no trivial matter, now that the ghost calamities have been classified as a top-priority crisis. We’ve been suspecting that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed is the culprit, but it appears to be the work of Great Yu cultivators!

“Fellow Daoist Qiu, could you discuss this in detail with His Excellency the Provincial Governor?”

Qiu Jin’an smiled. “I happen to have business with him.”

“That’s great! May I know who these people are?”

“The three of them are Dao-Seeking Sect disciples, and the one in front is the old Taciturn scoundrel’s youngest disciple.”

Upon hearing Lu Yang’s identity, Marshal An regarded him with newfound respect.

He was a junior who was not yet born when the Taciturn Daoist Priest was active. In a sense, he grew up on the Silent Daoist’s tales. He understood all too well how unlucky it was to be the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple.

“This is a disciple from the Corpse-Driving Sect. This Drowned Ghost and this unconscious mortal woman are involved in insurance fraud, and we were going to hand them over to you. They also have an accomplice, Liu San from Baishui Village.”

Without Marshal An having to issue any orders, his subordinates had already seized the Drowned Ghost and the unconscious Huang Zao’er, while someone raced to Baishui Village to apprehend Liu San. The follow-up matters would no longer require the involvement of Lu Yang and the rest.

“Wait a moment,” Lu Yang said before departing. Then, under the bewildered gazes of the crowd, he reached his hand into the dried-up frigid pool. An endless stream of saltwater gushed from his sleeve and filled the pool. The original water drained from the pool had been stored away by using Village in Palm.

Marshal An was dumbfounded. Lu Yang is so young, yet he has already mastered Sleeve Cosmos?

Noticing Marshal An’s expression, Qiu Jin’an guffawed. “Never expected that, right? Earlier, Lu Yang even fought with a Fusion cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew and emerged victorious. His combat prowess can be said to be the number one of the younger generation.” Although my own disciples can also defeat that reforged Fusion cultivator, they couldn’t have done it as effortlessly as Lu Yang.

During Lu Yang’s battle, Qiu Jin’an had been watching from the side. When he observed how Lu Yang never once drew upon his golden core’s power, he even suspected that Lu Yang had more formidable methods he had yet to unleash.

I couldn’t have defeated Lu Yang even if I were at his age. Truly a disciple taught by Yun Zhi.

“So strong?!” Marshal An was flabbergasted once again, not expecting such a high appraisal from Qiu Jin’an. With Qiu Jin’an’s vast experience and knowledge, his judgment wouldn’t be wrong. I mean, there’s no need for him to exaggerate. After all, Lu Yang is a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, not the Five-Elements Sect.

As always, the Dao-Seeking Sect is really teeming with talents.

Zhao Po nodded inwardly. When he saw Lu Yang’s ferocious combat style, he had an inkling that Lu Yang looked like the number one of the younger generation. However, due to his limited experience, he dared not come to a conclusion rashly.

“You heard that, didn’t you? I’m the number one of the younger generation!” Lu Yang preened himself like a triumphant peacock in front of Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu.

Man Gu applauded with sincerity from the bottom of his heart. “Brother Lu, you’re amazing!”

Meng Jingzhou pouted. This grandson Lu Yang is getting so full of himself that his tail is sticking up into the sky. “How are you the number one of the younger generation? Big Senior Sister is the one.”

Lu Yang was gleeful. “You’re just envious of me. Big Senior Sister is not the younger generation’s...”

Noticing the mischievous and dangerous glint in Meng Jingzhou’s eyes, Lu Yang suddenly realized his slip of the tongue, and the words died in his mouth as he shot a furious glare at Meng Jingzhou.

Meng Jingzhou glanced around innocently, as if he hadn’t been the one who dug the pit in the first place.

~~~

Under Marshal An’s lead, the group managed to meet the newly appointed Wilderness Province’s governor without any hiccups.

Chapter 433: I’m Under the Tutelage of Dao-Seeking Sect’s Yun Zhi

The provincial governor’s estate was located in the very center of Hanshui City. It was the nexus of power and influence in Wilderness Province, every layer fortified with defensive arrays like a fortress.

This was both the provincial governor’s residence and workplace. As Lu Yang traversed the compound, he noticed many officials clutching documents as they flew around in a hurry. They weren’t just running as fast as flying; they were literally flying.

Marshal An had already informed the provincial governor before arranging the meeting. When the provincial governor saw Qiu Jin’an and the others, he greeted them warmly with handshakes. As Marshal An still had to organize the citywide manhunt for Meng Tian True Lord, he excused himself.

“Fellow Daoist Qiu, your reputation precedes you! I am Lü Ke, but most just call me Old Lü.” Provincial Governor Lü was a loquacious person. Despite being swamped by the recent ghost calamities, he remained in glowing spirits and showed no signs of fatigue.

“Greetings, Lord Lü.” Qiu Jin’an smiled but didn’t call him “Old Lü.”

The last time someone acted this familiar with me was when I met the Dao-Seeking Nine. That’s not something I’ll be forgetting anytime soon.

Qiu Jin’an’s father had been the previous sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect. When Qiu Jin’an was young, he accompanied his father to visit the Dao-Seeking Sect, where he got to know the exuberant Dao-Seeking Nine.

Back then, he was young, naive, and a poor judge of character, unable to recognize the schemes brewing under their cheerful facades. The sole exception was Sixth Elder, Fengya, who didn’t seem to fit in with the rest of the Dao-Seeking Nine, but she’d never be absent during their misdeeds.

Therefore, he became wary of people who acted overly familiar with him on their first meeting.

Provincial Governor Lü complained, “Say, why did the previous provincial governor have to throw some birthday banquet for his daughter for no reason? He even invited many people, who came with heaps of lavish gifts, and he didn’t bother reporting to the imperial court in advance. Well, look how that turned out. He’s been dismissed from his position, and several key officials and prominent figures from big sects in Wilderness Province got dragged down with him.“

This explained part of the current chaos—manpower shortages, temporary replacements in critical positions, and deployment challenges; even dealing with ghost calamities required assistance from the nearest Corpse-Driving Sect.

“Old Xu—oh, I mean, the Minister of Justice—had taken an extended leave. Now that he’s finally had enough rest, he's handling their cases.” The Minister of Justice had announced to the public that a close friend had died suddenly, requiring emergency leave to meet him one last time.

“With all that, His Majesty lost trust in Wilderness Province’s officials and dragged me, a money-and-grain guy, from the capital to take charge here.

“By the way, I’ve been the only one talking all this time, and I haven’t had the chance to ask. Who are these youths?” Provincial Governor Lü suddenly noticed Lu Yang and the others.

“These three are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. They’re considered my juniors, and I help to look after them. This is Zhao Po, a disciple of the Corpse-Driving Sect’s First Elder. He also witnessed the entire battle earlier.”

Upon learning that Provincial Governor Lü was an official from the capital, Qiu Jin’an avoided mentioning that Lu Yang was a disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Solid foundations, full and plump golden cores—outstanding youths indeed.“ Provincial Governor Lü nodded approvingly. ”Now, Fellow Daoist Qiu, could you recount the battle earlier?” This is the most pressing matter at hand.

Qiu Jin’an recounted in detail how Lu Yang had encountered Huang Ming, defeated him, then how Meng Tian True Lord had intervened before being vanquished by Qiu Jin’an himself.

“That is to say that Meng Tian True Lord has been capturing evil ghosts from various places and dumping them in our Hanshui City?” Provincial Governor Lü’s rage flared. I’ve finally identified the culprit behind today’s chaos.

No wonder there are so many evil ghosts. Did he round up every ghost in Great Xia and even dredge the ghosts up from the East Sea?!

Hell, I’d be the ghost if all this could get cleaned up! [1]

Qiu Jin’an remarked, “The ghost calamities probably couldn’t have been orchestrated by one person alone. I suspect he has accomplices.”

“They’re taking advantage of the fact that I’ve been newly appointed and have yet to master the use of the national fortune’s power!” Provincial Governor Lü hadn’t known about the national fortune until the Xia Emperor recently informed him when he took office.

Qiu Jin’an reminded, “And we must keep a close watch on Huang Ming, the cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew. In the past, we had only focused on archaic Fusion cultivators, overlooking the possibility that some are reforged cultivators!”

Provincial Governor Lü signed. “Keeping watch won’t help. Dispersing one’s cultivation to cultivate anew is akin to rebirth and a new life. Tracking their origins is near impossible.

“Never mind. I’ll report the matter of reforged cultivators to the imperial court. Our priority now is to handle the ghost calamities. Previously, I suspected it was the work of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. After all, they keep plenty of ghosts. But now that we’ve confirmed that Great Yu cultivators are responsible, the matter has grown dire. Great Yu cultivators don’t nurture ghosts, yet they have gone through so much trouble to capture ghosts from various places and dumped them in Hanshui City. I believe it suggests deeper motives rather than mere mischief!” His expression darkened, and he wished he could tear those Great Yu cultivators limb from limb.

“Excuse me, may I ask if they could be setting up an array?” Lu Yang raised his hand gingerly.

“Array?” Provincial Governor Lü and Qiu Jin'an blinked in unison and ruminated over the word, seeming to have thought of something.

Back when Lu Yang was in Yanjiang Commandery, the commandery governor—who doubled as the Yanjiang Branch’s leader—had set up an array across the commandery, planning to drain the entire population’s lifespan to boost his power.

This memory prompted Lu Yang to bring up his question.

“It’s possible that they’re setting up an array!” Provincial Governor Lü smacked his thigh. I’ve been so busy these days that I failed to consider it.

He approached an enormous sand table and clapped lightly. The sand shook and undulated like waves before finalizing into the structure of Hanshui City.

Producing small flags from his sleeve, he tossed them onto positions matching the locations of ghost calamities. Each flag bore symbols to indicate the ghost type and level.

Provincial Governor Lü gasped. “If we look at it this way, it does resemble an array.” He was overjoyed that Lu Yang’s conjecture was likely the answer. “As expected of a disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect! A great master breeds brilliant disciples. May I know who your shifu is?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Before answering truthfully, Lu Yang wanted to know what grudge Provincial Governor Lü held against his shifu.

“I’m under the tutelage of Dao-Seeking Sect’s Yun Zhi.” Out of deference for his shifu, Lu Yang dared not speak his shifu’s name while away from the sect.

Meng Jingzhou shot Lu Yang a look of utter contempt. Absolutely shameless.

“Yun Zhi? The name sounds a bit familiar.” Provincial Governor Lü searched through his memory. I’ve never heard of any Dao-Seeking Sect elder who goes by the name of Yun Zhi.

“My shifu seldom leaves the sect, so few know of her.”

“I see.”

Provincial Governor Lü simply stopped trying to recall who Yun Zhi was. Since neither he nor Qiu Jin’an were adept at arrays, he summoned the great array masters from the city to examine what array the Great Yu cultivators had set up in the city.

Soon, several white-bearded old men clustered around the sand table, analyzing and making inferences. Fortunately, all were male cultivators. The great array masters worked together and quickly reached a preliminary conclusion.

Provincial Governor Lü was visibly more at ease than at the start of their meeting. “Fellow Daoist Lu’s conjecture was correct. The Great Yu cultivators have indeed set up an array. But it has been lost to time, so we’ll need time to deduce its purpose and how to break it. Let us wait for a bit.”

Seeing that the timing was right, Qiu Jin’an cupped his hands and said, “Since we have a moment, Lord Provincial Governor, could you allow this kid and me to borrow the national fortune’s power?”

1. Once again, it’s a figure of speech with the “character” for “ghost” in it. ☜

Chapter 434: Karmic Backlash Disappears

“Borrow the national fortune’s power?” Provincial Governor Lü blinked at the request.

“Is that not possible?”

“No no no, of course it’s allowed.”

The Five Great Immortal Sects and the imperial court were alliances of the righteous path without any true hierarchical relationship between them.

A hundred thousand years ago, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s ancestor, Primordial Heavenly Sovereign, along with four others, established the Five Great Immortal Sects and established an alliance with Great Xia, which included enforcement authority, supervision authority, and tax reduction and waiver.

Most notably, it granted sect leaders of immortal sects the right to use the national fortune’s power.

Qiu Jin’an had brought up his request because he was familiar with the terms of the alliance.

Provincial Governor Lü didn’t know about the contents of the alliance agreement, but during his emergency training, personally conducted by the Xia Emperor, he had been informed that immortal sects were authorized to use the national fortune’s power. In truth, Qiu Jin’an understood the national fortune better than he did.

“Sect Leader Qiu, with your peerless cultivation, what could have led to you being cursed?” Provincial Governor Lü inquired cautiously.

Qiu Jin’an sighed in exasperation. “It’s a long story. By chance, I encountered this Meng boy, and circumstances compelled us to infiltrate a diabolic lair to purge evil and return peace to the world. Unfortunately, the diabolic lair was their headquarters and housed numerous experts. Even I found myself at a disadvantage in battle, just like how two fists struggle against four hands. My strength alone was limited, and the diabolic path planted a curse on us during the battle!”

Provincial Governor Lü exclaimed indignantly, “So that’s how it was! Those diabolic cultivators are really incorrigible! May I know which of the Three Great Diabolic Creeds you infiltrated, Sect Leader Qiu?”

Qiu Jin’an shook his head, unwilling to elaborate, and Provincial Governor Lü tactfully dropped the subject.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou wore peculiar expressions but stayed silent.

“Sect Leader Qiu is amazing, charging alone into a diabolic creed!” Man Gu clenched his fists in admiration as he envisioned the scene. That must have been so cool!

When Qiu Jin’an infiltrated the Dao-Seeking Sect, Man Gu was still in the middle of his coming-of-age ceremony in the wilderness, so he was unaware of the situation then.

“You’re permitted to use the national fortune’s power, though I’ve just learned about it and am still unfamiliar with its application.”

“No worries, there’s no need for a complicated process. Cleansing us with the national fortune’s power will suffice.”

“Very well,” Provincial Governor Lü readily agreed.

As the national fortune’s power was a major secret, Provincial Governor Lü only allowed the two unlucky fellows, Qiu Jin’an and Meng Jingzhou, to follow him, while Lu Yang, Man Gu, and Zhao Po remained behind.

After the series of escalating events, the three of them were exhausted. What started as a simple mission to deal with a Drowned Ghost had spiraled out of control. First, a reforged cultivator, then a Great Yu Fusion cultivator joined the fray, and finally, Qiu Jin’an showed up to turn the tide.

“To think that Senior Brother Huang Ming is actually an archaic cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew!” Zhao Po smiled bitterly.

“Judging by Huang Ming’s methods, he was already adept at Corpse-Driving Techniques before dispersing his cultivation,” Lu Yang analyzed. This might have also been why Huang Ming chose the Corpse-Driving Sect.

That wasn’t strange. The history of Corpse-Driving Techniques could be traced back to the ancient era, so it was not surprising that a Great Yu cultivator was skilled in Corpse-Driving Techniques.

Lu Yang added gravely, “The real question is how many archaic cultivators have dispersed their cultivation to cultivate anew. Huang Ming cultivated until the Golden Core Stage, but that doesn’t mean that other archaic cultivators have also stopped at the same stage!” Unlike diabolic creeds, which have mid- and low-level cultivators, archaic cultivators start at the Fusion Stage with unknown upper limits, making them tougher to deal with.

“Just a reforged cultivator. Not a single one ascended to an immortal. Embarrassing.” As an immortal, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy held these people in contempt.

“Hmm, what are you looking at, Immortal Fairy?” Lu Yang noticed her lying prone on the bed and staring intently at the headboard’s light projection.

The figures that appeared on the screen were familiar. They were none other than Provincial Governor Lü, Qiu Jin’an, and Meng Jingzhou.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained, “I’ve never seen how the national fortune’s power is used. Let me take a look.

“Move over. Let me take a look too.” Lu Yang was equally curious, squeezing beside her to watch the projection.

Although the location had layers of seals, and the national fortune itself could prevent external probing from even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, they amounted to nothing before the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the head of the Five Ancient Immortals. Only if an immortal from the imperial court personally wielded the national fortune could the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s prying eyes be blocked.

The screen showed Provincial Governor Lü leading the two into a secret chamber made of stones. The place was impenetrable without even a single crack, seeming to have been carved from an enormous boulder rather than piled up from rocks.

In one area of the secret chamber was a small pool, though it was empty with only a square indentation in the center. Provincial Governor Lü placed the Wilderness Province’s official seal into the indentation.

Suddenly, luminous water-like strands materialized and filled the depression.

“So this thing is the national fortune’s power,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked.

Seeing Lu Yang still somewhat baffled, she explained, “The national fortune’s power has always permeated every inch of Great Xia’s land in an imperceptible and undetectable form. The Wilderness Province’s official seal is a key that turns the national fortune from an undetectable state to a detectable state.

“Since the Wilderness Province's official seal is a supreme treasure that recognizes a master, only Provincial Governor Lü can activate it.

“As for the might of the national fortune, it’s probably limited because it only draws upon one province. However, if the national fortune from seventeen provinces is consolidated, the power would be impressive. Looks like the Great Xia imperial court’s immortal does have a bit of ability.

“Of course, I mean ‘a bit.’ They’re still not at this immortal’s level.”

~~~

Meanwhile, it was Meng Jingzhou’s first time seeing the national fortune up close. He felt that the hope of resolving the karmic backlash was finally within reach.

“Do we just jump in?”

Qiu Jin’an stopped Meng Jingzhou’s suicidal impulse. “If you were at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, you might have a chance of surviving if you jump in.”

Although Meng Jingzhou believed himself to be a Golden Core expert, he acknowledged that he was still a distance away from the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. I shall not jump in for now then.

Provincial Governor Lü deployed an arm-thick strand of national fortune to fly out. Shakily controlling the national fortune, he weakened its inherent corrosive nature before directing it toward Qiu Jin’an and Meng Jingzhou with his fingers. With a soft command, “Go,” this mass of national fortune cleansed the two.

“So comfortable!” Meng Jingzhou exhaled in surprise. It’s even more comfortable than my first time coming into contact with spirit energy.

Pinkish mist drifted out and was soon absorbed and dissolved by the national fortune.

With the weight of the curse that had been bearing on their hearts finally lifted, Qiu Jin’an also found it refreshing. “Whew, it’s so comfortable! Brother Lü, now that the curse has disappeared, we should celebrate at a brothel! Where’s the best brothel in Hanshui City?”

Provincial Governor Lü, “...”

Is this really an appropriate question to ask me?

“There used to be a zoo that was the best brothel, but it’s currently closed for restructuring.”

Chapter 435: Early Heaven Bagua and Later Heaven Bagua

“Could these ghosts be positioned based on Early Heaven (Primordial) Bagua,[1] with the Kun (Earth) position as its core?

“Early Heaven Bagua encompasses all phenomena. Here, the ghosts symbolize each phenomenon. Look, this position is the Drowned Ghost, who drowned in water and represents water. This position is the Wronged Ghost, who was buried in the ground and represents earth. This position is the Alluring Ghost, who embodies fiery lust and represents fire. This position is the Painted Skin Ghost...umm, probably just to make up the numbers.”

“No, that’s wrong! This great array likely follows the Later Heaven (Manifested) Bagua, with the array’s focal point at the Zhen (Thunder) position.”

“Did you all even study arrays properly? Must the array nodes only be ghosts? Can’t buildings and structures serve as nodes?”

“See how Hanshui City is flanked by the Corpse-Driving Sect’s Yin-Corpse Mountain Range, which stands for extreme yin, and the bustling brothel district, which stands for extreme yang? The equilibrium of yin and yang is maintained with the provincial governor’s estate at the center, resulting in Hanshui City’s prosperity. This was the original intention behind establishing Hanshui City back then.

“But now, someone has placed malevolent ghosts in Hanshui City to disrupt this balance! How could you all not understand such simple logic?”

“Dogshit theory! The rumor about Hanshui City’s yin-yang balance has been around for a dozen thousand years, yet some still believe in it!”

“It’s not that I believe in it—this is called rational analysis!”

“What rational analysis? All of us are cultivators and revere the strong. If you truly got what it takes, prove it through battle!”

The great array masters’ debate grew increasingly heated until it was on the verge of coming to blows.

Lu Yang considered stepping forward to intervene, but he knew his insignificant status couldn’t quell their altercation.

In truth, it wasn’t completely impossible. As long as he announced that he was a disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Lu Yang believed the old pedants would immediately redirect their focus from arrays to him.

But this method is too dangerous—even the Immortal Fairy might not be able to protect me.

Not that she could protect me even if it weren’t dangerous.

“Great masters, how is the array research coming along?” Provincial Governor Lü left the secret stone chamber and came rushing over.

Relief was plastered across Qiu Jin’an’s and Meng Jingzhou’s faces.

“Don’t worry. I told you I’ll impart to you our sect’s secret spell. Once matters conclude, I’ll teach you!” Qiu Jin’an had promised this to Meng Jingzhou when he controlled the latter to smack Grandpa Ba. And I’m a man of my word.

“You’re fine now?” Lu Yang asked the obvious. I mustn’t let anyone know I was spying just now.

“Brother Meng’s curse is resolved?” Man Gu was genuinely concerned for Meng Jingzhou, a sentiment Zhao Po mirrored.

“It’s all good now! After so long, it’s finally settled. This young master has regained my freedom!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grumbled about the inefficiency. “If you had followed my approach and committed suicide once, the curse would have long been resolved.”

Man Gu suddenly asked in bafflement, “How did you break your curse, Brother Meng?” He felt like he remembered a moment ago but had now forgotten.

It was the same for Zhao Po.

This was due to the effect of an immortal trait.

Meng Jingzhou laughed it off without explanation. Otherwise, it’s likely that Man Gu will ask the same thing ten minutes later, and I’ll have to answer again, and then he’ll ask again and again with no end in sight.

“It’s a pity Big Senior Sister isn’t around, else we wouldn’t have needed to make a trip to Wilderness Province.” Meng Jingzhou missed the days when Yun Zhi was around.

Qiu Jin’an was stunned, perplexed by Meng Jingzhou’s comment. “Are you talking about Yun Zhi? She’s in the Dao-Seeking Sect! I saw her when inquiring about you two there.”

“When did Big Senior Sister return to the sect?”

“The day after you left for Wilderness Province.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Why were you in such a hurry to come here?!” Lu Yang struck first.

“How was I the one in such a hurry to come here? How would I have known that Big Senior Sister would return so quickly? But you? You follow her every day; how did you not even know she’d gone?!” Meng Jingzhou pushed the responsibility to Lu Yang with practiced ease.

“Who dares ask about Big Senior Sister’s whereabouts? Do you?!”

“I don’t!” Meng Jingzhou retorted proudly.

“If you two are wondering what she was up to, I know the answer,” Qiu Jin’an interjected.

“She went to handle the prison release procedures for the old Taciturn scoundrel.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Lu Yang, “...”

Man Gu was stumped. “Sect Leader did something wrong and got arrested again?”

Meanwhile, Provincial Governor Lü was listening to the opinions of the great array masters.

“Trust me, this array’s principle is definitely Early Heaven Bagua!”

“What Early Heaven Bagua? It’s clearly Later Heaven Bagua!”

Qiu Jin’an sighed, his temples hurting. “It’s the Early Heaven and Later Heaven Bagua debate again. A troublesome matter.”

“Early Heaven and Later Heaven Bagua debate?” Lu Yang and the others had never heard of this contention before.

“This involves profound array theories, so it’s no surprise you’ve never heard about it.

“Early Heaven Bagua and Later Heaven Bagua originated from ancient times. They were said to have been derived by an ancient immortal who observed celestial patterns above and terrestrial formations below, so they must align with the laws of heaven and earth.

“This ancient immortal proposed the Bagua Theory, but with the severe loss of ancient culture and civilization, only Early Heaven Bagua and Later Heaven Bagua were passed down until today. This engendered the endless debate over which was the orthodox one.

“If the Bagua Theory could be completed, this age-old conflict would finally cease.”

“Ah, Bagua Theory? That I know!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy displayed her wealth of knowledge and experience once again. I was personally involved in many ancient events, either having experienced them myself or pulling the strings behind the curtain.

“You know about it?”

“Do you hear what you’re saying? Is there anything beyond my ken? I was intimately involved in the birth of this Bagua Theory.”

“You proposed this theory, Immortal Fairy?” Lu Yang was utterly amazed, finding the Everlasting Immortal Fairy much more intelligent in his eyes.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand modestly, not taking credit. “Not at all. The Epoch Immortal inferred this theory, but during his whole deduction process, I was cheering him on from the sidelines and giving him moral support.”

Lu Yang wondered, Was there also a punishment aspect? If the Epoch Immortal couldn’t derive it within a stipulated time, did he have to eat your cooking?

Oblivious to Lu Yang’s snark, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminisced. “He looked up to count the stars, squatted down to look at the dirt, performed some calculations with his fingers, and created a theoretical framework.

“According to him, this Bagua Theory incorporated all celestial phenomena and could serve as a foundation for arrays. An array constructed based on this Bagua Theory would be so abstruse that cultivators of the same level would struggle to formulate a method to break it. It’s a top-tier array theory!

“The complete Bagua Theory comprised four parts: Early Heaven Bagua, Today Heaven Bagua, Tomorrow Heaven Bagua,[2] and Later Heaven Bagua. I don’t know how it spread, but now only the Early Heaven Bagua and Later Heaven Bagua remain.”

1. I decided to adopt the translation from this website. ☜

2. “Today (jintian)” and “tomorrow (mingtian)” has ‘heaven’ or ‘sky’ as the second character. ☜

Chapter 436: Three Possibilities

“The Epoch Immortal had poor naming sense. He coined the name ‘Early Heaven Bagua,’ while I came up with the other three Bagua names. Aren’t mine much better?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s contributions to the Bagua Theory extended beyond giving moral support; she was even involved in the crucial naming process.

Lu Yang went against his conscience and nodded. “...Indeed. The three other names are...remarkably easy to understand.”

“The Bagua Theory is considered an orthodox temporal spell. Saying that it encompasses all phenomena is not an exaggeration. Early Heaven Bagua observes the past, Today Heaven Bagua governs the present, and Tomorrow Heaven Bagua divines the future. These three represent the past, present, and future, forming an integral whole.

“Later Heaven Bagua represents the unpredictable distant future, predicting mere possibilities. It’s the hardest to master; even The Epoch Immortal dared not claim he could foresee the distant future due to too many variable factors.

“Arrays based on Bagua Theory are planned with a temporal aspect, making them nearly impossible for cultivators of the same level to decipher.”

Hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s explanation, Lu Yang felt that the Bagua Theory’s prestige had been salvaged.

“No wonder the great array masters have been endlessly debating about Early Heaven and Later Heaven Bagua without any results. It’s because they haven’t even grasped the fundamentals!” Lu Yang unwittingly solved a conundrum that had plagued the array community for three hundred thousand years.

Putting aside the application of the Early Heaven Bagua and Later Heaven Bagua, they weren’t even in the right direction. This was a theory about temporal spells. If Lu Yang were to publish his research findings, it would shake the entire array community; even Grandpa Ba, an expert in arrays, would have to serve tea to Lu Yang. Temporal spells were cryptic and abstruse, one of the hardest spells to learn in the world.

Even someone as talented as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had only managed to learn Weather Forecast.

And even someone as talented as Lu Yang had only managed to learn to “predict futures that would never come to pass.”

At the moment, the various great array masters were arguing over what kind of array was set up in Hanshui City and what its foundational principles were.

“Enough! All of you, stop arguing!”

Provincial Governor Lü’s roar finally cowed the array masters into silence. If I let them continue like this, they’ll still be squabbling by the time the Great Yu cultivators activate the array. It’s not like their bickering has yielded any result.

“Master Fang, you’re a master in Early Heaven Bagua. According to your theory, what is the purpose of the Great Yu cultivators’ array, and how should we break it?”

Master Fang had three wisps of white beard that accentuated his sage-like demeanor. “I have yet to discern the purpose of the array in the city. But the key to breaking the array lies in its core. In my opinion, the core is at Hundred Flowers Restaurant. The topmost priority now is to seal off the restaurant. If there are malevolent ghosts within the restaurant, it will confirm my conjecture!”

Provincial Governor Lü turned to another array master. “Master Miao, you’re a master in Later Heaven Bagua. According to your assessment, what is the purpose of the Great Yu cultivators’ array, and how should we break it?”

“The array in Hanshui City has the ability to reverse Later Heaven and invert yin and yang, though it’s uncertain what it’s trying to invert. The key to breaking it is the core, but what puzzles me is that the position of the core is at the Corpse-Driving Sect’s entrance. A malevolent ghost that acts as the array core should be there. Perhaps it has concealment capabilities and is hiding right under the Corpse-Driving Sect’s nose!”

Master Miao was unaware, but Provincial Governor Lü knew that with Huang Ming as a mole in the Corpse-Driving Sect, planting a malevolent ghost as the array core there wouldn’t be a problem.

“And you, Master Ren? Didn’t you say that this is neither a Later Heaven nor Early Heaven array, but an attempt by the Great Yu cultivators to overturn yin and yang?”

“Verily. With an imbalance in yin and yang, legions of ghosts will march, plunging the city into chaos. What we don’t yet know is whether the Great Yu cultivators intend to take advantage of this. For now, the top priority is to speed up the extermination of the malevolent ghosts.”

Provincial Governor Lü fell silent. Master Ren might not know the repercussions of chaos in the city, but he did. Hanshui City was the core of Wilderness Province. If the city was thrown into turmoil, it would destabilize the heart of the populace and shake the entire province’s national fortune.

“Does any other master have a differing insight?” Provincial Governor Lü scanned the remaining array masters who had yet to speak.

These masters shook their heads. Their views didn’t deviate from the three theories.

Seeing no alternatives, Provincial Governor Lü swiftly came to a decision and began delegating work to everyone. “Resolving the Early Heaven and Later Heaven theories is not difficult. Sect Leader Qiu, please head to Hundred Flowers Restaurant and investigate if there are any anomalies.”

If Hundred Flowers Restaurant was the array core, there would certainly be ferocious ghosts at the level of a Great Ghost King, making it extremely perilous. Provincial Governor Lü was thankful for Qiu Jin’an’s presence. This is a tremendous boon. A dangerous place like the array core would usually require sending three to five Fusion cultivators, but where would I get so many Fusion cultivators to head there? Thank goodness, Qiu Jin’an alone is worth three to five Fusion cultivators.

“Alright, I’ll depart at once.” Qiu Jin’an accepted with composure, completely unfazed by the potential danger he would face if Hundred Flowers Restaurant was the array core.

“As for the Corpse-Driving Sect, since Sect Leader Lu is in seclusion, let Elder Gai conduct a thorough internal investigation!” Provincial Governor Lü summoned a subordinate and dispatched him to the Corpse-Driving Sect with urgent orders.

With Sect Leader Lu in seclusion, Elder Gai held de facto authority. Provincial Governor Lü didn’t send Zhao Po as a messenger due to his low cultivation and speed; it was now a race against time.

Next, he summoned Marshal An Ping of Wilderness Province. “Old An, we can’t just leave the work to the Corpse-Driving Sect’s disciples. Mobilize more manpower to sweep the city. We must resolve Hanshui City’s ghost calamities in the shortest time possible!”

“Roger!”

After all the tasks were delegated, Provincial Governor Lü exhaled, some tension easing from his shoulders. He hadn’t forgotten about Lu Yang and the other three. “Hanshui City is not safe for now. Remain in the estate until this matter concludes. I’ll get Sect Leader Qiu to escort you back then.”

The four volunteered to go out and help eliminate the ghosts, but Provincial Governor Lü adamantly refused. Their statuses were too special, and he would have a tough time explaining to the Dao-Seeking Sect if anything happened. Thus, Lu Yang reluctantly stayed put.

~~~

“What?! You’re saying Huang Ming is a Great Yu cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew?!” Elder Gai’s veins bulged as fury contorted his face.

The back mountains of the Corpse-Driving Sect shook; this was where his true body resided.

Huang Ming is a Great Yu spy, yet he brazenly snatched first place during the sect’s grand tournament? This is a stain on the Corpse-Driving Sect’s reputation! We’ll be a laughing stock if word gets out!

“Provincial Governor Lü told the sect to carry out an internal investigation; he’s giving our sect a chance! We must conduct a strict investigation—no cutting corners!” Elder Gai called for the other three elders and relayed the news. Their outrage mirrored his own, and they were determined to comb the sect from top to bottom to check if Huang Ming had left behind any traps and schemes.

~~~

“Oh, so Meng Tian and Huang Ming are already unreachable. I sense Fusion cultivators exchanging blows outside the city. Was Meng Tian exposed? He fought with Great Xia cultivators and got caught?

“If that’s the case, our plan will be out of the bag soon. We can only strike first.”

In a secret chamber, a figure rose slowly, lips curling into a confident smirk.

And from him radiated a powerful aura that dwarfed even Apex Fusion cultivators.

Chapter 437: Crisis!

The Hundred Flowers Restaurant stood in the western district of Hanshui City, ranking among the top twenty restaurants in the city. Its most renowned offering was its Hundred Flowers Wine, brewed with over a hundred and fifty seasonal flowers, each season’s batch carrying a distinct flavor.

Qiu Jin’an stepped inside to find the restaurant packed to the brim, a cacophony of voices threatening to lift the roof. The waiters constantly darted between the tables and the back kitchen like spinning tops.

It wasn’t easy for Qiu Jin’an to finally secure a vacant seat in the corner. “May I ask if anyone’s sitting here?”

A rotund patron across from him dug into his food with gusto, his forehead glistening with sweat. He glanced up briefly at Qiu Jin’an and saw that it was someone unfamiliar. “No one. Feel free to sit here.”

“This is unexpected. It’s not even peak hours, yet the place is packed.” Qiu Jin’an chatted with the patron while waiting for a waiter to come over.

The patron wasn’t much of a talker and focused on his meal, responding perfunctorily every now and then.

When a waiter finally brought the menu, Qiu Jin’an skimmed through it and returned it to the waiter. “A bowl of rice, five house specialties, five most premium dishes, and a century-old jar of Hundred Flowers Wine.”

“Gotcha! Please wait a moment, guest!”

Qiu Jin’an didn’t wait too long. A bowl of rice, ten exquisite delicacies, and the fragrant Hundred Flowers Wine were laid out on the table, the sight making the rotund patron envious.

“Guest, if that is all, I’ll be taking my leave.”

The waiter was about to attend to other customers when Qiu Jin’an halted him. “Waiter, I’m a living person. How can I eat a dead person’s meal?”

The waiter was perplexed, his expression vacant.

Qiu Jin’an snapped his fingers. A series of faint cracks echoed, as if someone had stepped on a newly frozen lake and shattered the icy surface, revealing the true lake beneath.

He looked at the main hall again. Where was the busy restaurant now?

Patrons now sat slumped, with one-meter-tall imps straddling their necks and dancing about.

The rotund patron’s belly had swollen grotesquely, his body almost identical to a balloon.

The waiter was emaciated and fragile, as if a breeze could blow him away.

Laid before Qiu Jin’an were no longer delicacies but raw meat and maggots still writhing on the plates.

Only the white rice was unchanged, though three chopsticks were inserted in it like incense sticks.

Qiu Jin’an’s grin widened. “Two Ghost Kings, a Bloated Ghost, a Starved Ghost, and a bunch of grunts. You think you can deal with me with this kind of lineup?”

The rotund patron and the shriveled waiter dropped their pretense, their mouths twisting into ghastly smiles.

An imp stealthily materialized atop Qiu Jin’an’s neck...

~~~

Four cultivators clad in archaic plain robes appeared at the Corpse-Driving Sect’s entrance. They ignored the vigilant disciples and wasted no time as they split up and rushed toward the four locations in the Yin-Corpse Mountain Range.

Boom!

Boom!

Boom!

Boom!

Explosions erupted simultaneously at all four locations.

“Damn it, that bastard Huang Ming secretly scouted out our locations!” Elder Gai bellowed in rage. Before they could scour the Corpse-Driving Sect, their enemies had already struck.

Though caught off guard, the four elders of the Corpse-Driving Sect reacted swiftly and summoned their walking corpses.

One of the archaic cultivators sneered. “Heh, a mere sect that stumbled upon our legacy dares oppose us?”

“You’re from the Witchcraft Corpse Sect!” Elder Gai’s pupils constricted at the sight of their clothing.

The Corpse-Driving Sect had begun due to a fortuitous opportunity. The sect’s founding ancestor inadvertently entered a secret domain, survived three fatal crises, and obtained a legacy—a complete set of Corpse-Driving Techniques.

This legacy originated from the Witchcraft Corpse Sect in the Great Yu Dynasty. According to Great Xia’s categorization of sects, the Witchcraft Corpse Sect was considered an S-class sect, since it had a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

The Witchcraft Corpse Sect was destroyed during the conquest wars in the early days of Great Xia’s founding, leaving behind only a legacy that the Corpse-Driving Sect’s founding ancestor attained.

The archaic cultivator rubbed his ring. One by one, sealed walking corpses broke through their bindings. Reeking of age and a deathly energy, they crossed over a hundred thousand years of history to wage war with the later generations.

Four...eight...sixteen...twenty... A total of twenty walking corpses appeared and besieged Elder Gai and the others!

“Then let us seniors see how much you juniors have learned.”

~~~

An imposing figure loomed over Hanshui City, hovering directly above the provincial governor’s estate. This person moved like tigers and dragons and carried the dignity of a born emperor, every gesture exuding an air of dominance and tyranny. His presence was so overwhelming that everyone in Hanshui City instinctively looked up to the sky and beheld the imposing man whose brilliance rivaled the sun, panic taking root in their hearts.

“After preparing for so long, our plans still ended up leaked. Huang Ming and Meng Tian—these good-for-nothing trash have ruined everything!” The emperor-like figure’s eyes glinted with murderous intent. Had he not lost contact with the two, he wouldn’t have revealed himself prematurely.

Just a teeny little bit later. Only after the great array’s activation conditions are fully fulfilled can the plan be considered seamless.

“Never mind. There is no perfect plan in the world.

“The Calamity Venerable Lord failed and fell in Qing Province, reportedly due to some expert who suddenly arrived. I’ve already investigated Hanshui City these few days, but there’s no one who poses a threat to me.

“As a precaution, I hereby establish the rule: For one day, no information may leave Hanshui City.”

Adding this time restriction will reinforce the implementation of the rule.

Lu Yang gazed up at the emperor-like figure in the air and felt a headache coming on.

The moment the Everlasting Immortal Fairy warned him, he tried contacting Yun Zhi, but he was still a step late. The emperor-like figure had already established the rule. My Animal Form Fist can’t borrow Big Senior Sister’s power, which means she won’t be able to learn of the situation here.

“Aren’t Transcendent Tribulation cultivators supposed to be rare? Why do we keep running into them everywhere? The provincial governor even claimed that this was the safest place, but why do I find this the most dangerous place?

“Maybe it’s because my status as young creed leader is too high that they’re all eager to meet me.”

“Hey, since you’re already the young creed leader, shouldn’t I get a position in the Heavenly Court Creed too?”

“Why don’t you be the young creed leader’s loyal dog?”

“Get lost!”

The old horse sensed the Transcendent Tribulation-level aura emanating from the sky and wondered if it should consider retirement.

When Meng Jingzhou’s father had requested that it protect Meng Jingzhou, it thought it would be a simple task and agreed readily. From sending Yun Zhi to the Dao-Seeking Sect, to resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy at the Yanjiang Branch, then encountering a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in Qing Province, and now an archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in Wilderness Province...

It felt that it had overestimated itself.

Man Gu was unperturbed, his faith in Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou unwavering. With my two senior brothers around, nothing can go wrong.

Zhao Po was the most frantic of the four. Just this morning, we faced Meng Tian True Lord, a Great Yu Fusion cultivator, and now in the afternoon, we’ve encountered a Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

What kind of luck is this?

He felt that his luck had been terrible recently. Since when exactly did my luck turn for the worse?

Chapter 438: Cultivation Ranked Second Among All Yu Emperors

The moment the emperor-like figure appeared, the Great Yu cultivators lurking in the shadows moved out. Malevolent ghosts ran rampant and engulfed the mortal world in chaos, hindering cultivators from rushing toward the provincial governor’s estate.

The emperor-like figure loomed above the estate, his dragon-like eyes brimming with baleful energy. Stretching out a hand, the sky darkened as a palm half the size of the city descended. Within the palm encompassed layers of distorted space, churning spirit energy into stormy tides.

Should this palm strike land, Hanshui City would inevitably be reduced to a death zone!

“Scoundrel, how dare you?!” Provincial Governor Lü’s roar thundered, sending visible ripples through the air.

“Disperse!” Extending his hands skyward, he resembled a titan propping up the heavens, intercepting the emperor-like figure’s humongous hand!

Boom! The collision of two powers was like the clash between heavenly lightning and earthly fire, unleashing an explosion of boundless power.

The emperor-like figure withdrew his hand, surprise flickering across his face as he watched the wound in his palm heal sluggishly. “Oh? As far as this sovereign[1] knows, you junior are merely at the Fusion Stage, yet you could withstand my Cosmos in Palm. Looks like the national fortune’s power gave you a significant boost.”

“Who are you?!” Provincial Governor Lü demanded. Having forcefully borne the brunt of the palm, he felt as if his organs were still quaking from the impact. Without the national fortune shielding him, that strike would have left him crippled or dead.

Every fiber of his being screamed that he was against a formidable enemy. The other party really has everything planned well. Although the national fortune’s power can theoretically elevate me to the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, that’s under the premise that I’ve mastered it. I'd just assumed office a few days ago and am not yet familiar with the national fortune.

“This sovereign is Wu Youdao.”[2]

“Wu Youdao?!” Lu Yang was stunned. Since learning about the restlessness of Great Yu cultivators, he had studied the Great Yu Dynasty’s history in detail, particularly the period of the two imperial preceptors. Though records on Wu Youdao were sparse, they had left a deep impression on Lu Yang.

“Who’s Wu Youdao?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s ignorance contrasted starkly.

“The fifth Yu emperor had seven sons, and Wu Youdao was the eldest. Legends say that auspicious clouds shaped like dragons and tigers appeared at his birth, heralding the destiny of an emperor. He was extremely talented in cultivation, drawing qi into his body at sixteen, establishing his foundation in three months, and forming his golden core in six months—the most orthodox Dragon-Tiger Golden Core among first-grade golden cores!

“With his cultivation speed, his peers were soon left in the dust. Subsequently, he disappeared, devoting himself to cultivation.

“When the fifth Yu emperor was on his deathbed, his six sons vied for the throne. It was then that Wu Youdao reappeared. The six imperial princes knew their eldest brother had the best chance of becoming the sixth Yu emperor and decided to unite against him before competing for the throne.

“With a single palm strike, Wu Youdao sent his six younger brothers flying, leaving broken limbs and bones strewn across the floor. He ascended the throne by stepping on their mangled bodies and insipidly muttered ‘boring’ as he became the sixth Yu emperor. Before long, he abdicated the throne to a younger brother, vanishing again. He had the shortest reign among all Yu emperors.

“After that, based on this palm strike, people inferred that he had already reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. If their conjecture was true, Wu Youdao’s talent would rank second among all Yu emperors!”

“Who’s first?”

“The first Yu emperor who founded the dynasty, of course.”

“Oh, so this Wu Youdao is actually pretty strong?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded and made no further comments. I can’t help but feel that he’s average. His Cosmos in Palm is also half-baked.

“So it’s the legendary Wu Youdao, born with the destiny of an emperor!” Provincial Governor Lü had naturally heard of Wu Youdao. Every Transcendent Tribulation cultivator had their unique tales and past etched into the annals of history.

“Hand over the national fortune, and I can spare your life. I honor my word,” Wu Youdao stated condescendingly, clearly thinking nothing of Provincial Governor Lü.

So what if you have the combat prowess of a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator? It’s still insufficient to be comparable to a true Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. In Wu Youdao’s eyes, Provincial Governor Lü was just a human shield. I can exhaust him through attrition and outlast him.

“Historical records wrote that you had hemorrhoids such that sitting on the throne hurt your buttocks. That was why you were the Yu emperor with the shortest reign. Looks like history doesn’t lie.” Provincial Governor Lü was not one with a forgiving tongue.

“You’re courting death!” Wu Youdao’s face turned frosty. No one has ever dared say this to me!

Whoosh! His sleeves billowed as two masses of five-colored qi appeared overhead, gradually coalescing into a thousand-zhang Qinglong (Azure Dragon) with five claws and a mountain-sized Baihu (White Tiger), protecting him on both sides.

This scene was too terrifying. The civilians of Hanshui City trembled, their hearts lodged in their throats.

“Five-Colored Tiger-Dragon Qi—this is the aura waves of a monarch, the Son of Heaven!”

“It’s over! How can we fight that?”

“We must trust in the Provincial Governor! His Excellency will definitely have a way!”

Despite what they said, they weren’t certain deep down, unsure whether Provincial Governor Lü could defeat Wu Youdao.

“Kill him! Seize the national fortune’s power!”

As the dragon and tiger attacked, Provincial Governor Lü showed no sign of fear. If he fled, the millions of civilians in Hanshui City would be doomed to become Wu Youdao’s slaves.

“Mountain-Stabilizing!” Provincial Governor Lü slammed the Wilderness Province’s official seal downward. A giant character for “Wilderness” appeared in the sky and morphed into a titanic deity wielding a weapon, fending off the tiger and dragon’s qi assault.

This was the Mountain-Stabilizing Guardian, formed from national fortune. Its name was Mountain-Stabilizing, but it actually stabilized the nation, and it was much better than Provincial Governor Lü when it came to adaptability.

“I’ve underestimated you. To think you have such a method!” Wu Youdao’s playful mood faded. He didn’t possess intelligence on the Mountain-Stabilizing Guardian. If this fight drags on, who knows what other methods the national fortune has? Should they accidentally break this certain-death situation, all our efforts in Hanshui City will go down the drain!

“The national fortune’s power will definitely make my Dragon-Tiger Qi undergo a complete transformation. Die!” Wu Youdao’s palm strike contained cosmic might, as if it was a microcosm of an entire world. The whole space buzzed and shook, seeming to be resonating.

Provincial Governor Lü suddenly found himself immobilized by an inexplicable force, as if he was sinking in quicksand.

Squelch! The palm pierced through Provincial Governor Lü’s torso, emerging from his back. With a gaping hole in his chest, he couldn’t stop coughing up blood. Some of the timid people below were so frightened that they covered their eyes.

The light in his eyes dimmed, his life force rapidly draining away.

Just as Wu Youdao prepared for the killing blow, Provincial Governor Lü’s gaze rekindled, and his chest wound knitted shut and healed with unnatural speed. Wu Youdao’s speed was a beat slower, and his right hand fused with Provincial Governor Lü’s regenerating flesh at his chest!

Insanity danced in Provincial Governor Lü’s eyes. In terms of combat, I’m no match for Wu Youdao, who’s been a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator for ages, but what I have is my physical flesh.

The national fortune’s power flowed through him, continuously repairing his battered body. By trading injury for injury, I can exhaust him through attrition and outlast him!

“Madman!” Wu Youdao cursed out loud. Despite his wealth of combat experience, it was his first time encountering an insane and reckless combat method like Provincial Governor Lü’s!

“Come at me again, you hemorrhoid trash!” Provincial Governor Lü laughed wildly through a mouth full of blood that stained his teeth crimson.

1. Since the dynasty is unclear, it can refer to an emperor, king, crown prince etc. in history. ☜

2. The surname means something like “martial,” and the given name translates to something like “has Dao.” ☜

Chapter 439: This Move Wasn’t Meant For You

Marshal An activated the great array as soon as Provincial Governor Lü and Wu Youdao clashed. A hemispherical barrier descended over Hanshui City like an inverted city, containing the shockwaves from the battle between the two.
