Thunderous explosions rocked the skies above Hanshui City as the two clashed in a deadly duel. Blows collided, lighting up the heavens with dazzling radiance too brilliant for mortal eyes to bear. Even lower-level cultivators felt a heavy pressure in their chests just watching, as if their very beings were resonating with the battle.

Wu Youdao dared not use Cosmos in Palm to pierce through Provincial Governor Lü again, lest his other hand also fuse with the latter’s regenerating flesh. With one arm trapped in Provincial Governor Lü’s chest, his movements were significantly restricted, and along with his opponent’s unnatural healing speed, Wu Youdao was surprised to find himself at a disadvantage.

“Damn it! Get lost!” Wu Youdao was exasperated, still unable to understand how Provincial Governor Lü had thought of such an absurd tactic.

When Wu Youdao punched Provincial Governor Lü’s face, the latter’s head snapped sideways before slowly righting itself.

“This move was meant for that old Taciturn scoundrel,” Provincial Governor Lü growled, madness glinting in his eyes. “Never thought you’d get the honor to experience it first!”

“Old Taciturn Scoundrel? You mean the Taciturn Daoist Priest?!” Wu Youdao felt that the name rang a bell. “It is rumored that the Taciturn Daoist Priest has enemies everywhere in the world. Could he be elevating Great Xia cultivators’ combat power by making enemies?” Wu Youdao pondered. As an emperor, I have a clear line of thinking and naturally consider more possibilities than others.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect is truly our greatest obstacle in the resurgence of Great Yu!” Wu Youdao recalled the Imperial Preceptor’s warning. He said that I must be wary of people from the Dao-Seeking Sect and that they’re formidable enemies.

Fortunately, I’ve yet to encounter any of them.

“As expected of the Provincial Governor. He might actually win at this rate!” Lu Yang’s eyes shone, impressed by Provincial Governor Lü’s reliability and relieved that he hadn’t revealed his true shifu.

Judging by Provincial Governor Lü’s brutal combat approach, his grudge against Shifu must run deep.

“He can’t win,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy observed with her battle-honed wisdom. “This combat approach only works because Wu Youdao never encountered something like it before. Once the novelty wears off and he adapts, Little Lü will be at his mercy.” With her wealth of combat experience, she saw through the flaw of the tactic at a glance.

The only way to victory is to restrain Wu Youdao first, then strike with absolute power when he least expects it. Unfortunately, Provincial Governor Lü lacks such overwhelming power.

Just as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy predicted, after Wu Youdao suffered a few beatings, he swiftly devised a countermeasure. His left hand morphed into a heavenly saber that came slashing down at Provincial Governor Lü, who evaded the attack.

However, the true target wasn’t Provincial Governor Lü—it was Wu Youdao’s own right arm!

The heavenly saber severed his right arm in one clean stroke. A torrent of blood gushed out and formed a river of blood as it cascaded down to Hanshui City, sizzling ominously as it corroded the transparent barrier. Should the barrier fail, the blood of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would undoubtedly cause a catastrophe.

Fortunately, the transparent barrier held strong until the blood’s corrosive properties were depleted.

Wu Youdao’s severed arm regenerated with terrifying speed.

“Heavenly Melody In Ears!” Regaining his freedom, Wu Youdao opened his mouth to release an ear-piercing sound that resembled a cacophony of whispers from millions of gossipers. No matter how Provincial Governor Lü covered his ears and sealed his senses, he couldn’t stop the sound from ringing in his ears.

“Supreme Threefold Force!” Wu Youdao seized the advantage to strike with a resplendent fist with the splendor of a blazing sun. “Not even a senior monk with a Sixteen-Foot Golden Body[1] could withstand the impact of this fist!” He crowed nonstop with triumph.

Disoriented by the heavenly sound, Provincial Governor Lü couldn’t detect and took the full brunt of the fist.

Splurt! He coughed up blood incessantly as the national fortune’s power rapidly healed his wounds. However, the fist contained threefold strength. The first fold inflicted severe damage, while the subsequent second and third folds inhibited recovery.

“Still not dead? Let me add one more fist!” Wu Youdao’s eyes gleamed with avarice, envisioning the national fortune nearly within his grasp.

“Great Yu emperors sure are imposing.” A steady laugh tore through the air as a Five-Colored Light Wheel suddenly appeared, shielding Provincial Governor Lü.

Wu Youdao’s punch packed so much force that the Five-Colored Light Wheel merely resisted it for two breaths.

Crack! The light wheel shattered, and Provincial Governor Lü vanished.

“Over here!”

Wu Youdao turned to see Qiu Jin’an supporting the wounded Provincial Governor Lü.

“Are you alright?”

“I’ll live.”

“It’s you! An immortal sect leader! You should be at Hundred Flowers Restaurant!” Wu Youdao gazed at Qiu Jin’an icily. I stationed two of my most powerful ghosts there.

~~~

Hundred Flowers Restaurant.

A giant ghost lay eviscerated on the ground, its three ethereal souls shredded by three chopsticks and its mouth stuffed with a bowl of rice. Numerous little ghosts littered the hall, their heads and torsos separated.

~~~

“You talking about the Bloated Ghost and Starved Ghost? Mediocre at best. Had they devoured each other and merged into a new ghost, it might’ve been mildly entertaining.

“As for those imp ghosts that can lock one’s three ethereal souls just by straddling their necks? The Dao-Seeking Sect outgrew those tricks ages ago.”

The Bloated Ghost and Starved Ghost were highly compatible ghosts. The former died from overeating, and after becoming a ghost, it would keep eating and never feel satiated. The latter died from hunger, and after becoming a ghost, it would also keep eating and never feel full. If the two ghosts consumed each other, they would merge into a ghost entity called Taotie Ghost, spelling inevitable demise for any ordinary cultivator who crossed its path.

“If you were thinking of dealing with me with just a Bloated Ghost and Starved Ghost, you gravely underestimate me.”

Wu Youdao’s eyes narrowed to slits. Countless Fusion cultivators, including those at the Advanced Fusion Stage, have fallen prey to the Bloated Ghost and Starved Ghost. Such ghost entities shouldn’t be what a Fusion cultivator can handle.

This Qiu Jin’an’s combat power exceeds my expectations.

“You focus on defense while I attack, how’s that?” Qiu Jin’an transmitted an auditory message.

“Alright.” In terms of combat, Provincial Governor Lü paled to Qiu Jin’an.

“Your Excellency, we’ve arrived!” Several Fusion cultivators appeared to support them. Previously, they were stalled by the ghost outbreaks throughout the city, but Qiu Jin’an had helped them settle the issue, allowing them to come over.

“All of you, go down and help your colleagues deal with the ghosts and maintain order in the city!” Provincial Governor Lü waved them off. This isn’t a battle where a few additional ordinary Fusion cultivators can turn the tide. Even an Apex Fusion cultivator like me will die right away without the national fortune’s power.

Only one of the strongest Fusion cultivators like Qiu Jin’an can make a difference here.

But the problem is that such Fusion cultivators with the caliber of a sect leader from the Five Great Immortal Sects don’t just show up every day.

Wu Youdao repeated his previous tactic, attempting to control Qiu Jin’an. “Heavenly Sound In...”

Qiu Jin’an’s combat experience far surpassed Provincial Governor Lü’s. He conjured a fire lotus emitting destruction intent within his palm. “Red Lotus Karmic Fire!”

Boom!

Cataclysmic energy erupted as a gigantic crimson lotus blossomed over Hanshui City. Each of its twenty-eight petals carried the power to blast domains and pocket dimensions, and the combined destructive force was unimaginable. Even behind the barrier, Lu Yang could feel the scorching heat waves.

When the smoke cleared, it revealed a sorry Wu Youdao. His robes were in tatters, his body was covered in burns, his creased skin was peeling, and his head was now bald and shiny, all traces of his usual composure and supercilious attitude gone.

“This move was meant for the Dao-Seeking Sect. It’s a pity to use it on you first.” Qiu Jin’an slowly shook his head as he conjured another crimson lotus in his palm.

1. It’s technically one zhang and 6 chi, but for naming purposes, I have gone with “Sixteen-Foot.” It’s said to be the height of this particular golden body of Buddha. ☜

Chapter 440: Am I Qualified Now?

Crimson lotuses bloomed one after another over Hanshui City, their devastating power making Lu Yang’s eyelids twitch. He was secretly relieved that Qiu Jin’an was fair-minded enough not to transfer his grudge against the Taciturn Daoist Priest to the next generation.

After unleashing five Red Lotus Karmic Fire, Qiu Jin’an’s spirit energy bottomed out. Provincial Governor Lü immediately channeled the national fortune’s power to replenish Qiu Jin’an’s spirit energy. In the blink of an eye, his spirit energy was restored in full.

With the power of the national fortune, neither injuries nor spirit energy depletion posed a problem. In the Xia Emperor’s words, “When one bears the national fortune’s power, what they fear least is protracted battles.”

Qiu Jin’an wasn’t surprised. This wasn’t his first time fighting alongside someone who wielded the national fortune’s power.

“Great! Great indeed!” Not a single part of Wu Youdao’s body was intact. The entire populace of Hanshui City could sense his murderous aura and shivered uncontrollably, feeling like they had been plunged into ice. This wasn’t an attack but simply a side effect of being so powerful that even fluctuations in his emotions could affect those in his surroundings.

“Did you think mere Red Lotus Karmic Fire could defeat me?” White mist enveloped Wu Youdao, and his injuries healed at a visible speed.

Qiu Jin’an wasn’t counting on the Red Lotus Karmic Fire to bridge the chasm between the Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation stages, but their minimal impact still disappointed him.

Lu Yang was bewildered, not understanding why the effect of Red Lotus Karmic Fire on Wu Youdao was so insignificant. “Red Lotus Karmic Fire is used by Buddhist sects to purify and redeem those who’ve committed evil. Even the slightest touch will cause it to ignite, using one’s evil karma as fuel to burn fiercely. Could it be that he has never sinned?”

Man Gu and Zhao Po were similarly perplexed.

Meng Jingzhou explained, “See Wu Youdao’s Five-Colored Dragon-Tiger Qi? This is the symbol of an emperor. How could an emperor’s deeds be judged as kind or evil?”

Qiu Jin’an and Provincial Governor Lü had realized the same thing and adjusted their combat approach.

However, Wu Youdao didn’t give the two a chance to react by striking first, with countless chains materializing behind him. “Stupa Purgatory Palm!”

The ink-black chains stretched like a prison, as if they were forged from some mystical black iron yet seemingly condensed from tremendous magical power. The state of their existence was extremely bizarre.

“Transcendent Tribulation cultivators can create non-existent materials. Wu Youdao likely refined these chains!” Qiu Jin’an erupted with Five-Colored Divine Light that dissolved the chains’ “metallic” essence, leaving only their external framework condensed from magical power.

Qiu Jin’an’s words reminded Lu Yang of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s creation of the Mother-Child River and Twins River. If Transcendent Tribulation cultivators could create non-existent materials, an immortal’s capabilities would be even stronger.

Although the chains were no longer a threat, the force in Wu Youdao’s palm strike remained heavy and unavoidable.

Qiu Jin’an was not daunted and manifested five mini flames that were the color of liuli-glaze at his fingertips. As he transformed his fist into a palm, the five flames merged, and their aura leaked out from the gaps between his fingers, sufficient to warp space.

“Liuli-Glaze Purification Fire!”

The flames collided with the Stupa Purgatory Palm, resembling a standoff between dragons and tigers. However, due to Qiu Jin’an’s inadequate cultivation and depleting power, the Liuli-Glaze Purification Fire waned.

“Don’t forget about me!” Provincial Governor Lü pressed his palm against Qiu Jin’an, infusing him with an endless stream of spirit energy to reinvigorate the flames.

“Supreme Threefold Force!” Wu Youdao suddenly withdrew his power and delivered another palm strike. Every fold of the Supreme Threefold Force was stronger than the previous, dispelling the flames and smashing into Qiu Jin’an’s chest.

Qiu Jin’an quickly sealed his acupoints to lock the Threefold Force rampaging within his body.

“Three Thousand Weak Water!” Qiu Jin’an spewed forth Weak Water. The vast stream flowed ceaselessly and engulfed Wu Youdao, who tried to struggle free. But Weak Water was the lightest substance in the world—goose feathers couldn’t float, and reed flowers sank to the bottom. Even with Wu Youdao’s cultivation, escape was nearly impossible.

“Xirang!” Qiu Jin’an produced a chunk of Xirang soil, the legendary immortal soil personally used by an immortal. He should have conserved it wherever possible, but he couldn’t care that much now.

The Xirang Soil expanded exponentially upon contacting the Weak Water and buried Wu Youtao.

Splurt! Qiu Jin’an finally coughed up several mouthfuls of blood he had been holding in. This was due to the might of the Supreme Threefold Force. If he had vomited blood earlier, that would have given Wu Youdao an opening to secure absolute victory.

Provincial Governor Lü rushed over to heal Qiu Jin’an, shouldering part of the impact from the Supreme Threefold Force.

Crack! The Weak Water and Xirang Soil couldn’t trap Wu Youdao for long. Burning with fury, he attacked Qiu Jin’an. He could tell that his most intractable opponent was Qiu Jin’an, while Provincial Governor Lü was further behind in priority.

“Five-Colored Divine Light!” Qiu Jin’an fought desperately, casting Five-Colored Divine Light in succession and hurling five-element items one after another. Just the true fire he used alone already comprised thirty types!

Wu Youdao stopped holding back, activating his killing blow. “Heaven-Shocking Finger!” Although the name stated a “finger,” it referred to a world, condensing the power of Cosmos in Palm within his forefinger, and his fingerprints were wide enough for four horses to gallop abreast!

“Three flowers gather at the crown; five qi point to the origin.”[1] Qiu Jin’an refined essence into qi, qi into mind, and mind into void before gathering all at the crown of his head, rendering him impervious to myriad tribulations. Five qi—metal, wood, water, fire, and earth—converged to the origin and returned to the Yellow Court position at the dantian, achieving a state of clarity and wonder.

“Tanggu Valley[2] Water! Fusang Tree Wood! Jinwu Crow True Fire!” Qiu Jin’an whipped out three treasures, recreating the birth of the ten suns, surpassing even Meng Tian True Lord’s “Heaven-Patrolling Ten Suns” in might!

“Fusang Tree Wood? So the Fusang Tree has fallen into your hands!”

The two clashed in a brutal battle, both forsaking defense and opting for extreme offense to attack the other party, trading injury for injury.

Provincial Governor Lü struggled to follow their movements and could only focus on healing Qiu Jin’an as much as he could.

Suddenly, Qiu Jin’an was sent flying from a kick. It was unclear how many ribs were broken, and even his soul was damaged and shaken from the impact.

“Splendid!” Wu Youdao was stronger than Qiu Jin’an. Despite the injuries, his core was not affected, and his soul was unharmed. “It’s my first time meeting a Fusion cultivator who can trade blows with me!”

“Can you still fight?” Provincial Governor Lü secretly transmitted his voice as he healed Qiu Jin’an.

“Damn it! My offensive methods aren’t enough!” Qiu Jin’an was getting frustrated and cursed, “If only we had one more Fusion cultivator like me or even someone like the old Taciturn scoundrel, we could win!”

“Where would we find such a person?” Provincial Governor Lü asked. If it’s just a matter of numbers, that would be manageable, but a few Fusion cultivators are clearly not going to tip the scale in our case.

Wu Youdao guffawed, unconcerned about the two’s discussion. “I’ve inspected Hanshui City thoroughly. There’s no such person here.”

“Is that so? Have you inspected me?” An unfamiliar voice came from below, instantly putting the three on high alert.

“Who’s speaking?”

A man in a white paper hat slowly flew out of a house where the Sacrificial Ghost was supposed to be stationed, ascending to the sky step by step.

Wu Youdao saw through the white paper-hatted man’s cultivation realm at a glance and sneered at how the latter had overestimated himself. “You? A mere Basic Fusion cultivator? You think you’re qualified to join our battle?”

The white paper-hatted man didn’t reply.

At the same time, hundreds of civilians stepped out of their homes and onto the deserted streets, making their presence all the more conspicuous.

Some malevolent ghosts saw them and fiercely lunged at them for the kill, but one of the civilians casually killed the ghosts instead.

These hundreds of people had varied appearances and backgrounds—thieves, swindlers, bookkeepers, restaurant waiters, and even barbeque shop staff.

As the white paper-hatted man walked higher up into the sky, these people flew up and fused into him one by one. The man’s cultivation surged like a raging river, so fast that it caused one’s heart to tremble.

Basic Fusion Stage, Intermediate Fusion Stage, Advanced Fusion Stage...Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

Standing before Wu Youdao, he asked impassively, “Am I qualified now?”

1. This is a common phrase for the cultivation of the inner core. The “three flowers” actually refer to the essence, qi, and mind, while the “five qi” actually refer to the five organs. ☜

2. Tanggu is a valley where the sun rose from in legends. It is also home to the Fusang Tree. ☜

Chapter 441: The Tide Turns

“Immortal Fairy, are you saying this person’s cultivation rose from the Basic Fusion Stage all the way to the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” Lu Yang asked in astonishment, struggling to understand what had happened.

The Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage wasn’t an actual cultivation stage but rather a symbol of one’s combat prowess. Those whose combat power surpassed ordinary Fusion cultivators but had yet to reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage could be referred to as Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

“Haven’t I told you before? This is a cultivation method to train one’s soul. By splitting into countless incarnations to experience mortal lives and comprehend the mundane world before finally fusing back together, one can return to their peak or even attain higher heights.

”This person’s cultivation technique is similar to that Shop Manager Shi’s.”

After a pause, Lu Yang realized she was talking about Vice Creed Leader Shi of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. “He’s from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?”

“More than that. Based on the correlation between cultivation and status, he’s probably at the level of creed leader.”

Lu Yang was nonplussed, though he was more confused than shocked. “Is the Nine-Netherworlds Creed so poor that its creed leader must personally take on menial jobs?”

~~~

The white paper-hatted man sighed. “All my clones have returned, and I can’t use these identities anymore. How many spirit stones will it cost me this time?

“What other choice do I have? There’s a grudge between us and archaic cultivators like you.” He worked industriously to earn money, worried that his creed followers would find out about their massive debts, which were even used for construction and salaries in the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Even if I advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage in the future, I may not live if this matter gets exposed. I must toil away and work extra jobs while I’m still alive to fill the deficit—the more I earn, the higher my chance of survival.

Just like Vice Creed Leader Shi viewed the barbeque shop as their last life-saving straw to clutch at, so did the white paper-hatted man.

Wu Youdao demanded, “Who are you?!”

In the presence of the righteous path, the white paper-hatted man naturally couldn’t reveal that he was from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

So, he could only smirk.

In everyone’s eyes, it portrayed him in a mysterious light, though to be fair, his identity as creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was already mysterious enough.

“Talk is useless. Great Yu cultivator, it’s time to settle both our old and new scores together!” The white paper-hatted man understood that loose lips sank ships, so he attacked Wu Youdao without another word.

“Impudent cur, how dare you strike me first?! Avici Hell—Grand Millstone!”

A gigantic iceberg half the size of Hanshui City formed above Wu Youdao. It resembled mystic black ice that never melted and was on the verge of absolute cold.

Infernal flames erupted beneath Wu Youdao’s feet without boundary, burning more wildly than a prairie fire.

Trapped between the iceberg and flames like millstones, Wu Youdao couldn’t budge. “Heh, you dare challenge me with such petty tricks?”

“Count me in!” Qiu Jin’an joined, his hands nimbly forming seals to cast elemental spells.

The ancient mystic black ice grew even colder, such that even space and time had signs of stasis. The infernal flames were shrouded in a layer of black—Nether World Ghost Fire, which specialized in scorching souls.

Wu Youdao’s expression shifted. Their combined attack can threaten my life!

Crack. Crack. The sound of grinding bones could be heard as the blood of a Transcendent Tribulation Stage—immune to freezing or searing—oozed out from the edge of the millstone.

“Cosmos in Palm!” Wu Youdao roared and unleashed a strike in fury. Numerous tiny worlds overlapped and shattered the Avici Hell Grand Millstone!

“Form a Three Talents Array!”[1] Qiu Jin’an commanded, emboldened by the appearance of the white paper-hatted man.

“I command the power of the Five Elements—I’ll take the Heaven position!

“You’ve cast Avici Hell—take the Earth position!

“Lord Lü, you’re the provincial governor and a parent to the people—take the Mortal position!”

The renowned Three Talents Array was born in the ancient era, but there was rarely a chance to set it up successfully, for it imposed strict requirements on fate profile and cultivation.

Without hesitation, the three assumed their respective positions according to their fate profile. Once the Three Talents Array formed, the three instantly sensed they had become one unified whole, their powers elevating and their souls becoming firmer.

“Supreme Threefold Force!” Wu Youdao swung his fist, his fist seal flashing, and wherever the fist light cut through, space fractured, sealing off all possibilities of escape.

The fist closed in, landing squarely in the white paper-hatted man’s abdomen. The threefold force rippled through the trio—he bore the first wave, Qiu Jin’an the second, and Provincial Governor Lü the strongest third. In this way, the full force of the blow was greatly diminished.

Bolstered by the Three Talents Array, the national fortune’s power circulated between them more rapidly. The three were immediately healed, as if they had never suffered the blow.

“Attack!” The three operated the Three Talents Array to unleash their strongest move, engaging with Wu Youdao again.

The four of them had their bodies battered and healed over and over again. Injuries considered fatal for low-level cultivators didn’t even tickle them, simply draining a bit of their spirit energy.

“Huff...huff...” Wu Youdao’s chest heaved. He had been beaten more times than his opponents had, depleting significant spirit energy that couldn’t be recovered even by consuming pills. Every attempt to leave the battlefield was thwarted by the siege from the three.

“Damn it!”

“Five-Colored Divine Light!”

“Mortar-and-Pestle Hell!”[2]

“Mountain-Stabilizing Guardian!”

The three dished out their ultimate moves, dispersing the Five-Colored Tiger-Dragon Qi. Wu Youdao took the brunt of all three-strikes head-on, leaving his body a mangled wreck that could only recover sluggishly.

Hanshui City’s civilians cheered at this scene, and the dread Wu Youdao had cast over their hearts gradually dissipated.

“Enough spectacting! Come out and help!” Wu Youdao roared.

A gloomy old voice answered as an old man with a crutch appeared. “Your Majesty, this doesn’t seem like you. I didn’t know you could beg for help.”

“Azure Lightning, this isn’t begging for help—it’s this sovereign’s order!” Wu Youdao glowered at the old man.

“There’s not much difference.” The old man called Azure Lightning cackled, revealing his nearly toothless mouth.

“Azure Lightning...Could it be the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord?!” Provincial Governor Lü murmured, his dumbstruck gaze darting between Qiu Jin’an and the white paper-hatted man for confirmation, only to find matching astonishment in their eyes.

Having heard of Azure Lightning Venerable Lord’s reputation, the trio could feel their hearts sink. This is a Basic Transcendent Tribulation expert well-versed in lightning spells.

Yet another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Fighting one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator is already so tough, let alone two?!

“Hehe, I advise the three of you to surrender now. Our goal is only the national fortune’s power.” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord chuckled in his rasping voice. His crutch flickered with lightning, as if thunder strikes would descend as soon as Provincial Governor Lü dared to reject them.

The trio gave no reply, and an uncanny silence draped over them.

Suddenly, a thunderclap boomed, breaking the silence.

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord froze for a second. I haven’t made a move yet.

Provincial Governor Lü’s eyes lit up as he turned toward the sound. “It’s Sect Leader Lu! He’s about to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!”

~~~

At the Corpse-Driving Sect, Elder Gai spat on the corpse of the Witchcraft Corpse Sect’s members strewn across the ground. “Pah! What kind of pathetic joke is this? They wanted to test us with this level of skills? Don’t they know how to keep up with the times?”

“You...you...these aren’t Corpse-Driving Techniques...” The last surviving member of the Witchcraft Corpse Sect raised his trembling hand and pointed at Elder Gai as the light in him dimmed.

He couldn’t believe what he had witnessed earlier. Despite being alive, his body was refined by Elder Gai, becoming a true living walking corpse[3] and losing control of his own body. And all those other strange and eerie spells. Before Elder Gai and the other three, the Witchcraft Corpse Sect’s proud archaic Corpse-Driving Techniques didn’t provide them any advantage.

“How are they not Corpse-Driving Techniques? The Dao-Seeking Sect had enhanced them for us!” Elder Gai puffed out his chest proudly.

“All of you should meditate and recover now. We’ll need to head to the city to help in a bit,” Elder Gai beckoned the others. The battle just now had drained them significantly.

Heavenly thunder reverberated overhead, causing the four startled elders to look up.

Elder Gai was the first to react, joy flooding his heart. “The sect leader is about to break through!”

1. The “Three Talents” refer to heaven, earth, and mortal. ☜

2. One of the eighteen levels of hell. ☜

3. The original Chinese term is actually made up of “alive” and “corpse,” and the first character is the same character used in the term for a “living person.” ☜

Chapter 442: White Emperor Dragon Transformation Tribulation

The thunderclap seized everyone’s attention. The Yin-Corpse Mountain Range, where the Corpse-Driving Sect was located, had never experienced thunder since ancient times due to its overwhelming yin energy.

Yet today, clouds loomed over the mountain range as blinding white lightning crisscrossed the sky. It was as if the world had returned to its primordial state at the beginning of time, brimming with vitality.

“All disciples of the Corpse-Driving Sect, evacuate immediately!” Elder Gai organized a mass exodus. Sect Leader Lu’s breakthrough was faster than anticipated, rendering the Corpse-Driving Sect extremely dangerous. The chances of being struck by the lightning tribulation had become frighteningly high, and such lightning tribulation from a breakthrough to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage was beyond what ordinary disciples could withstand. Even a brush with it would mean demise!

Provincial Governor Lü’s party and Wu Youdao’s party ceased fighting with a tacit understanding. Near lightning tribulation of this level, there mustn’t be any energy fluctuations. Otherwise, one could easily be misinterpreted as interfering with the process, becoming the target of the lightning tribulation.

Provincial Governor Lü and the other two seized this moment of respite to recuperate, preparing for the next phase of battle. They counted their blessings, relieved to have Sect Leader Lu join them. The scales were balanced again, and the outcome of their fight with the Great Yu cultivators was still uncertain!

Excitement coursed through every fiber of Zhao Po’s being. How long has it been—nine thousand or ten thousand years? Since another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator hasn’t been seen in our Corpse-Driving Sect, we were downgraded from an S-class sect to a first-class sect. But today, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator is finally going to appear! Will we be regaining our former glory as an S-class sect?!

This was the difference between the Five Great Immortal Sects and S-class sects. The latter required just one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, but all cultivators would perish one day. When that day arrived, S-class sects would become first-class sects.

On the other hand, even if the Five Great Immortal Sects weakened to a point where they couldn’t produce even one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator across multiple generations, the sects could still rely on their methods comparable to those at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and retain their title as an immortal sect.

The Dao-Seeking Sect had experienced such a period fifty thousand years ago, where no Transcendent Tribulation cultivator was born within a span of two thousand years. This lasted until the emergence of their Resurgence Ancestor, Vast Sea Daoist Lord. Throughout that drought, however, the sect remained one of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

The lightning tribulation continued brewing in the sky, with only sporadic lightning strikes that shook heaven and earth, yet they couldn’t even qualify as a prelude.

The roiling dark clouds descended like a collapsing ceiling as white lightning flashed and erupted in full fury, enveloping the Corpse-Driving Sect. The accumulated yin energy of Yin-Corpse Mountain Range that had persisted for millennia began dissipating.

A howl reverberated through the air, faintly matching the lightning tribulation’s might. A figure clad in Daoist robes burst forth from seclusion and soared into the sky, dishing out numerous magical treasures, evidently well-prepared.

“So this is what undergoing a lightning tribulation is like,” Lu Yang muttered in awe. Though he had heard tales of cultivators facing lightning tribulation, today was his first time witnessing it. Moreover, it was an unparalleled Transcendent Tribulation-tier lightning tribulation. Even half a Hanshui City away, he could sense the heaven and earth trembling, a testament to the power of the lightning tribulation above the Corpse-Driving Sect.

“This lightning tribulation is average at best.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, not at all impressed. If it were me, I could simply yawn and still pass through it. I wouldn’t need these elaborate preparations.

“Is there anything special about lightning tribulations?” Lu Yang recalled that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was an expert on lightning tribulations. After all, the current lightning tribulations had originated from the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit.

“The Heavenly Mandate Immortal created lightning tribulations to temper cultivators, not strike them to death. The stronger the lightning tribulation, the greater the talent it signifies. Look at this lightning tribulation. It’s flashy and looks like the real deal, but if you experience it firsthand, you’d find its power mediocre.

“This particular lightning tribulation is called the ‘White Emperor Dragon Transformation Tribulation.’ It’s considered to be on the weaker side among lightning tribulations.”

The white lightning morphed into a dragon emperor—whiskers flowing, scales shimmering, and claws bared—as though it was possessed by a real dragon and had developed spirit intelligence.

With a deafening roar, the white dragon-emperor collided with Sect Leader Lu, piercing straight through his body and revealing ghastly white bones wreathed in deathly energy.

“Is the Sect Leader going to die?!” Lu Yang was flabbergasted. Sect Leader Lu’s failure came so swiftly?

“No, this is a walking corpse. His true body is hiding below, and that’s a pretty clever tactic. He knew that the first wave of heavenly lightning was too strong for him to resist, so he used his walking corpse to block it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw through Sect Leader Lu’s minor trick at a glance.

Just as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had said, while the walking corpse was sundered under the lightning, the true Sect Leader Lu burst forth from the soil to confront the lightning tribulation, whose power had diminished after its first wave of attack.

The white dragon-emperor struck again, eliciting agonized screams from Sect Leader Lu as the lightning rays left their mark on him by searing both his flesh and soul. He hurriedly fished out a jade vial and swallowed a recovery pill before the remaining contents, along with the vial, vanished into the vast lightning maelstrom.

The white dragon-emperor’s momentum was unstoppable as it crushed void and space, constantly hammering at Sect Leader Lu and making him feel like he was experiencing the vicissitudes of life.

Suddenly, the heavenly tribulation dissipated. The pressure was reduced, and the frenzied spirit energy gradually calmed down.

Sect Leader Lu was charred from head to toe, resembling a piece of coal that fell to the ground with a thud.

“He failed?” Everyone in the city felt their hearts sink, and murmurs spread through the crowd. If Sect Leader Lu had failed his tribulation to advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, no one else could oppose the Great Yu cultivators.

“Look! The sect leader moved!”

Thump, thump, thump.

It was the sound of a powerful heartbeat. This was a sign of his internal injuries healing and his hidden wounds disappearing. Then came a cracking sound. Sect Leader Lu’s charred layer split apart, revealing new, translucent skin beneath. He now looked over a decade younger.

Elder Gai exclaimed agitatedly, “The lightning tribulation encompassed vitality. The lightning cleansed the sect leader’s body, so his physical body must have become stronger by severalfold, or even tenfold!” He recalled texts describing the breakthrough to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage of the Corpse-Driving Sect’s talented forebear.

Sect Leader Lu’s eyes snapped open; they resembled bolts of lightning that pierced the clouds. He rose to his feet and was overflowing with vitality, a stark contrast to his sorry state when he countered the lightning tribulation. He was now a different person and radiated confidence. He had survived the lightning tribulation and become a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!

The entire city erupted in celebration, including Provincial Governor Lü’s trio and the civilians. Their hearts finally settled down upon confirming that Sect Leader Lu’s breakthrough was a success.

Only Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou weren’t happy. During the lightning tribulation, the lightning had torn away Sect Leader Lu’s clothes. The two locked their gazes on his right wrist, their scalps tingling and their blood running cold.

Three interlocking rings with the character for “ghost” written in the center!

This was the same mark they had seen on the masterless walking corpses when they came to Wilderness Province to spend the night. The village chief’s explanation echoed in their minds.

“There are mainly two reasons walking corpses are masterless. Either the master has died, freeing the walking corpses from their control and leaving them to wander, or the master voluntarily lifted the control over the walking corpses, where a third possibility is that the walking corpses turned on their master and devoured them.”

A walking corpse could resist a lightning tribulation, but Sect Leader Lu couldn’t have voluntarily relinquished control of his walking corpse.

But Sect Leader Lu stood before them, and it ruled out the third possibility of the walking corpse devouring its master.

That left only the first possibility—Sect Leader Lu had died, and his walking corpse had wandered to Jianshi Village, where it was discovered by the village chief!

If Sect Leader Lu is dead, who’s the one controlling his body now?!

The two exchanged glances, instantly thinking of the same possibility.

“A Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator has taken over Sect Leader Lu’s body!”

Chapter 443: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy Makes a Move

A Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator had taken over Sect Leader Lu’s body—everything suddenly made sense.

Why were there no records of Fusion cultivators clashing?

It’s because a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator can effortlessly take over a Fusion cultivator’s body!

Why was an unremarkable Sect Leader Lu the first among his generation to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?

It’s because his body had already been taken over by a Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator! For the latter, it’s equivalent to reentering the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, so the process was naturally a cinch for him!

These were all deductions, for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou lacked concrete proof. However, they couldn’t conceive of any other possibility that explained everything!

As Provincial Governor Lü and the rest were about to head over to the Corpse-Driving Sect to offer their congratulations, they heard Sect Leader Lu burst into uncharacteristically unbridled laughter.

“At last, at long last, I’ve returned to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!”

“Wait, you’re not Lu Baqian! Who are you?!” Provincial Governor Lü immediately demanded, an ominous feeling growing in his heart.

Wu Youdao and the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord congratulated “Sect Leader Lu.”

“Congratulations on your successful advancement, Fellow Daoist Witchcraft Sacrifice.”

Elder Gai’s pupils constricted, his face filled with incredulity. “Witchcraft Sacrifice? The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord?! From the Witchcraft Corpse Sect?!” The Witchcraft Corpse Sect had managed to become a S-class sect precisely because of this Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!

During the battle earlier, Elder Gai was puzzled about historical records stating that the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s whereabouts were unknown, likely in slumber and preparing to awaken for the Great Era. But if that was the case, why were only Fusion cultivators from the Witchcraft Corpse Sect involved in the fight? Where was the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord?

Now, he had finally received his answer. The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord has been right under our noses all along!

With three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators on Great Yu’s side, Qiu Jin’an’s predicament grew increasingly dire.

The white paper-hatted man gnashed his teeth as he glowered at the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord, who had taken over Sect Leader Lu’s body. Huang Ming and Meng Tian had already confessed to me about this matter, and it’s also one of the reasons why I’ve steeled my resolve to deal with these Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

Due to Corpse Drivers having a different outlook on life and death, there were rumors in the external world claiming that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s founder was originally from the Corpse-Driving Sect.

In truth, this was just a rumor, but it got one thing correct—the Corpse Drivers’ philosophies on life and death were close to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s, resulting in the two factions having favorable impressions of each other.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader was naturally incensed to see the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord. His original plan was to cooperate with Qiu Jin’an to eliminate Wu Youdao before the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord could return to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

However, fate had other plans. He didn’t expect the Great Yu’s party to include the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, and the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord had undergone tribulation earlier than anticipated.

With his full contingent assembled, Wu Youdao showed his original rapacious and ferocious colors. “Provincial Governor Lü, I have already given you a chance to surrender the national fortune. Since you refuse, I can only take it by force!”

The moment the last word left his mouth, the three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators attacked simultaneously, targeting Provincial Governor Lü, causing even the spirit energy in Hanshui City to go berserk. This cataclysmic strike immediately pushed Provincial Governor Lü to the brink of death. Thankfully, the national fortune saved him; otherwise, he would have died on the spot.

Provincial Governor Lü fell with a crash, hitting the estate and landing beside Lu Yang.

Lu Yang’s eyelids twitched. Things can’t get any worse. Great Yu has three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. The gulf in strength is too massive.

Wu Youdao remarked, “The national fortune’s power is truly impressive. Even that couldn’t kill you. I’m more and more bent on obtaining its power. I wonder the extent of metamorphosis my Dragon-Tiger Qi will go through.”

Provincial Governor Lü forced himself to hang in there, not afraid of dying. His voice dripped with scorn. “Do you really believe killing me would grant you the national fortune’s power? Absolutely risible! Even if I die, the national fortune will return to its source. You will not get a single bit!”

“Is that so?” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s lips twisted into an eerie rictus as he produced a familiar talisman. “Take a guess—why did I choose to take over this particular body?”

“Soul-Dispelling Talisman!” Provincial Governor Lü recognized the talisman, a sense of foreboding filling him. The local authorities and the Corpse-Driving Sect had rushed out these talismans overnight to settle the ghost calamities. The one the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord is holding is the main talisman. It was even imprinted with the Wilderness Province’s official seal to amplify its power.

What is he trying to accomplish by taking out this talisman now?!

The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord raised the talisman, and countless specks of light ignited across Hanshui City—these were all locations where Soul-Dispelling Talismans had been used.

“Array, rise!” The talisman in the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s hand burst into flames. Across Hanshui City, the spots of light intensified and linked together, forming a great array.

Provincial Governor Lü could feel the power of the national fortune being stripped from his body bit by bit, gradually becoming masterless.

“I’ve gone through great pains to take over this body—all for this moment!” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord cackled nonstop; everyone in Hanshui City could hear this grating laughter.

“After the previous provincial governor was removed and other factions were distrusted by the imperial court, a newly appointed provincial governor like you can only believe our Corpse-Driving Sect. With the ghost calamities, only our sect could resolve the problem!

“The Corpse-Driving Sect crafted these Soul-Dispelling Talismans together with you local authorities, so every talisman naturally carries the intention of the authorities. Along with the imprint from the Wilderness Province’s official seal, such intention was augmented.

“Using the malevolent ghosts as anchor points, I made the disciples use talismans to eliminate the ghosts. Once the talismans and ghostly energy combine, they will form the array’s nodes.”

All the array masters’ conjectures were wrong. Hanshui City’s array was neither constructed using malevolent spirits as nodes nor intended to disrupt the yin-yang balance—instead, its setup relied on Soul-Dispelling Talismans. However, they were completely in the dark about the existence of the Soul-Dispelling Talismans, so no one noticed the problem with the talismans.

“The talismans and dispelling the ghosts were all the intentions of the authorities, so the array also bears your intention. This is tantamount to the authorities intentionally giving up the national fortune’s power!” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s mouth twisted into a mocking smile. The condition for making the national fortune masterless is extremely strict—it requires the authorities to voluntarily give it up.

To achieve that, I’ve arranged all of this, just so I can obtain the national fortune’s power!

Sensing the control of the national fortune slipping from his grasp and becoming masterless, Provincial Governor Lü was wracked with helplessness. Had it been an experienced provincial governor, they wouldn’t have made such a fatal mistake.

“We mustn’t let them obtain the national fortune’s power!” Qiu Jin’an and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader hastily intervened.

But how could they be a match for three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators?

“Supreme Threefold Force!”

“Heavenly Punishment Thunderstrike!”

“Thousand-Li Corpse Energy!”

The three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators synchronized their assault, sending Qiu Jin’an and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s leader flying out and coughing blood incessantly.

A material resembling both light and water drifted out from Provincial Governor Lü’s body, turning into strands and fragments as it floated to the sky.

Seeing his dream national fortune, Wu Youdao extended his hand and executed Cosmos in Palm, crushing down toward Provincial Governor Lü.

And right beside him were Lu Yang and the others.

“The national fortune’s power is now this sovereign’s!”

“This immortal finds this national fortune’s power pretty satisfactory. Why don’t you let me use it first?” A frivolous voice suddenly echoed through heaven and earth, its source untraceable.

A figure suddenly appeared between Provincial Governor Lü and the giant hand, reaching out a slender jade hand to absorb all the national fortune.

“Are you not embarrassed to call this Cosmos in Palm?” The woman sneered and lifted her palm, sending Wu Youdao’s massive hand flying.

Wu Youdao clutched his wrist fixedly to stop it from trembling uncontrollably, a sliver of panic flickering in his eyes.

The woman was shrouded in the power of the national fortune. Though her appearance was obscured, she had a pretty figure and jade-like feet. Like a fairy immortal who had descended upon the mortal world, she felt inviolable and divine, involuntarily making people desire to prostrate before her in worship.

“Who are you?!” Wu Youdao glared at the mysterious woman fixedly, finding her profound and unfathomable. That strike that blew off my palm didn’t surpass the limits of the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, but her precise control over power far outclasses mine!

But how is that possible?!

The mysterious woman looked at Wu Youdao in disdain, parting her lips gently and lazily announcing her title. “This immortal is Dou Heavenly Sovereign, the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign of the Heavenly Court Creed.”

Chapter 444: Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign of the Heavenly Court Creed!

“Heavenly Court Creed? Dou (Battle)[ref]Take note that the “dou” here is the character for battle/fight instead of bean as in Huang Doudou./ref] Heavenly Sovereign?” Wu Youdao stared at the divine maiden before him in bewilderment, an uneasy feeling rising in his heart.

He had allowed Provincial Governor Lü to make his move, and even when Qiu Jin’an and the white paper-hatted man intervened, he remained confident of his victory. Against absolute power, he believed these people couldn’t stir up any waves.

But now, he felt like things were spiraling beyond his control.

And never in his life had he felt this way before.

“What is the Heavenly Court Creed? And what’s Dou (Battle) Heavenly Sovereign?” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord exchanged a glance with the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord, seeing the panic in each other’s eyes.

Their goal was to seize the national fortune’s power. When Wu Youdao was about to grasp it just now, they had been watching their surroundings intently. They were convinced that not a single movement could have escaped their detection.

Yet, this woman appeared before us under everyone’s eyes, and no one had seen how she arrived.

How is that possible?!

Their minds raced through all the intelligence they had collected, but from ancient times to the present, there was no matching record of a “Heavenly Court Creed” or a “Dou (Battle) Heavenly Sovereign.” The closest were the current Four Great Diabolic Creeds: the Everlasting Creed, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, the Radiant Sun Creed, and the Heartless Creed.

“There seem to be records of a Heavenly Court in ancient texts!” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s voice quivered, fear crawling through his heart.

“An ancient organization?!” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord gasped under his breath. He believed in the notion that the older something was, the more powerful it was. As someone who had lived for over a hundred thousand years, he looked down on the current Great Xia Dynasty, positive that Great Yu cultivators were the strongest.

But now, the Dou (Battle) Heavenly Sovereign seemed to hail from the most ancient of times.

And with “Dou (Battle)” as her honorific title, she must be an expert in combat!

“Hold on, did she just refer to herself as ‘this immortal?!’” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord recalled a detail that had been overlooked but was of utmost importance.

“She’s an immortal?!”

No matter their schemes and calculations, they had never expected an immortal to be hiding in Hanshui City!

An immortal with the honorific title of “Dou (Battle)” likely possesses formidable combat power even among immortals!

~~~

“Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign of the Heavenly Court Creed?” At first, the white paper-hatted man was perplexed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s appearance, unsure of who she was. But now that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had announced her identity, everything clicked for him.

He remembered the message Vice Creed Leader Shi had sent him, saying that someone from the Heavenly Court Creed had arrived in Hanshui City. The message also mentioned that the Heavenly Court Creed was displeased upon hearing rumors that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was behind the ghost calamities. Fortunately, Vice Creed Leader Shi had clarified the matter to avoid affecting their collaboration.

Now that he thought about it, the white paper-hatted man felt a chill of lingering fear. The “someone” from the Heavenly Court Creed is probably none other than this Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign before me. “Thank goodness this matter was already clarified.”

Who is the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign? That was the first immortal in ancient times and an unparalleled being that even the Four Ancient Immortals feared!

“You know this person?” Qiu Jin’an noticed the white paper-hatted man’s peculiar expression and secretly transmitted an auditory message to him.

“This is an ineffable puissant personage.” The white paper-hatted dared not and was unwilling to elaborate on the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign.

Qiu Jin’an raised an eyebrow, hesitating as he wanted to say more, but the words couldn’t leave his mouth.

~~~

“Lord Lü, are you alright?” While everyone else’s attention was drawn by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy bathed in national fortune, Lu Yang was the only one who noticed Provincial Governor Lü still coughing up blood.

“Cough cough...I’ll manage.” Provincial Governor Lü struggled to his feet, fishing out a few pills from his storage ring before swallowing them and meditating.

Only then did Lu Yang look up at the center of attention high up in the sky. A faint smile tugged at the corners of his mouth as he recalled the last words the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had uttered before joining the battle.

“I already said I’d ensure your safety in Wilderness Province.”

~~~

“Hmph, what immortal? It’s nothing but bluster!” Wu Youdao steadied himself. If this person before me were truly an immortal, I would have died from that strike earlier.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chuckled softly, looking at Wu Youdao in contempt. “Ignorant fool. What stands before you is but a wisp of this immortal’s thought. Seeing that this national fortune’s power was serviceable, I saw fit to borrow it. Can’t the juniors of later generations understand something so simple?”

Wu Youdao, after all, held the title of the second strongest among Yu emperors throughout history; he wasn’t one to be cowed so easily. “The national fortune can only elevate you to the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, just like the three of us. Do you truly believe you can win against three at once?”

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord and Witchcraft Venerable Lord also realized the same thing. This person might indeed be an immortal, but her true form isn’t here. The one controlling the national fortune is only a wisp of her thought.

Since her power is still at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, there’s nothing to fear.

As fellow Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, who’s to say who is weaker?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke again, her tone indifferent. “If it were Heaven Mandate, Qilin, or Nine-Layers at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they might pose some threat to this immortal. But as for you three trash...” She shook her head lightly, saying no more.

The so-called “second strongest among Yu emperors” was nothing special in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes. It’s not like second strongest among Yu emperors means second strongest in the ten thousand years of the Great Yu Dynasty.

Seeing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s attitude, Wu Youdao flew into a rage and bellowed, “Cosmos in Palm!”

Though it was daytime, the entire Hanshui City was abruptly plunged into darkness. Countless commoners instinctively looked up and shivered uncontrollably.

A colossal hand had blotted out the sky above Hanshui City. In the eyes of the mortals below, its size was indiscernible. They simply felt that the enormous hand had eclipsed everything, even the heavens.

Qiu Jin’an and the white paper-hatted man perceived more than that. Within the palm of the colossal hand were all things in the cosmos and countless pocket dimensions and domains containing immeasurable power. Once this palm slammed down, it would reduce all of Hanshui City to dust.

Faced with this terrifying hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t even bat an eyelid. “This immortal has told you that this petty trick isn’t worthy to be called ‘Cosmos in Palm.’ Today, I shall let you witness the true Cosmos in Palm.’”

Wu Youdao’s heart lurched. He jerked his head up, disbelief written across his face.

The crowd below couldn’t see the situation above; only Wu Youdao could.

A massive pillar pierced through the layers of cloud, appearing directly above the hand, its tip still tinged with clouds that had yet to disperse.

This was no pillar—it was a finger!

A finger even larger than the hand!

“It’s just a bit bigger. I refuse to believe a single finger of yours can defeat my palm!” Wu Youdao roared in fury, channeling his spirit energy madly. His gigantic hand flipped, and his palm now faced upward. Despite the simple motion, it stirred hurricanes across Hanshui City.

Pocket domains manifested within Wu Youdao’s palm one after another, each brimming with exotic flora and troves of natural treasures. Every domain was both a tiny world and a treasury.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched the frenzied Wu Youdao with detached aloofness, then pressed down slightly with her fingertip. Within that fingertip were endless galaxies, with stars shattering and reforming in an eternal cycle, unleashing tremendous energy.

When the fingertip met the hand, Wu Youdao’s hand didn’t last long before it was poked into oblivion by the finger.

Bang! Along with it, the “Rule” Wu Youdao had established—“For one day, no information may leave Hanshui City”—burst asunder.

A rule that had persisted even through the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s tribulation was now annihilated by a single poke of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s finger!

The world fell silent.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy withdrew her hand and gazed at Wu Youdao, now grievously wounded from the backlash of the rule and coughing up blood.

In the same unperturbed tone, she said, “This is the true Cosmos in Palm.”

Chapter 445: Sweeping Through

The world fell into a deathly silence. Whether one was from Great Xia or Great Yu, all were awestruck by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s single finger.

Anyone could see that Wu Youdao had poured everything into unleashing his Cosmos in Palm—it was his trump card and ultimate killing blow. Yet this move had been effortlessly dismantled, and even the “Rule” confining Hanshui City had been extirpated.

Just how terrifying was her mastery over power, spells, and “Rules?!”

Lower-realm cultivators who borrowed higher-realm power were often limited by factors such as their thinking and judgment, unable to bring out the potential of the higher-realm power. Moreover, the national fortune was an immortal method. Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators struggled to grasp its usage. This was also why Provincial Governor Lü remained on the defensive during the battle earlier.

In contrast, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had exchanged blows with peers of the same cultivation realm when she was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, allowing her to familiarize herself with the power a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator should possess. After she became an immortal, her horizons broadened, and she could even provide combat guidance to those at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

No one in the world could maximize the power of the national fortune better than her.

~~~

“Are you alright?” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord stepped forward to offer Wu Youdao a precious half-immortal-grade pill for his injuries. Such pills not only placed high demands on the pill-concocter’s skills but also required rare ingredients that were difficult to obtain. One successful concoction didn’t guarantee another.

But with a formidable foe in front of us, I can’t afford to care so much now. Wu Youdao is pivotal to Great Yu’s resurgence. The Imperial Preceptor’s plans require his coronation after Great Yu’s resurgence. He can’t fall here.

The half-immortal-grade pill was highly effective. After ingesting one, the backlash from the “Rule” abated, and his pierced palm began healing. However, its recovery was slower than expected due to the lingering effect of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s move.

“Attack together!” Wu Youdao had no choice but to admit that his opponent was not someone he could defeat alone. “Stop holding back! This commotion will draw more powerful cultivators from Great Xia. We must end this battle before they rush over!”

With the national fortune right before his eyes, Wu Youdao was bent on snatching it. If we return empty-handed, the losses this time would be unthinkable.

Logically speaking, Transcendent Tribulation-level battles hinged on one’s mastery of “Rules,” but the three had long realized their opponent was likely a true immortal. If one played with “Rules” before an immortal, they wouldn’t even know how they had died!

We might as well use spells to fight!

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord and Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord skipped the probing segment, deploying their trump cards right from the outset.

“Brilliant heavenly lightning, heed my command!” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord’s title contained the character for “lightning” precisely because he specialized in lightning spells.

In an instant, the sky seemed to be collapsing. Silver serpents danced wildly, resembling jiao dragons soaring through the sky. The deafening noises shook Hanshui City. Without the protective arrays, everyone’s eardrums would have burst.

Right after the “Rules” were shattered, the people outside the city didn’t have time to register what had happened when they saw a blackened sky over Hanshui City with lightning striking down like rain. Fear seized them, their legs quivering and their knees buckling.

The might of the thunder strikes was no less inferior to the earlier lightning tribulation, or even surpassed it! After all, the lightning tribulation offered a one-in-a-ten chance of survival, while the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord’s move left no room for mercy—it was a ten-out-of-ten chance of death![1]

The lightning wove into a layered bird cage, trapping the Everlasting Immortal Fairy within. One could imagine the overwhelming lightning assaults the person inside would suffer when the cramped cage compressed the space within to its extreme.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unfazed, speaking just loud enough for the three Great Yu cultivators to hear. “The tribulation punishments in the world stem from the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit, with most punishments being lightning tribulations. Yet even the Heaven Mandate Immortal dared not attack this immortal with lightning spells. How could your abysmal imitation possibly succeed?”

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord’s pupils constricted, and his face contorted in astonishment. Her few words revealed so many ancient secrets!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s mouth curved into a smug smile. Unfortunately, as she was shrouded in national fortune, no one could see her appearance, much less her smile.

She extended her fair forefinger and pointed to the sky. Parting her lips, she uttered a few words, and the frightening lightning cage instantly vanished without a trace. Clear skies returned as if nothing had happened.

As the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord was closest to her, only he heard her words and couldn’t stop trembling.

She said, “By decree, disperse.”

A decree is a command from a high-ranking figure to a subordinate. Yet, just these few simple words alone dispersed my proud imitation of lightning tribulation. That can only mean one thing...

Her status is even higher than lightning tribulation—the lightning tribulation dares not strike her!

How is that possible?!

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord had never heard of such a thing, but only this explanation remained.

Terror took root in his heart. She is my natural nemesis!

“Self-Sacrificial Fist!” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord strode forward, his steps sending ripples through the air as he executed his fist technique.

This was his strongest move that earned him his honorable title.

His fist technique radiated unmatched dominance, with blinding golden light and divine rays and a dusky fog appearing behind him. This was the corpse energy he had accumulated, all of them fueling his Self-Sacrificial Fist.

“Immortal Fairy Fist Technique.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy swung her delicate fist. Despite looking soft like cotton, it encompassed the supreme principles of the Great Dao and boundless wonders.

The Immortal Fairy Fist Technique was the culmination of over ten thousand fist techniques, including the Arhat Fruit Fist, Forsythia Fist, Semiaquilegia Root[2] Fist. Among them, there was no lack of fist techniques that neutralized corpse energy, such as the heat-clearing and detoxifying Arhat Fruit Fist and Forsythia Fist.

Before the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique, the corpse energy automatically dissipated. Deprived of its fuel, the Self-Sacrificial Fist became like rootless duckweed, its power nearly nonexistent.

The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord was dumbfounded. Ever since he mastered fist techniques, he had never encountered a situation like this. Without giving him time to react, the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique came crashing toward his face. A flurry of delicate fists rained down on his face, leaving him bruised and battered.

“Supreme Threefold Force!”

“Azure Lightning Body Refinement!”

“Earth-Sacrificial Fist!”

The three Great Yu cultivators launched their assault simultaneously, their spells and techniques astonishing the heavens, and their massive momentum resembling a cataclysm.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy transformed into a martial immortal and faced them three alone, capturing dragons and tigers and ignoring lightning spells. Her fist technique was unbeatable as she swept through everything. With combat prowess that defied the heavens, she beat the trio until they were forced to backpedal repeatedly, leaving them utterly routed.

Even for the most exceptional talents, the highest praise people could offer was merely “possesses the potential to become an immortal.”

But the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was a bona fide immortal. Such highest praise was actually demeaning to her.

She fought with effortless ease, capable of nullifying any attack. The so-called untransmitted spells displayed by Wu Youdao and the other two were nothing new to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. She had already seen them in the ancient era and countered them with practiced familiarity.

The techniques her enemies knew, she knew better. The techniques her enemies didn’t know, she knew too.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. If these three had lived in ancient times, they wouldn’t even have qualified to contend to become immortals. They’re too weak.

Boom! The three were blasted away by a single punch from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, catapulting halfway across Hanshui City before embedding themselves into the Corpse-Driving Sect’s Yin-Corpse Mountain Range.

“All of you are not up to par. You’re far inferior to the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others.”

1. There is a wordplay on the idiom “nine deaths one life,” where it is modified to “ten deaths no life” in the second half of the sentence. ☜

2. The Chinese name is actually just three syllables—Tian Kui Zi. ☜

Chapter 446: Fight to the Death!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy faced three opponents alone without showing the slightest sign of fatigue, instead growing increasingly valiant the more she fought. This sight instilled fear in people’s hearts.

Before such overwhelming cultivation, mountain ranges became softer than tofu. Wu Youdao and the other two crashed through countless mountains without slowing their momentum.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy appeared behind them with even greater speed, delivering several fists that sent them hurtling through the air once more.

The three bounced around like rubber balls; even stabilizing themselves was an extravagant hope.

“Space Defense!” Wu Youdao was the first to steady his footing. Faced with the fast and furious Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he erected multiple space defenses—protective magical treasures passed down through generations of Yu emperors.

These spaces were irregular in size and nearly impassable, each containing deadly traps and danger where survival was only a one in ten chance. Even if one could escape, they would still lose half of their life.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scanned the spaces before her, then gracefully traversed through the layers of space with lotus-like steps, delivering a kick square to Wu Youdao’s face. The impact snapped his neck directly.

“How is this possible?!” Wu Youdao gasped in shock. Even if she’s an expert in spatial spells, she absolutely couldn’t have passed through these spaces. The irregular sizes are to prevent people from using spatial spells to cross through.

“She simultaneously used Shrinking Earth To Inches and Close Horizon From Cliff!” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord’s sharp eyes recognized the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s moves. But I’ve never heard of anyone casting these two top-tier spatial spells at the same time!

The battered Wu Youdao’s trio weren’t the only ones whose scalps tingled. Even spectators like Qiu Jin’an and the white paper-hatted man felt chills seeping into their hearts. Fighting three opponents of the same cultivation realm at once with such ease and control—she’s definitely an immortal!

“As expected of Dou Heavenly Sovereign, the one who casually played with the stars like they were beans,” the white paper-hatted man murmured in awe. Even if it’s just the tip of the iceberg, judging by the power she has displayed, this description wasn’t an exaggeration.

Qiu Jin’an looked at the white paper-hatted man strangely. “Dou (Bean) Heavenly Sovereign who who casually played with the stars like they were beans? Not Dou (Battle) Heavenly Sovereign as in the ‘dou’ for ‘battle?’”

“It’s the ‘dou’ for ‘bean,’” the white paper-hatted man corrected Qiu Jin’an, though he didn’t reveal any further information.

~~~

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stretched comfortably. After staying in the mental space all this while, I finally get to move about and stretch my limbs.

“Enough playing around. Time to end this.”

She dished out three consecutive unavoidable fists, each encompassing comprehension of spatial spells. The trio suffered the three punches and could no longer hold on, falling from the sky like torn sacks.

Wu Youdao spat dark blood, his eyes bloodshot. Born with Dragon-Tiger Qi, his life had gone smoothly with exceptional cultivation talent. Everyone praised that he had inherited the aura of his ancestors and was destined for greatness. And indeed, it was the case. Cultivation came as naturally to him as drinking water, and he never encountered bottlenecks. Only when he was advancing to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage did he face some difficulties, but that was all.

He successfully ascended as the sixth Yu emperor, and none of his younger siblings were worthy to contend with him for the throne. After becoming emperor, he found that cultivation at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage was fraught with challenges and no longer as effortless as before. However, his ambitions extended far beyond just the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

He wanted to become an immortal.

To this end, he participated in the Imperial Preceptor’s plans, slumbering for 180,000 years before awakening to seize fortuitous opportunities for immortal ascension. He set his sights on the national fortune’s power, which could catalyze a complete transformation of his Dragon-Tiger Qi. It would be a tremendous boon to him in the upcoming Great Era’s battles for immortal ascension opportunities.

Since the Imperial Preceptor wanted to analyze the national fortune, and Wu Youdao wanted to obtain its power, the Hanshui City plan was thus born.

“I am the Yu Emperor. Emperors never speak of retreat!” Wu Youdao spat a mouthful of black blood before swallowing another half-immortal-grade great pill. His aura surged like a rainbow, with the Dragon and Tiger Qi flanking him like civil and martial ministers.

~~~

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord lay embedded in a mountain crevice. His already-aged features aged further, and he gasped raggedly. He had exhausted his hidden cards to fend off the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s fists but to no avail.

Against that strike, all he could do was preserve his life.

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord closed his eyes, reflecting on his life.

He was born to a middling ancestral clan, where the old ancestor was merely at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. At that time, the first imperial preceptor still assisted in governing the nation. Due to his background, he was subjected to neglect and bullying in his clan.

One day, while gathering herbs in the mountains, he accidentally stumbled across a secret domain and obtained a legacy of lightning spells. However, his circumstances only improved marginally. He possessed the legacy but lacked resources.

To get his hands on resources, he fought with all his might, enhanced himself through countless bloody battles, joined multiple factions, defeated numerous indomitable opponents, and finally attained success and fame, crushing the clan that once looked down on him beneath his feet.

His desperate fighting style in his younger days and the incomplete lightning spells legacy left him with a much shorter lifespan than other Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. To prolong his lifespan, he chose to slumber. While others contended for fortuitous opportunities to become an immortal, he forsook his own opportunities to seize lifespan-extending spirit items instead.

He didn’t care who the emperor was or who could become an immortal. He had participated in Hanshui City’s plans this time simply because the Imperial Preceptor had promised to help him acquire lifespan-extending spirit items.

Never had I imagined I’d encounter such a formidable foe who could threaten my life.

Should I concede defeat?

As the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord’s consciousness faded, his life flashed before him. Defeating my older cousin brother for Foundation Establishment spirit items, joining assassin guilds to comprehend my golden core, defeating three peers in succession to shatter my golden core and form my nascent soul, and slaughtering until my life force nearly extinguished...

No!

His eyes snapped open. I’ve been battling nonstop in my life. Every fortuitous opportunity was seized through struggles and bloodshed!

So what if she’s born to counter me? Does that necessarily mean I can’t defeat her?

“Kill her!”

~~~

The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord sighed at the familiar yet alien Yin-Corpse Mountain Rage. He was a descendant of the legendary seclusive Witchcraft Tribe. After he stole the Witchcraft Tribe’s forbidden Corpse-Driving Techniques, they crippled his cultivation, erased his memories of the techniques, and evicted him from the tribe.

Fortunately, he didn’t lose all his memories, and fragments of Corpse-Driving Techniques flashed through his mind occasionally. Relying on these fragments, he ventured into various tombs and harnessed the environment to cultivate, rebuilding his cultivation and finally recalling the complete Corpse-Driving Techniques.

To elevate his cultivation realm, he stirred up a notable corpse outbreak in Great Yu. The imperial court captured him but spared his life, recognizing his talent and planning to nurture him instead. With the imperial court grooming him, his cultivation gradually outclassed the other budding talents in his cohort, reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

The first thing he did after breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage was to storm the Witchcraft Tribe and slaughter every last member to obtain a plethora of legacies.

Since the imperial court has given me the cultivation to exact vengeance, I must repay them with lives! This is called gratitude!

“Your Majesty, you mustn’t die here. Let’s go all out!”

Infernal flames blazed in their eyes as they prepared to fight to the death.

“Dragon-Tiger Qi, fight with this sovereign!” Wu Youdao stepped on the Dragon Qi, while the Tiger Qi morphed into protective tattoos across his back. The roars of a tiger reverberated through the air as his left and right eyes transformed into the eye of a dragon and tiger respectively. His entire being radiated with an untamed bestial nature.

“Azure lightning rushes in, forged through countless trials!” A colossal azure lightning struck the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, branding his forehead with a lightning sigil. His hair stood on end and danced with electricity as his body became much younger, returning to his appearance in his prime.

He was burning his lifespan in exchange for the body in his prime!

“The Azure Lightning old ghost is already burning his lifespan. I shan’t be left behind. Witchcraft Tribe’s Secret Art—Heaven-Sacrificial Fist!” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord went mad and abandoned all optimism, no longer holding back. Letting out a roar, he sacrificed himself to the heavens. Majestic power descended from the sky and gushed into his body until every cell glistened with overflowing energy.

“Attack together!” The trio launched their assault simultaneously and went all in, unleashing their final trump cards and strongest moves to eliminate the Everlasting Immortal Fairy right on the spot.

“Be careful!” Qiu Jin’an warned as cold sweat beaded on his forehead. Even if he was spectating the battle from a distance, the trio’s do-or-die methods that threw all caution to the wind felt extremely menacing.

The white paper-hatted man gulped, worried whether the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could survive the deadly onslaught.

Bang, bang, bang! The Everlasting Immortal Fairy performed the Immortal Fairy Fist Technique, delivering a fist to each of the three, punching most of the life out of them.

The trio collapsed to the ground, spasming uncontrollably.

“Is this a joke? You almost gave this immortal a fright. I even thought you had some impressive moves.”

Chapter 447: The End of the Great Battle

Wu Youdao and his two companions finally understood. The figure before them was an opponent they could never dream of defeating. Forget victory—the moment the battle began, they hadn’t even been able to land a single scratch on her.

The Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign of the Heavenly Court Creed is utterly terrifying.

“Run!”

The three had accepted reality. Since victory was impossible, their only option was to flee and live to fight another day!

The physical body moved far slower than the soul. As seasoned combatants, the three immediately made the wisest choice—their souls left their bodies and fled in separate directions.

“Fortunately, she’s only a wisp of an immortal’s thought, so she can’t chase all three of us at once. Moreover, the national fortune can’t be easily moved. If she wants to pursue us, she must abandon it, but if she does that, her strength will wane. Even if she catches up, she won't be able to defeat us!”

With this reassurance, the trio transformed into streaks of escaping light.

~~~

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched impassively as the three fled, then withdrew her gaze.

By the time Provincial Governor Lü saw that the battle had concluded and rushed to the scene, only three lifeless bodies and the masterless national fortune remained.

He acted swiftly and used the Wilderness Province’s official seal to reclaim the national fortune’s power.

Qiu Jin’an turned and cupped his fists. “Many thanks for your assistance earlier, Fellow Daoist. May I ask your origins?”
