There was no one next to Qiu Jin’an; the white paper-hatted man had long since bolted.

“Impressive escape techniques,” Qiu Jin’an mumbled, narrowing his eyes. “Did he leave...or flee?” The white paper-hatted man’s combat moves had aroused some suspicions in him. That said, he did lend a hand, so it wouldn’t be suitable to fall out with him right afterward.

Elder Gai and the others rushed back to the Corpse-Driving Sect. At the sight of their sect leader’s corpse, they bawled their eyes out, tears raining down their cheeks.

“Sect Leader, you died so tragically!”

“We will definitely avenge you!”

The disciples wept until their eyes turned red, and the entire Corpse-Driving Sect was suffused with their grief.

Lu Yang and the others also arrived to see the three Transcendent Tribulation corpses laid out on the ground and the sect disciples wailing like a mess, their fists clenched and veins bulging.

As the First Elder of the sect, Elder Gai had to assume the role of sect leader now that Sect Leader Lu was no longer around. He turned to console the mourning crowd. “Old Lu was a cheerful and optimistic person. If his spirit is watching over us now, he wouldn’t wish to see all of you like this. Smile for him—let’s send him off one last time.

“Rest assured, Old Lu. We will inherit your legacy and strengthen the Corpse-Driving Sect!” Elder Gai chuckled softly as he grieved over Lu Baqian’s death.

“Old Gai, you bastard! I’m dead, and you’re telling them to smile?!”

Sect Leader Lu’s upper body abruptly sat upright, glaring at Elder Gai.

This sudden development caught everyone off guard. Provincial Governor Lü was wary, thinking Sect Leader Lu‘s corpse had suddenly been reanimated, preparing to deploy the power of the national fortune again.

“Dead my ass!” Elder Gai barked a laugh. “Did you really think I wouldn’t know you’re still alive?!”

“What on earth is going on?” Provincial Governor Lü couldn’t make head or tail of the situation. Judging by Elder Gai’s reaction, he doesn’t seem surprised by Sect Leader Lu’s resurrection.

Sect Leader Lu explained, “You are the newly appointed provincial governor, I presume? This should be considered our first proper meeting. I am Lu Baqian, Sect Leader of the Corpse-Driving Sect.”

Provincial Governor Lü returned the courtesy, though he was still perplexed by the whole situation.

“You may not be aware, Provincial Governor Lü, but our Corpse-Driving Sect has maintained cordial relations with the Dao-Seeking Sect generations—the Taciturn Daoist Priest notwithstanding.

“We observe a tradition in the Corpse-Driving Sect. To express goodwill, the sect’s higher-ups will craft two soul lanterns. One remains in our sect, while its counterpart resides in the Dao-Seeking Sect, precisely to guard against a situation like today’s.”

Qiu Jin’an gave an imperceptible nod. He had heard of this matter before, so he never suspected the Corpse-Driving Sect’s higher-ups had been compromised. Sects with friendly ties practiced such customs, including the Five-Elements Sect, which also housed soul lamps of higher-ups from other sects.

Lu Baqian continued, “We just never expected these archaic cultivators to possess special methods beyond our grasp. They could take over my body without destroying my soul.

“After Witchcraft Sacrifice took over my body, he was worried about the Dao-Seeking Sect’s detection, so he didn’t dare to extinguish my soul, simply separating my soul and body and sealing my soul. That’s how I managed to survive.

“Furthermore, since he couldn’t obtain my memories, frequent interaction with Elder Gai and the others might cause him to slip up. Thus, after he took over my body, he announced to the outer world that he was in seclusion, only showing himself once to craft the Soul-Dispelling Talismans.” Sect Leader Lu shuddered with lingering fear. If not for the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s fear of the Dao-Seeking Sect, I might truly have died.

Provincial Governor Lü thought of another question. “So, you are at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage now?”

“Not entirely, but I guess you could call this a blessing in disguise. My body is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, but since Witchcraft Sacrifice underwent the tribulation for me, my soul is still at its original realm. For now, I’m considered half a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. Only when my soul’s cultivation realm rises in the future will I be a true Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

“No matter the case, I’m the first among my peers to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, right?” Sect Leader Lu saw Qiu Jin’an and registered that his cultivation realm was now the highest among his peers.

“Do you have no shame?” Qiu Jin’an looked at Sect Leader Lu with disdain. No wonder he can be on friendly terms with the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Never mind whether I have shame. Just answer me this—did I not go through life and death, survive against all odds, and become a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?” Sect Leader Lu declared with righteous certainty, utterly unabashed.

Qiu Jin’an was at a loss for words. What Lu Baqian isn’t exactly wrong...

Lu Yang had only begun to enjoy the bickering between a Fusion and a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy returned to his mental space.

“Whew! How was it? You saw how cool and amazing I was just now, right?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gave a thumbs-up, the corners of her mouth lifting upward into a brilliant smile.

“Yes, you were so cool! Very reliable... But I do want to ask, what’s up with these three people behind you?” Lu Yang’s gaze drifted to the three familiar-looking souls standing behind her: Wu Youdao, the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, and the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord.

The three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators looked cadaverous. Never had they imagined that it wasn’t a wisp of an immortal’s thought that wielded the national fortune but a complete immortal’s soul. Before the soul of an immortal, there was no way they could escape.

Wasn’t it supposed to be just a wisp of an immortal’s thought?

“These three are spoils of war! As the Dao-Seeking Sect’s guest elder, isn’t it only natural for me to capture a few people in exchange for contribution points?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy counted on her fingers, gleefully calculating with her mental abacus.

Last time, the archaic Fusion cultivator I caught earned me three days of the Sect Leader Experience Pass. This time, I’ve caught three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators—how much good stuff would that be worth?

Lu Yang’s face darkened, unpleasant memories flooding back.

The three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were appalled by their conversation.

Such a strong immortal is only a guest elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect—how deep do the sect’s waters run?!

The Imperial Preceptor had underestimated the Dao-Seeking Sect’s combat power!

And why is this Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign acting completely different compared to during the battle just now?

Lu Yang was similarly baffled, asking the questions the three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators wanted to ask.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy disclosed an ancient secret once again. “The Heaven Mandate Immortal said that maintaining a cool image is an essential skill for immortals.”

Chapter 448: First Elder: What Have I Not Seen in the World?

Lu Yang’s mental space had become a lively place with a staggering five individuals, all of them peerless powerhouses. Among them were an ancient immortal, three great Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and a Golden Core expert.

Lu Yang wondered if his mental space was getting a bit too crowded. Besides, even though it’s supposed to be my mental space, thanks to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s pinkish decorations, it hardly looks like the mental space of a grown man.

At the moment, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy acted as the owner of the mental space as she lectured the three prisoners. “Listen up, you three! Stay put and behave yourselves! This is my territory, and this boy, Lu Yang, is the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage and under my protection. You will treat him with the same respect as you would me, got it?!” With one hand on her hip and the other jabbing a finger, she looked just like a spoiled young lady from some noble family.

As Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, Wu Youdao and his companions once reveled in endless luxury, their food, clothing, dwellings, and possessions all of the finest quality. Wu Youdao, in particular, had been the sixth Yu emperor and the second strongest among all Yu emperors, standing at the pinnacle of power and wealth during his reign as emperor. Never before had they found themselves kneeling in such a cramped mental space and subjected to a tirade like this.

The three exchanged glances, bitterness glistening in the bottom of their eyes. Even Wu Youdao had lost his usual arrogance.

Our skills fall short—there’s no helping it.

They were merely Transcendent Tribulation cultivators who had slumbered for 180,000 years and chose to awaken now in pursuit of becoming immortals. On the other hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had long since ascended to an immortal. The gulf between them was immeasurable.

And who exactly is this Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign?

No matter how the three racked their brains, they couldn’t reconcile the image of the Four Ancient Immortals with the young woman before them.

Reassured, Lu Yang withdrew from his mental space. With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy around, the three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators won’t be able to stir up any waves. She could suppress all three of them single-handedly at the same cultivation realm, let alone now when she’s a major realm higher.

In the outer world, everyone was overjoyed about Sect Leader Lu’s survival. Qiu Jin’an and Provincial Governor Lü were still lamenting their failure to capture Wu Youdao and his companions, unaware that the trio was currently confined in Lu Yang’s mind.

“It’s a pity with Wu Youdao and the other two. Capturing them would have been a monumental contribution.”

“Be content. The fact that the national fortune and Hanshui City are safe is already an incredible stroke of luck.”

Lu Yang had pondered why the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t apprehended the three on the spot and handed them over to Qiu Jin’an, instead going through the trouble of pretending to let them escape before capturing them and trapping them in his mental space.

There are likely three reasons.

One, Qiu Jin’an and the others might lack the ability to confine these three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

Two, doing so could have risked exposing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s identity.

Three, fertile water shouldn’t flow into others’ fields—why let outsiders take the spoils? Rather than the Provincial Governor Lü and Qiu Jin’an, she might as well hand them over to the Dao-Seeking Sect, where she can exchange them for contribution points.

Given the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s personality, she had probably only considered the third point.

Qiu Jin’an noticed Meng Jingzhou in the crowd and beckoned him over. “Back when I borrowed your body, I promised to teach you a five-elements spell in return. Come to the Five-Elements Sect to learn it when you have time.”

Originally, Qiu Jin’an had planned to borrow Meng Jingzhou’s body, deliver a punch to Grandpa Ba, take Meng Jingzhou away, and then fulfill his promise. Unfortunately, unforeseen events had unfolded too rapidly—karmic backlash, a sudden trip to the Wilderness Province, and the chaos and schemes orchestrated by the Great Yu cultivators. Only now had things finally settled.

With the great battle concluded, there was still much to handle, such as the lingering ghost calamities in the city, the possibility of other Great Yu cultivators hiding within the city, and comforting the civilians. Qiu Jin’an would need to stay here for the time being to assist Provincial Governor Lü in dealing with the aftermath.

During the battle earlier, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had displayed her overwhelming might, reducing the Yin-Corpse Mountain Range to ruins. Even the Corpse-Driving Sect’s headquarters had been obliterated, and the yin energy accumulated over tens of thousands of years had dissipated entirely.

However, with Lu Baqian—a half-baked Transcendent Tribulation cultivator—around, the Corpse-Driving Sect would regain its former prosperity quickly.

From a linguistic standpoint, a “Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator” and a “half-baked Transcendent Tribulation cultivator” essentially meant the same thing.

With Meng Jingzhou’s karmic backlash resolved and their goal in Wilderness Province achieved, Lu Yang and the other two bid farewell to Zhao Po and boarded their carriage to return to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Before they departed, an expert arrived in Hanshui City with a contingent of elite soldiers behind him, all Golden Core cultivators soaring through the skies. These were troops stationed at the border between Great Xia and the Golden Buddhist Kingdom. Their leader was an elderly general at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. After the “Rule” was shattered, he sensed the anomaly in Hanshui City and immediately mobilized his forces to rush over.

But he was still a step too late. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had already resolved the situation quietly.

“There were too many people earlier, so I didn’t dare to ask, but was it the Everlasting Immortal Fairy inside you who intervened just now?” Meng Jingzhou couldn’t contain his curiosity any longer and finally blurted out the question after holding it in for the whole journey.

Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, and the old horse had personally witnessed how Lu Yang resurrected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; there were no outsiders now.

“It was her.”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu inhaled sharply. They had seen firsthand how the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had thrashed Wu Youdao and his companions like unruly grandsons—all while using only the power of a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Truly unbeatable among her peers.

Meng Jingzhou hadn’t expected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s combat prowess to be so formidable and gazed at Lu Yang enviously. With the guidance from an immortal within him, it’s no wonder Lu Yang’s combat power is so terrifying. It must have been the result of an immortal’s tutelage.

“Not only did she deal with those three Great Yu cultivators, but she also captured their souls and stuffed them into my mind!” Lu Yang pointed at his head.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were about to inhale sharply again when the carriage suddenly lurched violently, sending the items inside tumbling. The carriage, which had been moving smoothly until now, began shaking wildly.

Meng Jingzhou stuck his head out and saw that the old horse was unlike its usual self. It had activated spatial spells, its legs blurring as it galloped at breakneck speed, as though it was desperate to reach the Dao-Seeking Sect immediately.

The old horse had no choice but to speed up. It was terrified! Not only are there three Golden Core brats on board, but there are also the souls of three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. How can I not rush back?

With the old horse’s frantic sprint, the trio returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect in record time. Only then did the old horse finally relax, feeling safe at last.

“You two go ahead. I’ll head to the Great Mission Hall first to report this matter to Senior Brother Dai.” Lu Yang said goodbye to Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu before making his way to the Great Mission Hall.

Upon arriving, he politely asked the senior female disciple on duty at the front desk. He recognized her—she had once lined up to beat him up.

“Senior Sister Tang, is Senior Brother Dai in? I made some gains during this trip and wanted to update him.”

“Senior Brother Dai isn’t here, but First Elder happens to be around. You can report your findings to him instead.”

Only then did Lu Yang remember that Dai Bufan was temporarily overseeing the Great Mission Hall in First Elder’s stead. The true person in charge was First Elder.

“Alright.”

“Before Senior Brother Dai left, he mentioned that if you need anything, you may enter directly.”

Lu Yang nodded and thanked her before striding confidently into the depths of the Great Mission Hall.

~~~

Having returned to the Great Mission Hall after a long absence, First Elder was busy organizing intelligence reports, assessing missions’ rank classifications and danger levels, and predicting future developments.

“Ai, Little Dai doesn’t know how to show consideration for an old man like me,” First Elder groaned, massaging his temples as he reclined in his chair.

“First Elder, are you here?” Lu Yang’s voice came through the door, accompanied by a knock.

“Ah, it’s Lu Yang. Come in.” First Elder straightened his posture, mindful of maintaining his dignified image.

He recalled Dai Bufan’s parting words. “Shifu, when you’re overseeing the Great Mission Hall, be careful of those two youngsters, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. If they have something to report to you, it’s bound to be major. Try not to be too shocked when that happens.”

First Elder had merely chuckled dismissively at the time. I know about Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s exploits. Didn’t they simply infiltrate the Everlasting Creed, take care of it, establish the Heavenly Court Creed, and deceive the Nine-Netherworlds Creed?

Little Dai is still too young and hasn’t seen much of the world to be shocked by a few events like these. As an almighty Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, the strongest beneath the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, what have I not seen in the world? No matter how major the news is, I can handle it.

“Lu Yang, I heard from Old Two and the others that you went to Wilderness Province. Now that you’re back, what brings you here?” First Elder leisurely took a sip of his tea, the picture of composure.

“Here’s the thing. I captured the souls of three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and they’re currently locked inside my head.”

"Pfft—"

Chapter 449: If His Big Senior Sister Is Already This Strong, Just How Formidable Must Lu Yang’s Shifu Be?

Lu Yang wiped the tea from his face and looked at First Elder innocently. “First Elder, what’s wrong?”

First Elder stared at Lu Yang as if he had seen a ghost, briefly wondering if age had dulled his hearing. I have lived over two thousand years, and as the Dao-Seeking Nine’s Big Bro and a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation powerhouse, this is the first time I’ve encountered something like this.

As far as I know, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou headed to Wilderness Province with at most that Dragon-Horse Great Demon King in tow. Forget about this lineup, even if their group had been ten times stronger, capturing the souls of three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators shouldn’t have been possible.

“Who did you capture?”

“Wu Youdao, the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, and the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord.” Lu Yang counted off his fingers.

First Elder almost choked on his tea. These three were legendary figures of the Great Yu Dynasty, especially Wu Youdao, whose born dragon-tiger imperial destiny had been praised by historians for generations.

“Thanks to the old horse’s speed, we returned before the news could spread. First Elder, you have no idea how perilous this trip to Wilderness Province was. We nearly lost our lives there. It was extremely dangerous.”

First Elder cast a sidelong glance at Lu Yang. By “extremely dangerous,” do you mean how these three were captured by you?

“Explain clearly, boy. How exactly did you catch these three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators?”

Lu Yang lowered his voice mysteriously. “First Elder, since there are no outsiders here and we’re all members of the Heavenly Court Creed, I’ll be frank. Our Heavenly Court Creed has a prominent figure—the ruler of the ancient Heavenly Court, the Supreme Grand Heavenly Sovereign, Dou Heavenly Sovereign!

“It was all because of Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s help that I managed to capture these three!”

First Elder paused, then smiled knowingly. So it was Yun Zhi who stepped in.

Although Junior Niece Yun’s official position in the Heavenly Court Creed is its creed leader, that doesn’t preclude her from holding multiple identities. For instance, she’s both the Big Senior Sister of the disciples and the acting sect leader.

“Alright, alright. Since this involves Junior Niece Yun Zhi, you should discuss this with her.” With that, First Elder unceremoniously threw Lu Yang out of the Great Mission Hall.

Lu Yang shook his head helplessly and said to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “See? I told you we’d have to look for Big Senior Sister. Yet you wanted to bypass her and come straight to the Great Mission Hall for contribution points? Impossible.”

“Fine.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was deflated.

Just like Qiu Jin’an had mentioned, Yun Zhi had already completed the prison release procedures for the Taciturn Daoist Priest and returned to the sect.

When Lu Yang returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi maintained her aloof and otherworldly demeanor as she sat atop the summit. Her eyes contained millions of stars and galaxies, exuding an air of enigma. Even when gazing from a distance, one could feel overwhelming pressure from her.

Wu Youdao and his companions felt their scalps prickle at the sight. While Lu Yang couldn’t grasp the meaning behind this scene, as Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, they understood all too well. And it was precisely that understanding that bred terror from the bottom of their hearts.

During the Great Yu era, the stars in the sky had been remnant afterimages from ancient times; real stars had all but vanished. Thus, when Wu Youdao and the others awoke from their slumber, they immediately noticed the anomaly in the starry sky.

The stars that were once afterimages had been silently filled in, with no records of how it happened.

What kind of tremendous power could have achieved such a feat?

And what cultivation realm must one be at to accomplish this?

They had long wondered who was responsible for the new resplendent stars in the sky.

Now, they knew.

Though they wished they didn’t.

“Big Senior Sister, I’m back.” Lu Yang became extremely well-behaved in Yun Zhi’s presence.

“What did he just call that immortal? Big Senior Sister?” the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord blurted out, utterly losing his composure.

The other two reacted similarly. This woman is actually Lu Yang’s Big Senior Sister?

Then just how formidable must Lu Yang’s shifu be?

The Dao-Seeking Sect is so terrifying.

“You’re back?” Yun Zhi rose, the stars in her frosty eyes flashing away as if they had never appeared, leaving only clear pupils quietly fixed on Lu Yang. “What’s the situation with these three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators inside you?” With just a cursory glance, she noticed the liveliness in Lu Yang’s mental space.

“Enough. Out you go.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy yanked all three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators out like they were chicks.

“Your cultivation foundations are mediocre. Immortal ascension is unlikely. Explain yourselves, what’s going on?” Yun Zhi had knocked on the doors of all current Transcendent Tribulation cultivators to seek their advice, but she recognized none of these three, so they were evidently archaic cultivators.

Lu Yang summarized the events succinctly. Omitting his romantic peach-blossom luck, he focused on how he headed to the Corpse-Driving Sect, discovered the ghost calamities in Hanshui City, ran into Huang Ming, a reforged Great Yu Fusion cultivator while he was vanquishing ghosts, and was saved by Qiu Jin’an after Meng Tian True Lord’s intervention.

“Meng Tian True Lord and Huang Ming escaped capture, but then Wu Youdao showed up, looking like his plans had been exposed and he was forced to execute his plan prematurely.”

Wu Youdao, “...”

So it wasn’t you lot who caught Meng Tian True Lord and Huang Ming!

The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord and the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord shot accusatory glares at Wu Youdao. Why did you have to rush in like that?

Their original plan had been to wait for the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord to successfully undergo the tribulation to reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, activate the great array, and seize the national fortune’s power. However, despite following the plan, they still ended up being thrashed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who borrowed the power of the national fortune.

Lu Yang also recounted the battle between Wu Youdao’s faction and Provincial Governor Lü’s party, emphasizing that Sect Leader Lu’s body was taken over and that the white paper-hatted man who had helped out was likely to be the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“Took over Sect Leader Lu’s body?” Yun Zhi’s eyes narrowed slightly as the space in their surroundings rippled.

The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s soul shuddered, as though he had been locked onto by some terrifying entity and rendered unable to escape.

When Yun Zhi went to the Corpse-Driving Sect for exchange, she had primarily consulted Sect Leader Lu on Corpse-Driving Techniques. “Sect Leader Lu’s soul lamp isn’t extinguished. It seems that it was due to this consideration that the body takeover wasn’t complete. Nevertheless, this is unforgivable.”

Yun Zhi stepped forward and coldly pressed down on the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s head. The latter’s agonized screams were blood-curdling, sounding as though his three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls had been forcefully torn apart, his consciousness rapidly dissipating.

“Why have you all disappeared? Why can’t I see any of you?” The Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord’s vision was consumed by darkness, staggering blindly as he reached out his hand to grope about.

“Witchcraft Sacrifice, you...” The Azure Lightning Venerable Lord hesitated. It’s not us who vanished, but you who have lost your external senses.

“Is someone speaking? Louder; I can’t hear you.” His hearing was gone.

His consciousness faded entirely, and his mouth moved soundlessly before he collapsed to the ground with a thud.

His soul had been scoured clean—from now on, the Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord existed no more.

“He can be used as an artifact spirit.” Yun Zhi tossed the hollowed shell aside, turning her gaze to the trembling Wu Youdao and Azure Lightning Venerable Lord.

A Transcendent Tribulation artifact spirit—even Transcendent Tribulation-grade magical treasures might not necessarily house such powerful artifact spirits. For a cultivator’s soul to be refined into an artifact spirit was a tragic fate second only to the disintegration of one’s soul.

“Should you two withhold information, you’ll join him as artifact spirits.”

Chapter 450: Great Yu’s Plans

Wu Youdao gritted his teeth, his mind in turmoil. As the sixth Yu emperor and the one destined to annihilate Great Xia and restore the glory of Great Yu, how can I possibly cave in to mere threats and spill my secrets?!

After all, I’m someone who has weathered storms and seen bloodshed. It’s just being refined into an artifact spirit. There’s nothing to fear!

Just as Wu Youdao was about to speak, Lu Yang mused aloud beside him. “It’s said that history is written by the victors. The Dao-Seeking Sect has always maintained cordial relations with the imperial court. We could discuss with the scribes about giving your legacy some...artistic embellishments.

“If you cooperate, we’ll have them write that after your capture, you’d rather die than submit, enduring endless torture without revealing a single secret—a man of steel and unbreakable resolve.

“Even the Xia Emperor would praise you as a wise ruler with the potential to become an immortal, though it was a pity you were born in the wrong era. If you had remained emperor in the Great Yu Dynasty, you could have pushed Great Yu to greater heights. Your talent is no less than that of your founding ancestor, the first Yu emperor himself.

“On the other hand, if you refuse to confess anything, we will make the scribes describe how you bawled and begged for mercy, admitting Great Xia’s legitimacy while disparaging how Great Yu is inferior to Great Xia. Or perhaps they could record that we Great Xia treat our captives with benevolence and how you feast on fine wine and meat in the Dao-Seeking Sect, living so luxuriously that you’ve forgotten your homeland...”

“I’ll spill everything.” Wu Youdao immediately capitulated, cold sweat drenching his back at Lu Yang’s words.

In any case, I’ve already failed and been captured, with no control over my own life or death, and immortal ascension is all the more impossible. The only thing I care about now is my reputation. By Lu Yang’s logic, a tarnished reputation will be worse than the disintegration of the soul, for I will be subjected to eternal ridicule and infamy.

Wu Youdao glared venomously at Lu Yang, who remained utterly unfazed and ignored him.

Yun Zhi cast Lu Yang a glance, surprised by his unconventional approach. She had been prepared to use her traditional method of interrogation through torture.

Reaching out her hand, the golden bells on her wrist chimed, and a luminous barrier rose, separating Wu Youdao and the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord for individual questioning.

“What was your plan in Wilderness Province?”

“The Imperial Preceptor told this sovereign—I mean, me—that Great Xia’s national fortune was the key to obstructing our resurgence. He needed to study its effects on Great Xia, so we devised a plan to seize the Wilderness Province’s national fortune. Once the mechanisms have been figured out, we would channel the national fortune to nourish my Dragon-Tiger Qi as fuel, thereby increasing my chances of immortal ascension.”

“How does Great Yu plan to resurge?”

“Only the first imperial preceptor knows the full resurgence plan. The second imperial preceptor and I only grasp a part of it. However, ever since my awakening, I’ve never met the legendary first imperial preceptor. It has been the second imperial preceptor collaborating with me all this while.”

The first imperial preceptor had already vanished before Wu Youdao’s birth. To Wu Youdao, the first imperial preceptor was also a figure who existed in the legends.

“Our strategy was to ally with the Demon Region, sea tribes, and diabolic creeds. When the Great Era arrives, we would coordinate from the inside and outside to overthrow Great Xia in one swift move, while I’d become the Yu emperor.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t help but feel that the first half of this plan sounded familiar.

Lu Yang pondered. Wu Youdao’s plan is extremely crude and only a general outline. Looks like the true masterminds are the two imperial preceptors.

This is also in line with historical records. In the early days of the Great Yu Dynasty, the emperor and imperial preceptors shared a symbiotic relationship. The imperial preceptor was talented in statecraft, offering strategies and counsel for the emperor, while the emperor was receptive to advice. Together, they fostered the prosperity of Great Yu.

It wasn’t possible for every Yu emperor to be talented in governance. For instance, Wu Youdao possessed talent in cultivation but not in the administration of a nation.

“You would become the Yu emperor? Then what about the first Yu emperor?”

The founding Yu Emperor was the strongest cultivator of the Great Yu Dynasty. According to historical records, he waged campaigns across the land, ultimately overthrew Great Qian, and unified the world, establishing the Great Yu Dynasty. His reign lasted for three thousand years until his hidden injuries sustained through years of warfare resurfaced, and he succumbed to illness.

Lu Yang had always been skeptical of this account. It’s not like I haven’t met strong cultivators before. As the strongest of the Great Yu Dynasty, how could the first Yu emperor have died just like that?

“Our founding ancestor really died. After my succession, I personally offered rites before his remains,” Wu Youdao stated with conviction. If the founding ancestor were still alive, I wouldn’t have agreed with the Imperial Preceptor’s plans. After all, with the founding Yu emperor present, it wouldn’t be my turn to become the new Yu emperor and obtain fortuitous opportunities for immortal ascension.

“How many of you have awakened so far, and at what cultivation level?”

“Thirty-two Fusion cultivators and seven Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.”

Lu Yang frowned. This far exceeds the Calamity Venerable Lord’s confession of only two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Looks like the Calamity Venerable Lord had been peripheral to Great Yu’s plans. For even a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator to be marginal—Great Yu’s hidden strength is quite terrifying.

“What are the exact cultivation realms of those seven Transcendent Tribulation cultivators?”

“Three are Basic, two are Intermediate, and two are Advanced. The latter four are still in slumber. As for whether there are more, I wouldn’t know.”

Lu Yang mentally tallied his encounters with Great Yu's Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Calamity Venerable Lord, Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, and Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord—precisely three Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

“Where are these four Intermediate and Advanced Transcendent Tribulation cultivators slumbering at?”

“The Imperial Preceptor knows. I don’t.”

“What cultivation realms are the two imperial preceptors at?”

“No one knows the cultivation realm of the first imperial preceptor. I’ve asked a few powerful cultivators who have met the first imperial preceptor before, but they gave conflicting accounts. Some said he stood only half a step from becoming an immortal, while others claimed that he had already attained the Dao and become an immortal. The second imperial preceptor is a half-immortal powerhouse.” Wu Youdao’s eyes shone with reverence when mentioning that the first imperial preceptor had potentially become an immortal.

Lu Yang was much calmer. These days, the topic of immortals simply made him think of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and her four unlucky peers.

Any sense of awe and admiration toward immortals had long since evaporated.

A “half-immortal” referred to a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator with an Incipient Dao Fruit. The only half-immortal cultivator Lu Yang knew was the third-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage—the Everlasting Immortal.

“Had the Wilderness Province plan succeeded, what would have been your next step?”

“The Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would step in, deploying 'Rules' to envelop a city in Ji Province to test whether the power of rules could convert the populace into Great Yu subjects.”

“Which city?”

“It’d be randomly selected.”

Yun Zhi repeated the questions to the Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, but his knowledge proved sparser than Wu Youdao's, though it was sufficient for cross-verification.

She felt that there was a need to share Wu Youdao’s intelligence, particularly regarding Ji Province, with the imperial court and four other Great Immortal Sects for coordinated preparations. Binding the refined Witchcraft Sacrifice Venerable Lord with chains, she handed the other end of the chains to Lu Yang. “I’ll send these two to Incarceration Peak before heading to the imperial city. You shall hand this soul over to Fifth Elder.”

As Yun Zhi departed, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy jolted awake from a dream. “Ah! I forgot to ask for contribution points!”
